=== Forms\Checkbox\BUIInputCheckbox.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms
@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<TValue, BUIInputCheckbox<TValue>, BUIInputCheckboxVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasDensity
@typeparam TValue

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {

    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? CheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? UncheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? IndeterminateIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; }

    private readonly string _inputId = $"bui-checkbox-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _preventKeyDefault;

    private bool IsChecked => GetCheckedState();
    private bool IsIndeterminate => GetIndeterminateState();

    public override BUIInputCheckboxVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputCheckboxVariant.Default;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputCheckboxVariant, Func<BUIInputCheckbox<TValue>, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputCheckboxVariant, Func<BUIInputCheckbox<TValue>, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputCheckboxVariant.Default] = c => c.RenderDefault(),
        };

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        Type valueType = typeof(TValue);
        Type? underlyingType = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(valueType) ?? valueType;

        if (underlyingType != typeof(bool))
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"BUIInputCheckbox only supports bool and bool? value types. Provided type: {valueType.Name}");

        base.OnInitialized();
    }

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out TValue result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;

        if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool))
        {
            if (bool.TryParse(value, out bool boolResult))
            {
                result = (TValue)(object)boolResult;
                return true;
            }
            result = default!;
            validationErrorMessage = $"Unable to parse '{value}' as boolean.";
            return false;
        }

        if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool?))
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            {
                result = (TValue)(object?)null!;
                return true;
            }
            if (bool.TryParse(value, out bool boolResult))
            {
                result = (TValue)(object?)(bool?)boolResult!;
                return true;
            }
            result = default!;
            validationErrorMessage = $"Unable to parse '{value}' as nullable boolean.";
            return false;
        }

        result = default!;
        validationErrorMessage = $"Unsupported type {typeof(TValue).Name}.";
        return false;
    }

    private bool GetCheckedState()
    {
        if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool))
            return CurrentValue is bool b && b;
        if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool?))
            return CurrentValue is bool nb && nb;
        return false;
    }

    private bool GetIndeterminateState() => typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool?) && CurrentValue is null;

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        base.BuildComponentDataAttributes(dataAttributes);
        dataAttributes["data-checked"] = IsChecked.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        if (IsIndeterminate)
            dataAttributes["data-indeterminate"] = "true";
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderDefault() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
            <div class="bui-checkbox"
                 role="checkbox"
                 aria-checked="@(IsIndeterminate ? "mixed" : IsChecked.ToString().ToLowerInvariant())"
                 aria-disabled="@IsDisabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                 aria-labelledby="@(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) ? null : $"{_inputId}-label")"
                 aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                 tabindex="@(IsDisabled ? -1 : 0)"
                 @onclick="HandleClick"
                 @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown"
                 @onkeydown:preventDefault="_preventKeyDefault">

                <_BUICheckMark Checked="@(IsIndeterminate ? null : IsChecked)"
                               Size="Size"
                               Disabled="IsDisabled"
                               CheckedIcon="@CheckedIcon"
                               UncheckedIcon="@UncheckedIcon"
                               IndeterminateIcon="@IndeterminateIcon" />

                @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label))
                {
                    <span id="@($"{_inputId}-label")" class="bui-checkbox__label">
                        @Label
                        @if (Required)
                        {
                            <span class="bui-field__required">*</span>
                        }
                    </span>
                }
            </div>

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="TValue"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

        </bui-component>
    };

    private async Task HandleClick(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (IsDisabled) return;

        if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool))
        {
            bool current = CurrentValue is bool b && b;
            CurrentValue = (TValue)(object)!current;
        }
        else if (typeof(TValue) == typeof(bool?))
        {
            bool? current = (bool?)(object?)CurrentValue;
            bool? next = current switch
            {
                false => null,
                null => true,
                true => false
            };
            CurrentValue = (TValue)(object?)next!;
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        _preventKeyDefault = e.Key == " ";
        if (e.Key == " " || e.Key == "Enter")
        {
            await HandleClick(new MouseEventArgs());
        }
    }
}

        outline-offset: var(--bui-highlight-outline-offset);

    }

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public class BUIInputCheckboxVariant : Variant
{
    public static readonly BUIInputCheckboxVariant Default = new("Default");

    public BUIInputCheckboxVariant(string name) : base(name)
    {
    }

    public static BUIInputCheckboxVariant Custom(string name) => new(name);
}



=== Forms\Color\JsInterop\ColorPickerJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public interface IColorPickerJsInterop
{
    ValueTask<double[]> GetRelativePositionAsync(ElementReference element, double clientX, double clientY);

    ValueTask SetHandlerPositionAsync(ElementReference handler, double x, double y);
}

public sealed class ColorPickerJsInterop : ModuleJsInteropBase, IColorPickerJsInterop
{
    public ColorPickerJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.ColorPicker)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask<double[]> GetRelativePositionAsync(ElementReference element, double clientX, double clientY)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        return await module.InvokeAsync<double[]>("getRelativePosition", element, clientX, clientY);
    }

    public async ValueTask SetHandlerPositionAsync(ElementReference handler, double x, double y)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("setHandlerPosition", handler, x, y);
    }
}



=== Forms\Color\BUIColorPicker.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IPickerFamilyComponent
@implements IAsyncDisposable

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    <BUIDraggable OnDrag="HandleSelectionDrag" OnDragEnd="HandleSelectionDrag">
        <div @ref="_selectionRef"
             tabindex="0"
             class="bui-colorpicker__selection"
             @onkeydown="HandleSelectionKeyDown"
             @onkeydown:preventDefault="_preventKeyDown"
             style="width:@(SelectionWidth)px; height:@(SelectionHeight)px; background-color:@GetHueColor();">
            <div class="bui-colorpicker__selection-gradient">
                <span @ref="_handlerRef" class="bui-colorpicker__handler"></span>
            </div>
        </div>
    </BUIDraggable>

    <div class="bui-picker__slider bui-colorpicker__slider--hue"
         style="--value:@((_hsvColor.Hue / 360.0 * 100).ToString("0.##", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture))%">
        <input type="range" min="0" max="360" step="1" value="@_hsvColor.Hue" @oninput="HandleHueChange" />
    </div>

    <div class="bui-picker__slider bui-colorpicker__slider--alpha"
         style="--value:@((_alpha / 255.0 * 100).ToString("0.##", System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture))%; --color:@GetOpaqueColor()">
        <input type="range" min="0" max="255" step="1" value="@_alpha" @oninput="HandleAlphaChange" />
    </div>

    <div class="bui-picker__row">
        @switch (OutputFormat)
        {
            case ColorPickerOutputFormat.Hex:
                <input type="text"
                       class="bui-picker__input"
                       style="flex:1"
                       value="@GetCurrentColor().ToString(ColorOutputFormats.HexA)"
                       @onchange="SetHex" />
                break;
            default:
                <_BUIInNumber Value="@GetCurrentColor().R"
                              Min="0"
                              Max="255"
                              AriaLabel="Red"
                              ValueChanged="v => SetRgbChannel(v, 0)" />
                <_BUIInNumber Value="@GetCurrentColor().G"
                              Min="0"
                              Max="255"
                              AriaLabel="Green"
                              ValueChanged="v => SetRgbChannel(v, 1)" />
                <_BUIInNumber Value="@GetCurrentColor().B"
                              Min="0"
                              Max="255"
                              AriaLabel="Blue"
                              ValueChanged="v => SetRgbChannel(v, 2)" />
                <_BUIInNumber Value="@((int)_alpha)"
                              Min="0"
                              Max="255"
                              AriaLabel="Alpha"
                              ValueChanged="SetAlphaChannel" />
                break;
        }
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.MaterialIconsRound.i_sync" OnClick="CycleFormat" />
    </div>

    <div class="bui-picker__preview">
        <div style="background-color:@GetCurrentColor().ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Rgba);"></div>
    </div>

    @if (ShowActions)
    {
        <div class="bui-picker__row" style="justify-content:flex-end; border-top:1px solid var(--palette-border);">
            <_BUIBtn OnClick="HandleRevert">@RevertText</_BUIBtn>
        </div>
    }
</bui-component>

@code {
    private ElementReference _selectionRef;
    private ElementReference _handlerRef;
    private HsvColor _hsvColor = new(0, 1, 1);
    private byte _alpha = 255;
    private bool _isInitialized;
    private bool _preventKeyDown = false;

    [Inject] private IColorPickerJsInterop JsInterop { get; set; } = default!;

    [Parameter] public CssColor? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<CssColor?> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public ColorPickerOutputFormat OutputFormat { get; set; } = ColorPickerOutputFormat.Hex;
    [Parameter] public EventCallback OnRevert { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowActions { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public string RevertText { get; set; } = "Revert";
    [Parameter] public int SelectionWidth { get; set; } = 200;
    [Parameter] public int SelectionHeight { get; set; } = 150;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();
        if (Value != null && !_isInitialized)
        {
            _hsvColor = HsvColor.FromCssColor(Value);
            _alpha = Value.A;
            _isInitialized = true;
        }
    }

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (firstRender && Value != null) await UpdateHandlerPosition();
    }

    private CssColor GetCurrentColor() => _hsvColor.ToCssColor(_alpha);
    private string GetHueColor() => new HsvColor(_hsvColor.Hue, 1, 1).ToCssColor().ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Rgb);
    private string GetOpaqueColor() => _hsvColor.ToCssColor(255).ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Rgb);

    private async Task HandleSelectionDrag(DragEventArgs e)
    {
        double[] pos = await JsInterop.GetRelativePositionAsync(_selectionRef, e.ClientX, e.ClientY);
        _hsvColor = _hsvColor.WithSaturation(pos[0] / SelectionWidth).WithValue(1 - pos[1] / SelectionHeight);
        await JsInterop.SetHandlerPositionAsync(_handlerRef, pos[0], pos[1]);
        await NotifyColorChanged();
    }

    private async Task HandleHueChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        if (int.TryParse(e.Value?.ToString(), out int hue))
        {
            _hsvColor = _hsvColor.WithHue(hue);
            await NotifyColorChanged();
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleAlphaChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        if (int.TryParse(e.Value?.ToString(), out int alpha))
        {
            _alpha = (byte)Math.Clamp(alpha, 0, 255);
            await NotifyColorChanged();
        }
    }

    private async Task SetRgbChannel(int? val, int component)
    {
        if (!val.HasValue) return;
        CssColor c = GetCurrentColor();
        int r = c.R, g = c.G, b = c.B;
        int clampedVal = Math.Clamp(val.Value, 0, 255);
        switch (component)
        {
            case 0: r = clampedVal; break;
            case 1: g = clampedVal; break;
            case 2: b = clampedVal; break;
        }
        _hsvColor = HsvColor.FromCssColor(new CssColor(r, g, b, _alpha));
        await UpdateHandlerPosition();
        await NotifyColorChanged();
    }

    private async Task SetAlphaChannel(int? val)
    {
        if (!val.HasValue) return;
        _alpha = (byte)Math.Clamp(val.Value, 0, 255);
        await NotifyColorChanged();
    }

    private async Task SetHex(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        try
        {
            CssColor c = new(e.Value?.ToString() ?? "");
            _hsvColor = HsvColor.FromCssColor(c);
            _alpha = c.A;
            await UpdateHandlerPosition();
            await NotifyColorChanged();
        }
        catch { }
    }

    private void CycleFormat() => OutputFormat = OutputFormat switch
    {
        ColorPickerOutputFormat.Hex => ColorPickerOutputFormat.Rgb,
        _ => ColorPickerOutputFormat.Hex
    };

    private async Task HandleRevert() => await OnRevert.InvokeAsync();

    private async Task HandleSelectionKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        _preventKeyDown = false;

        const double step = 0.02;
        const double fineStep = 0.005;

        double delta = e.ShiftKey ? fineStep : step;
        HsvColor newColor = _hsvColor;

        switch (e.Key)
        {
            case "ArrowRight":
                newColor = _hsvColor.WithSaturation(Math.Min(1, _hsvColor.Saturation + delta));
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                break;
            case "ArrowLeft":
                newColor = _hsvColor.WithSaturation(Math.Max(0, _hsvColor.Saturation - delta));
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                break;
            case "ArrowUp":
                newColor = _hsvColor.WithValue(Math.Min(1, _hsvColor.Value + delta));
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                break;
            case "ArrowDown":
                newColor = _hsvColor.WithValue(Math.Max(0, _hsvColor.Value - delta));
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                break;
            default:
                return;
        }

        if (newColor != _hsvColor)
        {
            _hsvColor = newColor;
            await UpdateHandlerPosition();
            await NotifyColorChanged();
        }
    }

    private async Task UpdateHandlerPosition()
    {
        double x = _hsvColor.Saturation * SelectionWidth;
        double y = (1 - _hsvColor.Value) * SelectionHeight;
        await JsInterop.SetHandlerPositionAsync(_handlerRef, x, y);
    }

    private async Task NotifyColorChanged() => await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(GetCurrentColor());

    public ValueTask DisposeAsync() => ValueTask.CompletedTask;
}

    position: absolute;

    border: 2px solid var(--palette-white);

=== Forms\Color\BUIInputColor.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Utils
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<CssColor, BUIInputColor, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private string _inputId = $"bui-input-color-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _isOpen;
    private bool _isFocused;
    private bool _isDirty;
    private CssColor? _initialValue;
    private CssColor? _valueBeforeOpen;

    [Inject] private IClipboardJsInterop ClipboardJs { get; set; } = default!;

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // Component-specific
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; } = "#000000";
    [Parameter] public bool InputEditable { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool ShowCopyButton { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Clearable { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public ColorPickerDisplayMode DisplayMode { get; set; } = ColorPickerDisplayMode.Dropdown;
    [Parameter] public ColorPickerOutputFormat OutputFormat { get; set; } = ColorPickerOutputFormat.Hex;
    [Parameter] public string RevertText { get; set; } = "Revert";
    [Parameter] public int SelectionWidth { get; set; } = 200;
    [Parameter] public int SelectionHeight { get; set; } = 150;

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    private bool HasValue => CurrentValue != null;
    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || _isDirty;
    private string DisplayValue => CurrentValue?.ToString(GetDisplayFormat()) ?? "";

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        base.OnInitialized();
        _initialValue = Value;
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();

        if (!_isFocused && !_isOpen && !EqualityComparer<CssColor>.Default.Equals(Value, CurrentValue))
        {
            _initialValue = Value;
        }
    }

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputColor, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputColor, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = c => c.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = c => c.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = c => c.RenderInput()
        };

    private RenderFragment RenderInput() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown">

            <div class="bui-input__wrapper">

                <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label" For="@_inputId" Required="@Required" />
                <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

                <input type="text"
                       id="@_inputId"
                       class="bui-input__field"
                       value="@DisplayValue"
                       placeholder="@(IsFloated? Placeholder : null)"
                       readonly="@(!InputEditable)"
                       disabled="@IsDisabled"
                       @onchange="HandleInputChange"
                       @onfocus="HandleFocus"
                       @onblur="HandleBlur"
                       aria-label="@(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) ? Placeholder : null)"
                       aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                       aria-invalid="@IsError.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       aria-required="@Required.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()" />

                @if (ShowCopyButton && HasValue)
                {
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Copy"
                             AriaLabel="Copy color"
                             OnClick="(e)=> CopyToClipboard()"
                             OnClickStopPropagation="true" />
                }

                @if (Clearable && (HasValue || _isDirty) && !Disabled)
                {
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                             AriaLabel="Clear"
                             OnClick="(e)=> Clear()"
                             OnClickStopPropagation="true" />
                }

                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.MaterialIconsRound.i_palette"
                         Disabled="@IsDisabled"
                         AriaLabel="Open color picker"
                         OnClick="(e)=> TogglePicker()">
                    <div class="bui-input-color__preview-chess">
                        <div class="bui-input-color__preview-color"
                             style="background-color: @(CurrentValue?.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Rgba) ?? "transparent")">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </_BUIBtn>

                <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />
                <BUIInputLoading Loading="@Loading" LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="@Size" />

            </div>

            @if (_isOpen)
            {
                @if (DisplayMode == ColorPickerDisplayMode.Modal)
                {
                    <BUIDialog @bind-Open="_isOpen"
                               Closable="true"
                               CloseOnOverlayClick="true"
                               CloseOnEscape="true"
                               MinWidth="auto"
                               MaxWidth="fit-content">
                        <Content>
                            <BUIColorPicker @bind-Value="CurrentValue"
                                            OutputFormat="OutputFormat"
                                            SelectionWidth="SelectionWidth"
                                            SelectionHeight="SelectionHeight"
                                            Size="Size"
                                            Density="Density"
                                            ShowActions="true"
                                            RevertText="@RevertText"
                                            OnRevert="HandleRevert" />
                        </Content>
                    </BUIDialog>
                }
                else
                {
                    <div class="bui-input-color__dropdown-overlay" @onclick="ClosePicker"></div>
                    <div class="bui-input-color__dropdown" @onclick:stopPropagation="true">
                        <BUIColorPicker @bind-Value="CurrentValue"
                                        OutputFormat="OutputFormat"
                                        SelectionWidth="SelectionWidth"
                                        SelectionHeight="SelectionHeight"
                                        Size="Size"
                                        Density="Density"
                                        ShowActions="true"
                                        RevertText="@RevertText"
                                        OnRevert="HandleRevert" />
                    </div>
                }
            }

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="CssColor"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

        </bui-component>
    };

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
        _isDirty = false;
    }

    private void HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (_isOpen && e.Key == "Escape")
        {
            ClosePicker();
        }
    }

    private void HandleInputChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        if (!InputEditable) return;

        string? value = e.Value?.ToString();

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            CurrentValue = null!;
            _isDirty = false;
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            CurrentValue = new CssColor(value);
            _isDirty = false;
        }
        catch
        {
            _isDirty = true;
        }
    }

    private void TogglePicker()
    {
        if (IsDisabled || IsReadOnly) return;

        if (!_isOpen)
        {
            _valueBeforeOpen = CurrentValue;
        }
        _isOpen = !_isOpen;
    }

    private void ClosePicker() => _isOpen = false;

    private void HandleRevert()
    {
        CurrentValue = _valueBeforeOpen!;
        ClosePicker();
    }

    private void Clear()
    {
        CurrentValue = _initialValue!;
        _isDirty = false;
    }

    private async Task CopyToClipboard()
    {
        if (CurrentValue != null)
        {
            await ClipboardJs.CopyTextAsync(DisplayValue);
        }
    }

    private ColorOutputFormats GetDisplayFormat() => OutputFormat switch
    {
        ColorPickerOutputFormat.Rgb => ColorOutputFormats.Rgba,
        _ => ColorOutputFormats.HexA
    };

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out CssColor result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            result = null!;
            return true;
        }

        try
        {
            result = new CssColor(value);
            return true;
        }
        catch
        {
            result = null!;
            validationErrorMessage = $"'{value}' is not a valid color.";
            return false;
        }
    }
}

=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUIDatePicker.razor ===

@using System.Globalization
@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IPickerFamilyComponent

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    <div class="bui-picker__row">
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronLeft"
                    AriaLabel="Previous year"
                    OnClick="PrevYearClicked" />
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronLeft"
                    AriaLabel="Previous month"
                    OnClick="PrevMonthClicked" />
        <span class="bui-picker__title">@CurrentMonth.ToString("MMMM yyyy", CultureInfo.CurrentCulture)</span>
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronRight"
                    AriaLabel="Next month"
                    OnClick="NextMonthClicked" />
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronRight"
                    AriaLabel="Next year"
                    OnClick="NextYearClicked" />
    </div>

    <div class="bui-picker__grid">
        @foreach (string day in WeekDays)
        {
            <span class="bui-picker__cell bui-picker__cell--muted">@day[..2]</span>
        }
        @foreach (DayCell day in Days)
        {
            <_BUIBtn Active="@day.IsSelected"
                        class="@($"bui-picker__cell {(!day.IsCurrentMonth ? "bui-picker__cell--muted" : "")}")"
                        OnClick="() => SelectDateClicked(day.Date)">
                @day.Date.Day
            </_BUIBtn>
        }
    </div>
</bui-component>

@code {
    [Parameter] public DateOnly? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<DateOnly?> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    private DateTime CurrentMonth = DateTime.Today;
    private DateOnly SelectedDate = DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today);

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();
        if (Value.HasValue)
        {
            SelectedDate = Value.Value;
            CurrentMonth = new DateTime(Value.Value.Year, Value.Value.Month, 1);
        }
    }

    private void PrevYearClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => CurrentMonth = CurrentMonth.AddYears(-1);
    private void NextYearClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => CurrentMonth = CurrentMonth.AddYears(1);
    private void PrevMonthClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => CurrentMonth = CurrentMonth.AddMonths(-1);
    private void NextMonthClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => CurrentMonth = CurrentMonth.AddMonths(1);

    private async Task SelectDateClicked(DateTime date)
    {
        SelectedDate = DateOnly.FromDateTime(date);
        CurrentMonth = new DateTime(date.Year, date.Month, 1);
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(SelectedDate);
    }

    private IEnumerable<string> WeekDays => CultureInfo.CurrentCulture.DateTimeFormat.AbbreviatedDayNames;

    private IEnumerable<DayCell> Days
    {
        get
        {
            DateTime firstOfMonth = new(CurrentMonth.Year, CurrentMonth.Month, 1);
            DateTime start = firstOfMonth.AddDays(-(int)firstOfMonth.DayOfWeek);
            return Enumerable.Range(0, 42).Select(i =>
            {
                DateTime d = start.AddDays(i);
                return new DayCell
                {
                    Date = d,
                    IsCurrentMonth = d.Month == CurrentMonth.Month,
                    IsSelected = SelectedDate.DayNumber == DateOnly.FromDateTime(d).DayNumber
                };
            });
        }
    }

    private sealed class DayCell
    {
        public DateTime Date { get; set; }
        public bool IsCurrentMonth { get; set; }
        public bool IsSelected { get; set; }
    }

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        base.BuildComponentDataAttributes(dataAttributes);
        dataAttributes["data-bui-picker-base"] = "true";
    }
}



=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUIDatePicker.razor.css ===




=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUIInputDateTime.razor ===

@using System.Globalization
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Utils

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@typeparam TValue
@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<TValue, BUIInputDateTime<TValue>, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private string _inputId = $"bui-datetime-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _isPickerOpen;
    private bool ShowDate;
    private bool ShowTime;
    private TValue? _initialValue;
    private BUIDateTimePattern? _patternRef;
    private bool _isFocused;
    private bool _isDirty;
    private string? _patternKey = Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N");

    private DateOnly _tempDateValue;
    private TimeOnly _tempTimeValue;

    private DateOnly DateValue { get; set; } = DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today);
    private TimeOnly TimeValue { get; set; } = TimeOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Now);

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // Component-specific
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }

    private Type UnderlyingType => Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(typeof(TValue)) ?? typeof(TValue);
    private string Format => GetCultureFormatString();
    private bool HasValue => CurrentValue != null;
    private bool CanClear => _isDirty;
    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || _isDirty;

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputDateTime<TValue>, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputDateTime<TValue>, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = i => i.RenderInput()
        };

    private RenderFragment RenderInput() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

            <div class="bui-input__wrapper">

                <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label" For="@_inputId" Required="@Required" />
                <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

                <BUIDateTimePattern @key="@_patternKey"
                                    @ref="_patternRef"
                                    Id="@_inputId"
                                    ContainerClass="bui-input__field"
                                    ShowPattern="@IsFloated"
                                    @bind-Text="@CurrentValueAsString"
                                    Format="@Format"
                                    Editable="@(!ReadOnly)"
                                    Disabled="@IsDisabled"
                                    OnFocus="HandleFocus"
                                    OnBlur="HandleBlur"
                                    OnDirtyStateChanged="HandleDirtyChanged" />

                @if (CanClear && !ReadOnly)
                {
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                             AriaLabel="Clear"
                             OnClick="(e)=> Clear()"
                             OnClickPreventDefault="true"
                             OnClickStopPropagation="true" />
                }

                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_calendar_today"
                         Disabled="@IsDisabled"
                         Loading="@Loading"
                         LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant"
                         AriaLabel="Open picker"
                         OnClick="(e)=> OpenPicker()"
                         OnClickPreventDefault="true"
                         OnClickStopPropagation="true" />

                <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />

            </div>

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="TValue"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

            <BUIDialog @bind-Open="_isPickerOpen"
                       Title="@GetPickerTitle()"
                       Closable="true"
                       CloseOnOverlayClick="true"
                       CloseOnEscape="true"
                       MinWidth="auto"
                       MaxWidth="fit-content">
                <Content>
                    <div class="bui-input-datetime__picker-content">
                        @if (ShowDate)
                        {
                            <BUIDatePicker Value="DateValue"
                                           ValueChanged="OnDateChanged"
                                           Size="Size"
                                           Density="Density" />
                        }
                        @if (ShowTime)
                        {
                            <BUITimePicker Value="TimeValue"
                                           ValueChanged="OnTimeChanged"
                                           Size="Size"
                                           Density="Density" />
                        }
                    </div>
                </Content>
                <Footer>
                    <BUIButton Text="Cancel"
                               OnClick="() => _isPickerOpen = false"
                               Variant="BUIButtonVariant.Default" />
                    <BUIButton Text="Apply"
                               OnClick="ApplyPickerValue" />
                </Footer>
            </BUIDialog>
        </bui-component>
    };

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        base.OnInitialized();

        _initialValue = Value;

        Type type = UnderlyingType;

        ShowDate = type == typeof(DateOnly)
                || type == typeof(DateTime)
                || type == typeof(DateTimeOffset);

        ShowTime = type == typeof(TimeOnly)
                || type == typeof(DateTime)
                || type == typeof(DateTimeOffset);
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();

        if (!HasValue) return;

        SyncPickersFromValue();
    }

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void HandleDirtyChanged(bool isDirty)
    {
        _isDirty = isDirty;
    }

    private void SyncPickersFromValue()
    {
        if (CurrentValue == null) return;

        Type type = UnderlyingType;

        if (type == typeof(DateOnly))
        {
            DateValue = (DateOnly)(object)CurrentValue;
        }
        else if (type == typeof(TimeOnly))
        {
            TimeValue = (TimeOnly)(object)CurrentValue;
        }
        else if (type == typeof(DateTime))
        {
            DateTime dt = (DateTime)(object)CurrentValue;
            DateValue = DateOnly.FromDateTime(dt);
            TimeValue = TimeOnly.FromDateTime(dt);
        }
        else if (type == typeof(DateTimeOffset))
        {
            DateTimeOffset dto = (DateTimeOffset)(object)CurrentValue;
            DateValue = DateOnly.FromDateTime(dto.DateTime);
            TimeValue = TimeOnly.FromDateTime(dto.DateTime);
        }
    }

    private string GetPickerIcon() => UnderlyingType switch
    {
        Type t when t == typeof(TimeOnly) => BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_schedule,
        _ => BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_calendar_today
    };

    private void OpenPicker()
    {
        if (!HasValue)
        {
            DateValue = DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today);
            TimeValue = TimeOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Now);
        }

        _tempDateValue = DateValue;
        _tempTimeValue = TimeValue;

        _isPickerOpen = true;
    }

    private void Clear()
    {
        // Reset the value to initial
        CurrentValue = _initialValue;

        // Sync pickers with the new value
        if (HasValue)
        {
            SyncPickersFromValue();
        }
        else
        {
            // Reset to sensible defaults when clearing to null
            DateValue = DateOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Today);
            TimeValue = TimeOnly.FromDateTime(DateTime.Now);
        }

        // CRITICAL FIX: Force Pattern to recreate by changing its @key
        // This ensures the Pattern reinitializes with the new value (or null)
        // Without this, the Pattern doesn't detect the change from incomplete → initial
        _patternKey = Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N");

        _isDirty = false;

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private Task OnDateChanged(DateOnly? value)
    {
        if (value.HasValue)
        {
            _tempDateValue = value.Value;
        }
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    private Task OnTimeChanged(TimeOnly? value)
    {
        if (value.HasValue)
        {
            _tempTimeValue = value.Value;
        }
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    private async Task ApplyPickerValue()
    {
        DateValue = _tempDateValue;
        TimeValue = _tempTimeValue;
        await UpdateCurrentValue();
        _isPickerOpen = false;
    }

    private async Task UpdateCurrentValue()
    {
        Type type = UnderlyingType;

        object? newValue = type switch
        {
            Type t when t == typeof(DateOnly) => DateValue,
            Type t when t == typeof(TimeOnly) => TimeValue,
            Type t when t == typeof(DateTime) => DateValue.ToDateTime(TimeValue),
            Type t when t == typeof(DateTimeOffset) => new DateTimeOffset(DateValue.ToDateTime(TimeValue)),
            _ => throw new InvalidOperationException($"Unsupported type: {type}")
        };

        CurrentValue = (TValue?)newValue;
        await Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    private string GetPickerTitle()
    {
        if (ShowDate && ShowTime) return "Select Date & Time";
        if (ShowDate) return "Select Date";
        return "Select Time";
    }

    protected override string? FormatValueAsString(TValue? value)
    {
        if (value == null) return null;

        Type type = UnderlyingType;

        return type switch
        {
            Type t when t == typeof(DateOnly)
                => ((DateOnly)(object)value).ToString(Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

            Type t when t == typeof(TimeOnly)
                => ((TimeOnly)(object)value).ToString(Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

            Type t when t == typeof(DateTime)
                => ((DateTime)(object)value).ToString(Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

            Type t when t == typeof(DateTimeOffset)
                => ((DateTimeOffset)(object)value).ToString(Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

            _ => value.ToString()
        };
    }

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(
        string? value,
        out TValue result,
        out string? validationErrorMessage)
    {
        result = default!;
        validationErrorMessage = null;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            return true;
        }

        try
        {
            Type type = UnderlyingType;

            object parsed = type switch
            {
                Type t when t == typeof(DateOnly)
                    => DateOnly.ParseExact(value, Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

                Type t when t == typeof(TimeOnly)
                    => TimeOnly.ParseExact(value, Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

                Type t when t == typeof(DateTime)
                    => DateTime.ParseExact(value, Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

                Type t when t == typeof(DateTimeOffset)
                    => DateTimeOffset.ParseExact(value, Format, CultureInfo.CurrentCulture),

                _ => throw new InvalidOperationException($"Unsupported type: {type}")
            };

            result = (TValue)parsed;
            return true;
        }
        catch (FormatException)
        {
            validationErrorMessage = $"The value '{value}' does not match the expected format ({Format}).";
            return false;
        }
    }

    private string GetCultureFormatString()
    {
        DateTimeFormatInfo dtfi = CultureInfo.CurrentCulture.DateTimeFormat;
        Type type = UnderlyingType;

        return type switch
        {
            Type t when t == typeof(DateOnly) => dtfi.ShortDatePattern,
            Type t when t == typeof(TimeOnly) => dtfi.ShortTimePattern,
            Type t when t == typeof(DateTime) || t == typeof(DateTimeOffset)
                => $"{dtfi.ShortDatePattern} {dtfi.ShortTimePattern}",
            _ => string.Empty
        };
    }
}



=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUIInputDateTime.razor.css ===

/* Picker dialog content */
bui-component[data-bui-component="input-date-time"] .bui-input-datetime__picker-content {

    flex-direction: column;
    gap: calc(0.5rem * var(--bui-density-multiplier));
}



=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUITimePicker.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms
@using System.Globalization

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IPickerFamilyComponent

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    <div class="bui-picker__row">
        <_BUIBtn Size="Size" OnClick="ToggleFormatClicked">
            @(Format == "24" ? "24h" : "12h")
        </_BUIBtn>

        <div class="bui-picker__row" style="flex:1; justify-content:center;">
            <div style="display:flex; flex-direction:column; align-items:center; gap:0.25rem;">
                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronUp"
                                     AriaLabel="Increment hour"
                                     OnClick="IncrementHourClicked" />
                <_BUIInText Value="@DisplayHour.ToString("00")"
                                          ValueChanged="OnHourInputChanged"
                                          maxlength="2" />
                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronDown"
                                     AriaLabel="Decrement hour"
                                     OnClick="DecrementHourClicked" />
            </div>

            <span class="bui-picker__separator">:</span>

            <div style="display:flex; flex-direction:column; align-items:center; gap:0.25rem;">
                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronUp"
                                     AriaLabel="Increment minute"
                                     OnClick="IncrementMinuteClicked" />
                <_BUIInText Value="@Minute.ToString("00")"
                                          ValueChanged="OnMinuteInputChanged"
                                          maxlength="2" />
                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronDown"
                                     AriaLabel="Decrement minute"
                                     OnClick="DecrementMinuteClicked" />
            </div>
        </div>

        @if (Format == "12")
        {
            <_BUIBtn OnClick="ToggleAmPmClicked">
                @AmPm
            </_BUIBtn>
        }
    </div>
</bui-component>

@code {
    [Parameter] public TimeOnly? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TimeOnly?> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    private int Hour;
    private int Minute;
    private string Format = "24";
    private string AmPm = "AM";

    private int DisplayHour => Format == "24" ? Hour : (Hour % 12 == 0 ? 12 : Hour % 12);

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        base.OnInitialized();
        Format = CultureInfo.CurrentCulture.DateTimeFormat.ShortTimePattern.Contains("tt") ? "12" : "24";
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();
        if (Value.HasValue)
        {
            Hour = Value.Value.Hour;
            Minute = Value.Value.Minute;
            AmPm = Hour >= 12 ? "PM" : "AM";
        }
    }

    private async Task IncrementHourClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await UpdateHour((Hour + 1) % 24);
    private async Task DecrementHourClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await UpdateHour((Hour + 23) % 24);
    private async Task IncrementMinuteClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await UpdateMinute((Minute + 1) % 60);
    private async Task DecrementMinuteClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await UpdateMinute((Minute + 59) % 60);

    private async Task OnHourInputChanged(string? value)
    {
        if (int.TryParse(value, out int h))
        {
            if (Format == "12")
            {
                if (h >= 1 && h <= 12)
                {
                    int newHour = h == 12 ? 0 : h;
                    if (AmPm == "PM") newHour += 12;
                    await UpdateHour(newHour);
                }
            }
            else if (h >= 0 && h < 24)
            {
                await UpdateHour(h);
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task OnMinuteInputChanged(string? value)
    {
        if (int.TryParse(value, out int m) && m >= 0 && m < 60)
            await UpdateMinute(m);
    }

    private async Task UpdateHour(int newHour)
    {
        Hour = newHour;
        AmPm = Hour >= 12 ? "PM" : "AM";
        await NotifyValueChanged();
    }

    private async Task UpdateMinute(int newMinute)
    {
        Minute = newMinute;
        await NotifyValueChanged();
    }

    private async Task NotifyValueChanged()
    {
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(new TimeOnly(Hour, Minute));
    }

    private void ToggleFormatClicked(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        Format = Format == "24" ? "12" : "24";
    }

    private async Task ToggleAmPmClicked(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (AmPm == "AM")
        {
            AmPm = "PM";
            if (Hour < 12) Hour += 12;
        }
        else
        {
            AmPm = "AM";
            if (Hour >= 12) Hour -= 12;
        }
        await NotifyValueChanged();
    }

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        base.BuildComponentDataAttributes(dataAttributes);
        dataAttributes["data-bui-picker-base"] = "true";
    }
}



=== Forms\DateAndTime\BUITimePicker.razor.css ===




=== Forms\Dropdown\JsInterop\DropdownCallbacksRelay.cs ===

using Microsoft.JSInterop;
using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public sealed class DropdownCallbacksRelay : IDisposable
{
    private readonly IDropdownJsCallback _callback;

    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnClickOutside))]
    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnKeyDown))]
    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnRequestPosition))]
    public DropdownCallbacksRelay(IDropdownJsCallback callback)
    {
        _callback = callback;
        DotNetReference = DotNetObjectReference.Create(this);
    }

    public DotNetObjectReference<DropdownCallbacksRelay> DotNetReference { get; }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        DotNetReference.Dispose();
    }

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnClickOutside()
        => _callback.OnClickOutside();

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnKeyDown(string key, bool shiftKey, bool ctrlKey)
        => _callback.OnKeyDown(key, shiftKey, ctrlKey);

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task<DropdownPosition> OnRequestPosition()
        => _callback.OnRequestPosition();
}



=== Forms\Dropdown\JsInterop\DropdownJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public interface IDropdownJsInterop
{
    ValueTask DisposeAsync(string componentId);

    ValueTask FocusSearchInputAsync(string componentId);

    ValueTask<DropdownPosition> GetPositionAsync(string componentId);

    ValueTask InitializeAsync(
                    ElementReference triggerElement,
        ElementReference menuElement,
        DotNetObjectReference<DropdownCallbacksRelay> dotnetReference,
        string componentId);
}

public sealed class DropdownJsInterop : ModuleJsInteropBase, IDropdownJsInterop
{
    public DropdownJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.Dropdown)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync(string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("dispose", componentId);
    }

    public async ValueTask FocusSearchInputAsync(string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("focusSearchInput", componentId);
    }

    public async ValueTask<DropdownPosition> GetPositionAsync(string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        return await module.InvokeAsync<DropdownPosition>("getPosition", componentId);
    }

    public async ValueTask InitializeAsync(
                    ElementReference triggerElement,
        ElementReference menuElement,
        DotNetObjectReference<DropdownCallbacksRelay> dotnetReference,
        string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync(
            "initialize",
            triggerElement,
            menuElement,
            dotnetReference,
            componentId);
    }
}



=== Forms\Dropdown\JsInterop\IDropdownJsCallback.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public interface IDropdownJsCallback
{
    Task OnClickOutside();

    Task OnKeyDown(string key, bool shiftKey, bool ctrlKey);

    Task<DropdownPosition> OnRequestPosition();
}

public record struct DropdownPosition(
    double TriggerTop,
    double TriggerLeft,
    double TriggerWidth,
    double TriggerHeight,
    double ViewportHeight,
    double ViewportWidth,
    double ScrollY);



=== Forms\Dropdown\BUIDropdownContainer.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components


@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms.Dropdown

@typeparam TValue

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<TValue, BUIDropdownContainer<TValue>, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IDropdownJsCallback
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private readonly string _componentId = $"bui-dropdown-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";

    private ElementReference _triggerElement;
    private ElementReference _menuElement;
    private DropdownCallbacksRelay? _callbacksRelay;
    private bool _jsInitialized;
    private DropdownPlacement _computedPlacement;
    private bool _isFocused;

    [Inject] private IDropdownJsInterop JsInterop { get; set; } = default!;

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public DropdownPlacement Placement { get; set; } = DropdownPlacement.Auto;
    [Parameter] public int MaxMenuHeight { get; set; } = 320;

    [Parameter, EditorRequired] public string DisplayValue { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    [Parameter] public bool HasValue { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string AriaRole { get; set; } = "listbox";
    [Parameter] public bool AriaMultiselectable { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? MenuContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback OnOpened { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback OnClosed { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<DropdownKeyboardEventArgs> OnKeyboardNavigation { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TValue> OnValueChanged { get; set; }

    public bool IsOpen { get; private set; }
    public string ComponentId => _componentId;

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIDropdownContainer<TValue>, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIDropdownContainer<TValue>, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = c => c.RenderDropdown(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = c => c.RenderDropdown(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = c => c.RenderDropdown()
        };

    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || IsOpen;

    private RenderFragment RenderDropdown() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       data-bui-dropdown-open="@IsOpen.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       data-bui-placement="@GetEffectivePlacement().ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

            <div class="bui-input__wrapper" @ref="_triggerElement">

                <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label" For="@_componentId" Required="@Required" />
                <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

                <button id="@_componentId"
                        type="button"
                        class="bui-input__field bui-dropdown__trigger"
                        @onclick="ToggleAsync"
                        @onfocus="HandleFocus"
                        @onblur="HandleBlur"
                        disabled="@IsDisabled"
                        aria-expanded="@IsOpen.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                        aria-haspopup="@AriaRole"
                        aria-describedby="@_helperTextId">

                    <span class="bui-dropdown__value @(HasValue ? "" : "bui-dropdown__placeholder")">
                        @if (HasValue)
                        {
                            @DisplayValue
                        }
                        else if ((string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) || IsFloated) && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(Placeholder))
                        {
                            @Placeholder
                        }
                    </span>

                    <_BUIAddon Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ExpandMore"
                               IconRotation="@(IsOpen ? 180 : 0)"
                               Size="Size" />
                </button>

                @if (IsOpen)
                {
                    <div class="bui-dropdown__menu"
                         @ref="_menuElement"
                         role="@AriaRole"
                         aria-multiselectable="@(AriaMultiselectable ? "true" : null)"
                         style="max-height: @(MaxMenuHeight)px;">
                        @MenuContent
                    </div>
                }

                <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />
                <BUIInputLoading Loading="@Loading" LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="@Size" />

            </div>

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="TValue"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

        </bui-component>
    };

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);

        if (IsOpen && !_jsInitialized)
        {
            _callbacksRelay ??= new DropdownCallbacksRelay(this);
            await JsInterop.InitializeAsync(_triggerElement, _menuElement, _callbacksRelay.DotNetReference, _componentId);
            _jsInitialized = true;

            if (Placement == DropdownPlacement.Auto)
            {
                await ComputePlacementAsync();
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task ComputePlacementAsync()
    {
        DropdownPosition position = await JsInterop.GetPositionAsync(_componentId);
        double spaceBelow = position.ViewportHeight - position.TriggerTop - position.TriggerHeight;
        double spaceAbove = position.TriggerTop;

        _computedPlacement = spaceBelow >= MaxMenuHeight || spaceBelow >= spaceAbove
            ? DropdownPlacement.Bottom
            : DropdownPlacement.Top;

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private DropdownPlacement GetEffectivePlacement()
        => Placement == DropdownPlacement.Auto ? _computedPlacement : Placement;

    public async Task ToggleAsync()
    {
        if (Disabled || Loading) return;

        if (IsOpen)
            await CloseAsync();
        else
            await OpenAsync();
    }

    public async Task OpenAsync()
    {
        if (IsOpen || Disabled || Loading) return;

        IsOpen = true;
        _computedPlacement = Placement == DropdownPlacement.Auto ? DropdownPlacement.Bottom : Placement;
        StateHasChanged();

        await OnOpened.InvokeAsync();
    }

    public async Task CloseAsync()
    {
        if (!IsOpen) return;

        IsOpen = false;
        _jsInitialized = false;

        if (_callbacksRelay != null)
        {
            await JsInterop.DisposeAsync(_componentId);
        }

        StateHasChanged();
        await OnClosed.InvokeAsync();
    }

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
    }

    Task IDropdownJsCallback.OnClickOutside() => CloseAsync();

    async Task IDropdownJsCallback.OnKeyDown(string key, bool shiftKey, bool ctrlKey)
    {
        DropdownKeyboardEventArgs args = new(key, shiftKey, ctrlKey);

        switch (key)
        {
            case "Escape":
            case "Tab":
                await CloseAsync();
                break;

            case "ArrowDown":
                if (!IsOpen)
                    await OpenAsync();
                else
                    await OnKeyboardNavigation.InvokeAsync(args);
                break;

            case "ArrowUp":
            case "Home":
            case "End":
                if (IsOpen)
                    await OnKeyboardNavigation.InvokeAsync(args);
                break;

            case "Enter":
            case " ":
                if (IsOpen)
                    await OnKeyboardNavigation.InvokeAsync(args);
                else
                    await OpenAsync();
                break;

            case "a":
                if (IsOpen && ctrlKey)
                    await OnKeyboardNavigation.InvokeAsync(args);
                break;

            default:
                await OnKeyboardNavigation.InvokeAsync(args);
                break;
        }
    }

    async Task<DropdownPosition> IDropdownJsCallback.OnRequestPosition()
        => await JsInterop.GetPositionAsync(_componentId);

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out TValue result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;
        result = default!;
        return true;
    }

    public async Task FocusSearchInputAsync()
    {
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.FocusSearchInputAsync(_componentId);
        }
    }

    public override async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.DisposeAsync(_componentId);
        }

        _callbacksRelay?.Dispose();
        await base.DisposeAsync();
    }
}
