=== Forms\Dropdown\BUIInputDropdown.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms.Dropdown
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Components.Selection
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Search
@using System.Linq.Expressions

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@typeparam TValue

@implements IDropdownContainer
@implements IAsyncDisposable

<CascadingValue Value="(IDropdownContainer)this" IsFixed="true">
    @ChildContent
</CascadingValue>

<BUIDropdownContainer @ref="_container"
                      TValue="TValue"
                      Value="@Value"
                      ValueChanged="@SetValueAsync"
                      ValueExpression="@ValueExpression"
                      Variant="@Variant"
                      Size="@Size"
                      Density="@Density"
                      Disabled="@Disabled"
                      Loading="@IsLoading"
                      LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant"
                      Required="@Required"
                      ReadOnly="@ReadOnly"
                      Shadow="@Shadow"
                      Border="@Border"
                      Color="@Color"
                      BackgroundColor="@BackgroundColor"
                      Label="@Label"
                      Placeholder="@Placeholder"
                      HelperText="@HelperText"
                      Placement="@Placement"
                      MaxMenuHeight="@ComputedMaxMenuHeight"
                      DisplayValue="@GetDisplayValue()"
                      HasValue="@(_selectionState.Count > 0)"
                      AriaRole="listbox"
                      AriaMultiselectable="@_selectionState.IsMultiple"
                      OnOpened="@HandleOpenedAsync"
                      OnClosed="@HandleClosed"
                      OnKeyboardNavigation="@HandleKeyboardNavigation">
   <MenuContent>
    @if (Searchable)
    {
        <div class="bui-dropdown__search">
            <_BUIInText Value="@_searchText"
                                      Placeholder="@SearchPlaceholder"
                                      Size="Size"
                                      UpdateOnInput="true"
                                      OnInput="OnSearchInputChanged"
                                      @onclick:stopPropagation="true" />
        </div>
    }

    @if (_selectionState.IsMultiple && ShowSelectAll && _options.Count > 0)
    {
        <div class="bui-dropdown__select-all">
            <_BUIBtn OnClick="SelectAllClicked" OnClickStopPropagation="true">
                @SelectAllText
            </_BUIBtn>
            <_BUIBtn OnClick="DeselectAllClicked" OnClickStopPropagation="true">
                @DeselectAllText
            </_BUIBtn>
        </div>
    }

    <div class="bui-dropdown__items">
        @{
            List<ISelectionOption> filteredOptions = GetFilteredOptions();
        }

        @foreach (ISelectionOption option in filteredOptions)
        {
            bool isSelected = _selectionState.IsSelected(option.Value);
            bool isFocused = _focusedIndex >= 0 && filteredOptions.ElementAtOrDefault(_focusedIndex) == option;

            <div class="bui-dropdown__option @(isSelected ? "bui-dropdown__option--selected" : "") @(isFocused ? "bui-dropdown__option--focused" : "") @(option.IsDisabled ? "bui-dropdown__option--disabled" : "")"
                 role="option"
                 aria-selected="@isSelected.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                 aria-disabled="@(option.IsDisabled ? "true" : null)"
                 tabindex="@(option.IsDisabled ? -1 : 0)"
                 @onclick="() => SelectOptionAsync(option)"
                 @onclick:stopPropagation="true">

                @if (_selectionState.IsMultiple)
                {
                    <_BUICheckMark Checked="@isSelected"
                                            Size="Size"
                                            Disabled="option.IsDisabled" />
                }

                <span class="bui-dropdown__option-content">
                    @option.Content
                </span>
            </div>
        }

        @if (filteredOptions.Count == 0)
        {
            <div class="bui-dropdown__no-options">
                @if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_searchText))
                {
                    @(NoOptionsTemplate ?? _defaultNoOptionsTemplate)
                }
                else
                {
                    @if (NoResultsTemplate != null)
                    {
                        @NoResultsTemplate(new NoResultsContext(_searchText, _options.Count))
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <span>No results for "@_searchText"</span>
                    }
                }
            </div>
        }
    </div>
</MenuContent>
</BUIDropdownContainer>

@code {
    private BUIDropdownContainer<TValue>? _container;
    private readonly List<ISelectionOption> _options = [];
    private readonly SelectionState<TValue> _selectionState;

    private string _searchText = string.Empty;
    private int _focusedIndex = -1;

    private readonly RenderFragment _defaultNoOptionsTemplate;

    [Parameter] public TValue? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TValue> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Expression<Func<TValue>>? ValueExpression { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public BUIInputVariant Variant { get; set; } = BUIInputVariant.Outlined;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public bool FullWidth { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool IsLoading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant? LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Required { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ReadOnly { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnSelect { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public DropdownPlacement Placement { get; set; } = DropdownPlacement.Auto;
    [Parameter] public int MaxVisibleItems { get; set; } = 8;
    [Parameter] public int ItemHeight { get; set; } = 40;

    [Parameter] public bool Searchable { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string SearchPlaceholder { get; set; } = "Search...";
    [Parameter] public SearchMode SearchMode { get; set; } = SearchMode.Smart;

    [Parameter] public bool ShowSelectAll { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public string SelectAllText { get; set; } = "Select All";
    [Parameter] public string DeselectAllText { get; set; } = "Deselect All";

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? NoOptionsTemplate { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment<NoResultsContext>? NoResultsTemplate { get; set; }

    bool IDropdownContainer.IsMultiple => _selectionState.IsMultiple;
    Type IDropdownContainer.ElementType => _selectionState.ElementType;

    private int ComputedMaxMenuHeight => Math.Min(_options.Count, MaxVisibleItems) * ItemHeight + 8 +
        (Searchable ? 48 : 0) +
        (_selectionState.IsMultiple && ShowSelectAll ? 40 : 0);

    public BUIInputDropdown()
    {
        _selectionState = new SelectionState<TValue>();

        _defaultNoOptionsTemplate = builder =>
        {
            builder.AddContent(0, "No options available");
        };
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        _selectionState.SetValue(Value);
    }

    void IDropdownContainer.RegisterOption(ISelectionOption option)
    {
        if (!_options.Contains(option))
        {
            _options.Add(option);
            StateHasChanged();
        }
    }

    void IDropdownContainer.UnregisterOption(ISelectionOption option)
    {
        if (_options.Remove(option))
        {
            StateHasChanged();
        }
    }

    private List<ISelectionOption> GetFilteredOptions()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_searchText))
            return _options.ToList();

        return SearchAlgorithms
            .Search(_options, _searchText, o => o.DisplayText, SearchMode)
            .Select(r => r.Item)
            .ToList();
    }

    private string GetDisplayValue()
    {
        if (_selectionState.Count == 0)
            return string.Empty;

        if (!_selectionState.IsMultiple)
        {
            object? selectedValue = _selectionState.SelectedValues.FirstOrDefault();
            ISelectionOption? option = _options.FirstOrDefault(o => Equals(o.Value, selectedValue));
            return option?.DisplayText ?? selectedValue?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        }

        if (_selectionState.Count == 1)
        {
            object? selectedValue = _selectionState.SelectedValues.First();
            ISelectionOption? option = _options.FirstOrDefault(o => Equals(o.Value, selectedValue));
            return option?.DisplayText ?? selectedValue?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        }

        return $"{_selectionState.Count} selected";
    }

    private async Task SetValueAsync(TValue? value)
    {
        Value = value;
        _selectionState.SetValue(value);
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(value);
    }
    private async Task OnSearchInputChanged(string? value)
    {
        _searchText = value ?? string.Empty;
        _focusedIndex = -1;
    }

    private async Task SelectAllClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await SelectAll();
    private async Task DeselectAllClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await DeselectAll();

    private async Task HandleOpenedAsync()
    {
        _searchText = string.Empty;
        _focusedIndex = -1;

        if (Searchable && _container != null)
        {
            await Task.Yield();
            await _container.FocusSearchInputAsync();
        }
    }

    private void HandleClosed()
    {
        _searchText = string.Empty;
        _focusedIndex = -1;
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyboardNavigation(DropdownKeyboardEventArgs args)
    {
        List<ISelectionOption> filtered = GetFilteredOptions();

        switch (args.Key)
        {
            case "ArrowDown":
                _focusedIndex = Math.Min(_focusedIndex + 1, filtered.Count - 1);
                StateHasChanged();
                break;

            case "ArrowUp":
                _focusedIndex = Math.Max(_focusedIndex - 1, 0);
                StateHasChanged();
                break;

            case " ":
                if (_focusedIndex >= 0 && _focusedIndex < filtered.Count)
                {
                    await SelectOptionAsync(filtered[_focusedIndex]);
                }
                break;

            case "Enter":
                if (_focusedIndex >= 0 && _focusedIndex < filtered.Count)
                {
                    await SelectOptionAsync(filtered[_focusedIndex]);
                }
                if (_container != null)
                {
                    await _container.CloseAsync();
                }
                break;

            case "Home":
                _focusedIndex = 0;
                StateHasChanged();
                break;

            case "End":
                _focusedIndex = filtered.Count - 1;
                StateHasChanged();
                break;

            case "a" when args.CtrlKey && _selectionState.IsMultiple:
                if (args.ShiftKey)
                    await DeselectAll();
                else
                    await SelectAll();
                break;
        }
    }

    private async Task SelectOptionAsync(ISelectionOption option)
    {
        if (Disabled || option.IsDisabled) return;

        if (_selectionState.IsMultiple)
        {
            _selectionState.Toggle(option.Value);
        }
        else
        {
            _selectionState.SetSingleValue(option.Value);
        }

        await SetValueAsync(_selectionState.GetValue());

        if (!_selectionState.IsMultiple && CloseOnSelect && _container != null)
        {
            await _container.CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private async Task SelectAll()
    {
        if (!_selectionState.IsMultiple || Disabled) return;

        IEnumerable<object?> allValues = GetFilteredOptions()
            .Where(o => !o.IsDisabled)
            .Select(o => o.Value);

        _selectionState.SelectAll(allValues);
        await SetValueAsync(_selectionState.GetValue());
    }

    private async Task DeselectAll()
    {
        if (!_selectionState.IsMultiple || Disabled) return;
        _selectionState.Clear();
        await SetValueAsync(_selectionState.GetValue());
    }

    private void OnSearchInput(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        _searchText = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        _focusedIndex = -1;
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        _options.Clear();

        if (_container != null)
        {
            await _container.DisposeAsync();
        }
    }
}

=== Forms\Dropdown\BUIInputDropdownTree.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms.Dropdown
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Components.Selection
@using System.Linq.Expressions

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@typeparam TItem
@typeparam TValue

@implements IAsyncDisposable

<BUIDropdownContainer @ref="_container"
                      TValue="TValue"
                      Value="@Value"
                      ValueChanged="@SetValueAsync"
                      ValueExpression="@ValueExpression"
                      Variant="@Variant"
                      Size="@Size"
                      Density="@Density"
                      Disabled="@Disabled"
                      Loading="@IsLoading"
                      LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant"
                      Required="@Required"
                      ReadOnly="@ReadOnly"
                      Shadow="@Shadow"
                      Border="@Border"
                      Color="@Color"
                      BackgroundColor="@BackgroundColor"
                      Label="@Label"
                      Placeholder="@Placeholder"
                      HelperText="@HelperText"
                      Placement="@Placement"
                      MaxMenuHeight="@MaxMenuHeight"
                      DisplayValue="@GetDisplayValue()"
                      HasValue="@(_internalSelectedKeys.Count > 0)"
                      AriaRole="tree"
                      AriaMultiselectable="@IsMultiple"
                      OnOpened="@HandleOpened"
                      OnClosed="@HandleClosed"
                      OnKeyboardNavigation="@HandleKeyboardNavigation">
    <MenuContent>
        <div class="bui-dropdown__tree-content">
            <BUITreeSelector TItem="TItem"
                             @ref="_treeSelectorRef"
                             Items="@Items"
                             KeySelector="@KeySelector"
                             ChildrenSelector="@ChildrenSelector"
                             HasChildrenSelector="@HasChildrenSelector"
                             OnLoadChildren="@OnLoadChildren"
                             NodeTemplate="@NodeTemplate"
                             DisplayTextSelector="@DisplayTextSelector"
                             SelectedKeys="@_internalSelectedKeys"
                             SelectedKeysChanged="@OnTreeSelectionChangedAsync"
                             SelectionMode="@(IsMultiple ? TreeSelectionMode.Multiple : TreeSelectionMode.Single)"
                             Size="@Size"
                             ShowCheckboxes="@ShowCheckboxes"
                             ExpandAll="@ExpandAll"
                             ExpandedKeys="@ExpandedKeys"
                             ExpandedKeysChanged="@ExpandedKeysChanged"
                             AnimateExpand="@AnimateExpand" />

            @if (Items == null || !Items.Any())
            {
                <div class="bui-dropdown__no-options">
                    @(NoOptionsTemplate ?? _defaultNoOptionsTemplate)
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </MenuContent>
</BUIDropdownContainer>

@code {
    private readonly SelectionTypeInfo _typeInfo;
    private BUIDropdownContainer<TValue>? _container;
    private BUITreeSelector<TItem>? _treeSelectorRef;
    private HashSet<string> _internalSelectedKeys = new();

    private readonly RenderFragment _defaultNoOptionsTemplate;

    [Parameter] public TValue? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TValue> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Expression<Func<TValue>>? ValueExpression { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public BUIInputVariant Variant { get; set; } = BUIInputVariant.Outlined;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public bool FullWidth { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool IsLoading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant? LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Required { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ReadOnly { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public DropdownPlacement Placement { get; set; } = DropdownPlacement.Auto;
    [Parameter] public int MaxMenuHeight { get; set; } = 320;
    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnSelect { get; set; } = true;

    [Parameter, EditorRequired] public IEnumerable<TItem>? Items { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, string>? KeySelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? ChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, bool>? HasChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, Task<IEnumerable<TItem>>>? OnLoadChildren { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>? NodeTemplate { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, string>? DisplayTextSelector { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool ShowCheckboxes { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool ExpandAll { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool AnimateExpand { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public HashSet<string>? ExpandedKeys { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<HashSet<string>> ExpandedKeysChanged { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public TreeSelectionCascade SelectionCascade { get; set; } = TreeSelectionCascade.None;

    [Parameter] public TreeDisplayMode DisplayMode { get; set; } = TreeDisplayMode.Single;
    [Parameter] public string InheritanceSeparator { get; set; } = " > ";

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? NoOptionsTemplate { get; set; }

    public bool IsMultiple => _typeInfo.IsMultiple;

    public BUIInputDropdownTree()
    {
        _typeInfo = new SelectionTypeInfo(typeof(TValue));

        _defaultNoOptionsTemplate = builder =>
        {
            builder.AddContent(0, "No options available");
        };
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        SyncSelectionFromValue();
    }

    private void SyncSelectionFromValue()
    {
        _internalSelectedKeys.Clear();

        if (Value == null) return;

        IEnumerable<object> values = _typeInfo.ExtractValues(Value);

        foreach (object value in values)
        {
            string? key = FindKeyForValue(value);
            if (key != null)
                _internalSelectedKeys.Add(key);
        }
    }

    private string? FindKeyForValue(object value)
    {
        if (Items == null || KeySelector == null) return null;
        return FindKeyRecursive(Items, value);
    }

    private string? FindKeyRecursive(IEnumerable<TItem> items, object value)
    {
        foreach (TItem item in items)
        {
            if (Equals(item, value))
                return KeySelector!(item);

            if (ChildrenSelector != null)
            {
                IEnumerable<TItem>? children = ChildrenSelector(item);
                if (children != null)
                {
                    string? found = FindKeyRecursive(children, value);
                    if (found != null) return found;
                }
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    private TItem? FindItemByKey(string key)
    {
        if (Items == null || KeySelector == null) return default;
        return FindItemByKeyRecursive(Items, key);
    }

    private TItem? FindItemByKeyRecursive(IEnumerable<TItem> items, string key)
    {
        foreach (TItem item in items)
        {
            if (KeySelector!(item) == key)
                return item;

            if (ChildrenSelector != null)
            {
                IEnumerable<TItem>? children = ChildrenSelector(item);
                if (children != null)
                {
                    TItem? found = FindItemByKeyRecursive(children, key);
                    if (found != null) return found;
                }
            }
        }
        return default;
    }

    private string GetDisplayValue()
    {
        if (_internalSelectedKeys.Count == 0)
            return string.Empty;

        if (!IsMultiple || _internalSelectedKeys.Count == 1)
        {
            string key = _internalSelectedKeys.First();
            TItem? item = FindItemByKey(key);

            if (item != null)
            {
                if (DisplayMode == TreeDisplayMode.Inheritance)
                {
                    return GetInheritancePath(key);
                }

                return GetItemDisplayText(item, key);
            }
            return key;
        }

        return $"{_internalSelectedKeys.Count} selected";
    }

    private string GetItemDisplayText(TItem item, string fallbackKey)
    {
        if (DisplayTextSelector != null)
            return DisplayTextSelector(item);

        return item?.ToString() ?? fallbackKey;
    }

    private string GetInheritancePath(string key)
    {
        List<string> path = new();
        TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? node = _treeSelectorRef?.GetNode(key);

        while (node != null)
        {
            string text = node.Item != null
                ? GetItemDisplayText(node.Item, node.Key)
                : node.Text ?? node.Key;

            path.Insert(0, text);
            node = node.ParentNode;
        }

        return string.Join(InheritanceSeparator, path);
    }

    private async Task SetValueAsync(TValue? value)
    {
        Value = value;
        SyncSelectionFromValue();
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(value);
    }

    private async Task OnTreeSelectionChangedAsync(HashSet<string> selectedKeys)
    {
        HashSet<string> newKeys = ApplySelectionCascade(selectedKeys);
        _internalSelectedKeys = newKeys;

        List<object> selectedValues = new();
        foreach (string key in _internalSelectedKeys)
        {
            TItem? item = FindItemByKey(key);
            if (item != null)
                selectedValues.Add(item);
        }

        TValue newValue = _typeInfo.CreateValue<TValue>(selectedValues);
        Value = newValue;
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(newValue);

        if (!IsMultiple && CloseOnSelect && _internalSelectedKeys.Count > 0 && _container != null)
        {
            await _container.CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private HashSet<string> ApplySelectionCascade(HashSet<string> selectedKeys)
    {
        if (SelectionCascade == TreeSelectionCascade.None)
            return selectedKeys;

        HashSet<string> result = new(selectedKeys);

        foreach (string key in selectedKeys.ToList())
        {
            TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? node = _treeSelectorRef?.GetNode(key);
            if (node == null) continue;

            if (SelectionCascade == TreeSelectionCascade.Children || SelectionCascade == TreeSelectionCascade.Both)
            {
                AddDescendantKeys(node, result);
            }

            if (SelectionCascade == TreeSelectionCascade.Parents || SelectionCascade == TreeSelectionCascade.Both)
            {
                AddAncestorKeys(node, result);
            }
        }

        return result;
    }

    private void AddDescendantKeys(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node, HashSet<string> keys)
    {
        foreach (TreeSelectionNode<TItem> child in node.ChildrenInternal)
        {
            if (!child.IsDisabled)
            {
                keys.Add(child.Key);
                AddDescendantKeys(child, keys);
            }
        }
    }

    private void AddAncestorKeys(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node, HashSet<string> keys)
    {
        TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? parent = node.ParentNode;
        while (parent != null)
        {
            if (!parent.IsDisabled)
                keys.Add(parent.Key);
            parent = parent.ParentNode;
        }
    }

    private void HandleOpened()
    {
    }

    private void HandleClosed()
    {
    }

    private Task HandleKeyboardNavigation(DropdownKeyboardEventArgs args)
    {
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    public void ExpandAllNodes() => _treeSelectorRef?.ExpandAllNodes();
    public void CollapseAllNodes() => _treeSelectorRef?.CollapseAllNodes();

    public void ClearSelection()
    {
        _internalSelectedKeys.Clear();
        _treeSelectorRef?.ClearSelection();
        Value = default;
        ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(default);
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        if (_container != null)
        {
            await _container.DisposeAsync();
        }
    }
}

=== Forms\Dropdown\DropdownOption.cs ===

// File: Components/Forms/Dropdown/DropdownOption.cs
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms.Dropdown;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Components.Selection;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public class DropdownOption<TOption> : ComponentBase, ISelectionOption, IDisposable
{
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [CascadingParameter] public IDropdownContainer? Container { get; set; }

    RenderFragment? ISelectionOption.Content => ChildContent ?? (builder => builder.AddContent(0, Text ?? Value?.ToString()));
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    string ISelectionOption.DisplayText => Text ?? Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
    bool ISelectionOption.IsDisabled => Disabled;
    [Parameter] public string? Text { get; set; }
    [Parameter, EditorRequired] public TOption? Value { get; set; }
    object? ISelectionOption.Value => Value;

    public void Dispose()
    {
        Container?.UnregisterOption(this);
    }

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        if (Container == null)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException($"{nameof(DropdownOption<TOption>)} must be used inside a BUIInputDropdown.");
        }

        ValidateOptionType();
        Container.RegisterOption(this);
    }

    private void ValidateOptionType()
    {
        Type optionType = typeof(TOption);
        Type expectedType = Container!.ElementType;

        if (!expectedType.IsAssignableFrom(optionType))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"DropdownOption<{optionType.Name}> is not compatible with the dropdown's element type {expectedType.Name}. " +
                $"For single selection, use DropdownOption<{expectedType.Name}>. " +
                $"For multiple selection (arrays/lists), use DropdownOption<{expectedType.Name}> (the element type, not the collection type).");
        }
    }
}

=== Forms\Number\BUIInputNumber.razor ===

@using System.Globalization
@using System.Text
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@typeparam TValue

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<TValue, BUIInputNumber<TValue>, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private ElementReference _inputRef;
    private string _inputId = $"bui-number-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private CancellationTokenSource? _accelerationCts;
    private bool _isIncrementing;
    private bool _isDecrementing;
    private readonly Type _underlyingType;
    private readonly bool _isNullable;
    private bool _preventKeyDown = false;

    private string _displayText = string.Empty;
    private bool _isFocused = false;
    private bool _isDirty;

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // Number-specific parameters
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public TValue? Min { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public TValue? Max { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public decimal Step { get; set; } = 1m;

    [Parameter] public int? DecimalPlaces { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool AllowNegative { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool ShowStepButtons { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public StepButtonPlacement ButtonPlacement { get; set; } = StepButtonPlacement.Right;

    [Parameter] public bool UseThousandsSeparator { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public CultureInfo? Culture { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool EnableMouseWheel { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool EnableAcceleration { get; set; } = true;

    [Parameter] public int AccelerationInitialDelay { get; set; } = 400;
    [Parameter] public int AccelerationMinDelay { get; set; } = 50;
    [Parameter] public int AccelerationStepReduction { get; set; } = 50;

    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TValue?> OnIncrement { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TValue?> OnDecrement { get; set; }

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    private CultureInfo CurrentCulture => Culture ?? CultureInfo.CurrentCulture;
    private NumberFormatInfo NumberFormat => CurrentCulture.NumberFormat;
    private char DecimalSeparator => NumberFormat.NumberDecimalSeparator[0];
    private char GroupSeparator => NumberFormat.NumberGroupSeparator[0];
    private string NegativeSign => NumberFormat.NegativeSign;
    private bool HasValue => CurrentValue != null && !EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(CurrentValue, default);
    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || _isDirty;

    public BUIInputNumber()
    {
        _underlyingType = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(typeof(TValue)) ?? typeof(TValue);
        _isNullable = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(typeof(TValue)) != null;

        if (!IsNumericType(_underlyingType))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"BUIInputNumber only supports numeric types. Provided type: {typeof(TValue).Name}");
        }
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();

        if (!_isFocused)
        {
            _displayText = FormatValueForDisplay(CurrentValue);
        }
    }

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputNumber<TValue>, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputNumber<TValue>, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = i => i.RenderInput()
        };

    private static bool IsNumericType(Type type)
    {
        return type == typeof(int) || type == typeof(long) || type == typeof(decimal) ||
               type == typeof(double) || type == typeof(float) || type == typeof(short) ||
               type == typeof(byte) || type == typeof(uint) || type == typeof(ulong) ||
               type == typeof(ushort) || type == typeof(sbyte);
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderInput() => __builder =>
{
    <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                   data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                   data-bui-button-placement="@ButtonPlacement.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

        <div class="bui-input__wrapper">

            <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label"
                             For="@_inputId"
                             Required="@Required" />

            @if (ShowStepButtons && ButtonPlacement == StepButtonPlacement.Left)
            {
                @RenderStepButtons()
            }

            <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

            <input @ref="_inputRef"
                   id="@_inputId"
                   type="text"
                   inputmode="decimal"
                   class="bui-input__field"
                   value="@_displayText"
                   @oninput="HandleInput"
                   @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown"
                   @onkeydown:preventDefault="_preventKeyDown"
                   @onwheel="HandleWheel"
                   @onfocus="HandleFocus"
                   @onblur="HandleBlur"
                   aria-label="@(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) ? Placeholder : null)"
                   aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                   aria-invalid="@IsError.ToString().ToLower()"
                   aria-required="@Required.ToString().ToLower()"
                   placeholder="@(IsFloated? Placeholder : null)"
                   disabled="@IsDisabled"
                   readonly="@ReadOnly"
                   required="@Required" />

            @if (ShowStepButtons && ButtonPlacement == StepButtonPlacement.Right)
            {
                @RenderStepButtons()
            }

            <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />
            <BUIInputLoading Loading="@Loading" LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="@Size" />

        </div>

        <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="TValue"
                         Id="@_helperTextId"
                         HelperText="@HelperText"
                         ShowValidation="@IsError"
                         EditContext="@EditContext"
                         For="@ValueExpression" />

    </bui-component>
};

    private RenderFragment RenderStepButtons() => __builder =>
    {
        <div class="bui-input__step-buttons">
            <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronUp"
                        Disabled="@(Disabled || IsAtMax())"
                        AriaLabel="Increment"
                        @onmousedown="StartIncrement"
                        @onmouseup="StopIncrement"
                        @onmouseleave="StopIncrement" />
            <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronDown"
                        Disabled="@(Disabled || IsAtMin())"
                        AriaLabel="Decrement"
                        @onmousedown="StartDecrement"
                        @onmouseup="StopDecrement"
                        @onmouseleave="StopDecrement" />
        </div>
    };
    private string FormatValueForDisplay(TValue? value)
    {
        if (value == null || EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(value, default))
            return string.Empty;

        decimal decimalValue = ConvertToDecimal(value);

        string format;
        if (DecimalPlaces.HasValue)
        {
            format = UseThousandsSeparator
                ? $"N{DecimalPlaces.Value}"
                : $"F{DecimalPlaces.Value}";
        }
        else
        {
            format = UseThousandsSeparator ? "N" : "G";
        }

        return decimalValue.ToString(format, NumberFormat);
    }

    private void HandleInput(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        if (Disabled || ReadOnly) return;

        string? inputValue = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        _isDirty = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(inputValue);
        _displayText = inputValue;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(inputValue))
        {
            CurrentValue = default;
            return;
        }

        if (TryParseInput(inputValue, out TValue? parsed))
        {
            TValue? clamped = ClampValue(parsed);
            if (!EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(CurrentValue, clamped))
            {
                CurrentValue = clamped;
            }
        }
    }

    private bool IsValidInputChar(char c, string currentText)
    {
        if (char.IsDigit(c)) return true;

        if (c == '.' || c == ',')
        {
            return true;
        }

        if (AllowNegative && (c == '-'))
        {
            return string.IsNullOrEmpty(currentText) || !currentText.Contains('-');
        }

        return false;
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        _preventKeyDown = false;

        if (Disabled || ReadOnly) return;

        switch (e.Key)
        {
            case "ArrowUp":
                await IncrementValue();
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                return;
            case "ArrowDown":
                await DecrementValue();
                _preventKeyDown = true;
                return;
            case "Backspace":
            case "Delete":
            case "Tab":
            case "Enter":
            case "Escape":
            case "ArrowLeft":
            case "ArrowRight":
            case "Home":
            case "End":
                return;
        }

        if (e.CtrlKey || e.MetaKey)
        {
            return;
        }

        if (e.Key.Length == 1)
        {
            char key = e.Key[0];

            if (!IsValidInputChar(key, _displayText))
            {
                _preventKeyDown = true;
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleWheel(WheelEventArgs e)
    {
        if (!EnableMouseWheel || Disabled || ReadOnly || !_isFocused) return;

        if (e.DeltaY < 0)
            await IncrementValue();
        else if (e.DeltaY > 0)
            await DecrementValue();
    }

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;

        if (CurrentValue != null && !EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(CurrentValue, default))
        {
            decimal decimalValue = ConvertToDecimal(CurrentValue);

            string format = DecimalPlaces.HasValue
                ? $"F{DecimalPlaces.Value}"
                : "G";

            _displayText = decimalValue.ToString(format, NumberFormat);
        }

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
        _isDirty = false;

        if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_displayText))
        {
            if (TryParseInput(_displayText, out TValue? parsed))
            {
                TValue? clamped = ClampValue(parsed);
                CurrentValue = clamped;
                _displayText = FormatValueForDisplay(CurrentValue);
            }
            else
            {
                _displayText = FormatValueForDisplay(CurrentValue);
            }
        }
        else
        {
            CurrentValue = default;
            _displayText = string.Empty;
        }

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void StartIncrement(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (Disabled || IsAtMax()) return;

        _isIncrementing = true;
        _ = IncrementValue();

        if (EnableAcceleration)
        {
            _accelerationCts = new CancellationTokenSource();
            _ = RunAcceleratedAction(IncrementValue, _accelerationCts.Token);
        }
    }

    private void StopIncrement(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        _isIncrementing = false;
        _accelerationCts?.Cancel();
        _accelerationCts?.Dispose();
        _accelerationCts = null;
    }

    private void StartDecrement(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (Disabled || IsAtMin()) return;

        _isDecrementing = true;
        _ = DecrementValue();

        if (EnableAcceleration)
        {
            _accelerationCts = new CancellationTokenSource();
            _ = RunAcceleratedAction(DecrementValue, _accelerationCts.Token);
        }
    }

    private void StopDecrement(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        _isDecrementing = false;
        _accelerationCts?.Cancel();
        _accelerationCts?.Dispose();
        _accelerationCts = null;
    }

    private bool _preventStepKeyDown = false;

    private void HandleIncrementKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        _preventStepKeyDown = false;

        if (e.Key != " " && e.Key != "Enter") return;

        _preventStepKeyDown = true;

        if (e.Repeat) return;

        if (Disabled || IsAtMax()) return;

        _isIncrementing = true;
        _ = IncrementValue();

        if (EnableAcceleration)
        {
            _accelerationCts = new CancellationTokenSource();
            _ = RunAcceleratedAction(IncrementValue, _accelerationCts.Token);
        }
    }

    private void HandleIncrementKeyUp(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.Key != " " && e.Key != "Enter") return;

        _isIncrementing = false;
        _accelerationCts?.Cancel();
        _accelerationCts?.Dispose();
        _accelerationCts = null;
    }

    private void HandleDecrementKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        _preventStepKeyDown = false;

        if (e.Key != " " && e.Key != "Enter") return;

        _preventStepKeyDown = true;

        if (e.Repeat) return;

        if (Disabled || IsAtMin()) return;

        _isDecrementing = true;
        _ = DecrementValue();

        if (EnableAcceleration)
        {
            _accelerationCts = new CancellationTokenSource();
            _ = RunAcceleratedAction(DecrementValue, _accelerationCts.Token);
        }
    }

    private void HandleDecrementKeyUp(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.Key != " " && e.Key != "Enter") return;

        _isDecrementing = false;
        _accelerationCts?.Cancel();
        _accelerationCts?.Dispose();
        _accelerationCts = null;
    }

    private async Task RunAcceleratedAction(Func<Task> action, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
    {
        int currentDelay = AccelerationInitialDelay;

        try
        {
            while (!cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)
            {
                await Task.Delay(currentDelay, cancellationToken);

                if (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)
                    break;

                await InvokeAsync(async () =>
                {
                    await action();
                    StateHasChanged();
                });

                if (currentDelay > AccelerationMinDelay)
                {
                    currentDelay = Math.Max(AccelerationMinDelay, currentDelay - AccelerationStepReduction);
                }
            }
        }
        catch (TaskCanceledException)
        {
        }
    }

    private async Task IncrementValue()
    {
        if (Disabled || IsAtMax()) return;

        decimal current = CurrentValue != null
            ? ConvertToDecimal(CurrentValue)
            : 0m;

        decimal newValue = current + Step;
        TValue? converted = ConvertFromDecimal(newValue);
        TValue? clamped = ClampValue(converted);

        CurrentValue = clamped;
        _displayText = FormatValueForDisplay(CurrentValue);

        StateHasChanged();

        if (OnIncrement.HasDelegate)
            await OnIncrement.InvokeAsync(CurrentValue);
    }

    private async Task DecrementValue()
    {
        if (Disabled || IsAtMin()) return;

        decimal current = CurrentValue != null
            ? ConvertToDecimal(CurrentValue)
            : 0m;

        decimal newValue = current - Step;
        TValue? converted = ConvertFromDecimal(newValue);
        TValue? clamped = ClampValue(converted);

        CurrentValue = clamped;
        _displayText = FormatValueForDisplay(CurrentValue);

        StateHasChanged();

        if (OnDecrement.HasDelegate)
            await OnDecrement.InvokeAsync(CurrentValue);
    }

    private bool IsAtMin()
    {
        if (CurrentValue == null || Min == null) return false;
        return ConvertToDecimal(CurrentValue) <= ConvertToDecimal(Min);
    }

    private bool IsAtMax()
    {
        if (CurrentValue == null || Max == null) return false;
        return ConvertToDecimal(CurrentValue) >= ConvertToDecimal(Max);
    }

    private TValue? ClampValue(TValue? value)
    {
        if (value == null) return value;

        decimal decimalValue = ConvertToDecimal(value);

        if (Min != null)
        {
            decimal minValue = ConvertToDecimal(Min);
            if (decimalValue < minValue)
                return Min;
        }

        if (Max != null)
        {
            decimal maxValue = ConvertToDecimal(Max);
            if (decimalValue > maxValue)
                return Max;
        }

        return value;
    }

    private decimal ConvertToDecimal(TValue value)
    {
        return Convert.ToDecimal(value, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);
    }

    private TValue? ConvertFromDecimal(decimal value)
    {
        try
        {
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(int))
                return (TValue)(object)(int)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(long))
                return (TValue)(object)(long)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(decimal))
                return (TValue)(object)value;
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(double))
                return (TValue)(object)(double)value;
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(float))
                return (TValue)(object)(float)value;
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(short))
                return (TValue)(object)(short)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(byte))
                return (TValue)(object)(byte)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(uint))
                return (TValue)(object)(uint)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(ulong))
                return (TValue)(object)(ulong)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(ushort))
                return (TValue)(object)(ushort)Math.Round(value);
            if (_underlyingType == typeof(sbyte))
                return (TValue)(object)(sbyte)Math.Round(value);

            return default;
        }
        catch
        {
            return default;
        }
    }

    private bool TryParseInput(string input, out TValue? result)
    {
        result = default;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
            return false;

        string normalized = NormalizeNumericInput(input);

        try
        {
            if (!decimal.TryParse(normalized, NumberStyles.Number, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, out decimal decimalValue))
                return false;

            if (!AllowNegative && decimalValue < 0)
                return false;

            result = ConvertFromDecimal(decimalValue);
            return result != null;
        }
        catch
        {
            return false;
        }
    }

    private string NormalizeNumericInput(string input)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(input))
            return string.Empty;

        StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
        List<int> separatorPositions = new List<int>();

        for (int i = 0; i < input.Length; i++)
        {
            char c = input[i];

            if (char.IsDigit(c))
            {
                result.Append(c);
            }
            else if (c == '-' && result.Length == 0)
            {
                result.Append(c);
            }
            else if (c == '.' || c == ',')
            {
                separatorPositions.Add(result.Length);
                result.Append('.');
            }
        }

        if (separatorPositions.Count <= 1)
        {
            return result.ToString();
        }

        string temp = result.ToString();
        result.Clear();

        int lastSeparatorIndex = separatorPositions[separatorPositions.Count - 1];
        int dotCount = 0;

        for (int i = 0; i < temp.Length; i++)
        {
            if (temp[i] == '.')
            {
                dotCount++;
                if (i == lastSeparatorIndex)
                {
                    result.Append('.');
                }
            }
            else
            {
                result.Append(temp[i]);
            }
        }

        return result.ToString();
    }

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out TValue? result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
        {
            result = default;
            return true;
        }

        if (TryParseInput(value, out result))
        {
            return true;
        }

        validationErrorMessage = $"'{value}' is not a valid number.";
        return false;
    }

    protected override void Dispose(bool disposing)
    {
        _accelerationCts?.Cancel();
        _accelerationCts?.Dispose();
        base.Dispose(disposing);
    }
}

=== Forms\Number\StepButtonPlacement.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

/// <summary>
/// Defines the placement of step buttons in numeric input components.
/// </summary>
public enum StepButtonPlacement
{
    /// <summary>
    /// Step buttons positioned on the left side of the input.
    /// </summary>
    Left,

    /// <summary>
    /// Step buttons positioned on the right side of the input (default).
    /// </summary>
    Right
}



=== Forms\Radio\BUIInputRadio.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms
@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<TValue, BUIInputRadio<TValue>, BUIInputRadioVariant>
@implements IRadioContainer
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasColor
@typeparam TValue

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

<CascadingValue Value="@((IRadioContainer)this)" IsFixed="true">
    @ChildContent
</CascadingValue>

@code {
    private readonly List<IRadioOption> _options = [];
    private readonly string _groupName = $"radio-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _preventKeyDefault;

    private readonly Type _elementType;

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Clearable { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string ClearText { get; set; } = "Clear";
    [Parameter] public string? CheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? UncheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RadioOrientation Orientation { get; set; } = RadioOrientation.Vertical;

    void IRadioContainer.RegisterOption(IRadioOption option)
    {
        if (_options.Contains(option)) { return; }
        _options.Add(option);
        StateHasChanged();
    }
    void IRadioContainer.UnregisterOption(IRadioOption option)
    {
        _options.Remove(option);
        StateHasChanged();
    }
    bool IRadioContainer.IsOptionSelected(object? value) => EqualityComparer<object>.Default.Equals(CurrentValue, value);
    async Task IRadioContainer.SelectOptionAsync(object? value) => await SelectValueAsync(value);
    Type IRadioContainer.ElementType => _elementType;

    public BUIInputRadio()
    {
        _elementType = typeof(TValue);
    }

    public override BUIInputRadioVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputRadioVariant.Default;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputRadioVariant, Func<BUIInputRadio<TValue>, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputRadioVariant, Func<BUIInputRadio<TValue>, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputRadioVariant.Default] = r => r.RenderDefault(),
        };

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out TValue result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;
        result = default!;
        return true;
    }

    private async Task SelectValueAsync(object? value)
    {
        if (IsDisabled) return;
        CurrentValue = value == null ? default! : (TValue)value;
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(CurrentValue);
    }

    private async Task ClearAsync()
    {
        if (IsDisabled || !Clearable) return;
        CurrentValue = default!;
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(CurrentValue);
    }

    private bool HasValue => CurrentValue != null && !EqualityComparer<TValue>.Default.Equals(CurrentValue, default);
    private bool ShowClearButton => Clearable && HasValue && !IsDisabled;

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        base.BuildComponentDataAttributes(dataAttributes);
        dataAttributes["data-orientation"] = Orientation.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderDefault() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-orientation="@Orientation.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">
    
            @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label))
            {
                <span class="bui-radio__label">
                    @Label
                    @if (Required)
                    {
                        <span class="bui-field__required">*</span>
                    }
                </span>
            }
    
            <div class="bui-radio__group" role="radiogroup">
                @foreach (IRadioOption option in _options)
                {
                    bool isSelected = ((IRadioContainer)this).IsOptionSelected(option.RawValue);
                    bool isOptionDisabled = IsDisabled || option.IsDisabled;
    
                    <div class="bui-radio__option @(isOptionDisabled ? "bui-radio__option--disabled" : "")"
                         role="radio"
                         aria-checked="@isSelected.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                         aria-disabled="@isOptionDisabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                         aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                         tabindex="@(isOptionDisabled ? -1 : 0)"
                         @onclick="() => HandleOptionClick(option, isOptionDisabled)"
                         @onkeydown="e => HandleOptionKeyDown(e, option, isOptionDisabled)"
                         @onkeydown:preventDefault="_preventKeyDefault">
    
                        <_BUICheckMark Checked="@isSelected"
                                       Mode="_BUICheckMark.CheckMarkMode.Radio"
                                       Size="Size"
                                       Disabled="isOptionDisabled"
                                       CheckedIcon="@CheckedIcon"
                                       UncheckedIcon="@UncheckedIcon" />
    
                        <span class="bui-radio__text">@option.Content</span>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
    
            @if (ShowClearButton)
            {
                <_BUIBtn OnClick="ClearClicked">
                    @ClearText
                </_BUIBtn>
            }
    
            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="TValue"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />
    
        </bui-component>
    };

    private async Task HandleOptionClick(IRadioOption option, bool isDisabled)
    {
        if (isDisabled) return;
        await SelectValueAsync(option.RawValue);
    }

    private async Task HandleOptionKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e, IRadioOption option, bool isDisabled)
    {
        _preventKeyDefault = e.Key == " ";
        if ((e.Key == " " || e.Key == "Enter") && !isDisabled)
        {
            await SelectValueAsync(option.RawValue);
        }
    }

    private async Task ClearClicked(MouseEventArgs e) => await ClearAsync();
}

=== Forms\Radio\RadioOption.cs ===

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public class RadioOption<TOption> : ComponentBase, IRadioOption, IDisposable
{
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [CascadingParameter] public IRadioContainer? Container { get; set; }

    RenderFragment IRadioOption.Content => ChildContent ?? (builder => { });
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    bool IRadioOption.IsDisabled => Disabled;
    object? IRadioOption.RawValue => Value;
    [Parameter, EditorRequired] public TOption? Value { get; set; }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        Container?.UnregisterOption(this);
    }

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        if (Container == null)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"{nameof(RadioOption<TOption>)} must be used inside a BUIInputRadio.");
        }

        ValidateOptionType();
        Container.RegisterOption(this);
    }

    private void ValidateOptionType()
    {
        Type optionType = typeof(TOption);
        Type expectedType = Container!.ElementType;

        Type underlyingExpected = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(expectedType) ?? expectedType;
        Type underlyingOption = Nullable.GetUnderlyingType(optionType) ?? optionType;

        if (!underlyingExpected.IsAssignableFrom(underlyingOption))
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException(
                $"RadioOption<{optionType.Name}> is not compatible with the radio's value type {expectedType.Name}.");
        }
    }
}

=== Forms\Switch\BUIInputSwitch.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<bool, BUIInputSwitch, BUIInputSwitchVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasDensity

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private string _inputId = $"bui-switch-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";

    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? IconInactive { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? IconActive { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public CssColor? TrackColorInactive { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public CssColor? TrackColorActive { get; set; }

    public override BUIInputSwitchVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputSwitchVariant.Default;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputSwitchVariant, Func<BUIInputSwitch, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputSwitchVariant, Func<BUIInputSwitch, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputSwitchVariant.Default] = c => c.RenderDefault()
        };

    protected bool IsChecked => CurrentValue;

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out bool result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;
        if (bool.TryParse(value, out bool boolResult))
        {
            result = boolResult;
            return true;
        }
        result = false;
        validationErrorMessage = $"Unable to parse '{value}' as boolean.";
        return false;
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderDefault() => __builder =>
    {
        <BUISwitch TValue="bool"
                   Value="@CurrentValue"
                   ValueChanged="@OnSwitchValueChanged"
                   OptionInactive="@false"
                   OptionActive="@true"
                   Disabled="@IsDisabled"
                   Size="@Size"
                   Density="@Density"
                   Label="@Label"
                   HelperText="@HelperText"
                   IconInactive="@IconInactive"
                   IconActive="@IconActive"
                   TrackColorInactive="@TrackColorInactive"
                   TrackColorActive="@TrackColorActive"
                   InputId="@_inputId"
                   AriaDescribedBy="@_helperTextId"
                   @attributes="ComputedAttributes" />

        <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="bool"
                         Id="@_helperTextId"
                         HelperText="@HelperText"
                         ShowValidation="@IsError"
                         EditContext="@EditContext"
                         For="@ValueExpression" />
    };

    private async Task OnSwitchValueChanged(bool newValue)
    {
        if (IsDisabled) return;

        CurrentValue = newValue;
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(CurrentValue);
    }
}

=== Forms\Text\BUIInputText.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<string, BUIInputText, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private string _inputId = $"bui-input-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _isFocused;
    private bool _isDirty;

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // Component-specific
    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool UpdateOnInput { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<string> OnInput { get; set; }

    private bool HasValue => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(CurrentValue);
    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || _isDirty;

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputText, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputText, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = i => i.RenderInput(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = i => i.RenderInput()
        };

    private RenderFragment RenderInput() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

            <div class="bui-input__wrapper">

                <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label" For="@_inputId" Required="@Required" />
                <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

                <input type="text"
                       id="@_inputId"
                       class="bui-input__field"
                       value="@CurrentValue"
                       @onchange="HandleChange"
                       @oninput="HandleInput"
                       @onfocus="HandleFocus"
                       @onblur="HandleBlur"
                       aria-label="@(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) ? Placeholder : null)"
                       aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                       aria-invalid="@IsError.ToString().ToLower()"
                       aria-required="@Required.ToString().ToLower()"
                       placeholder="@(IsFloated? Placeholder : null)"
                       disabled="@IsDisabled"
                       readonly="@ReadOnly"
                       required="@Required" />

                <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />
                <BUIInputLoading Loading="@Loading" LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="@Size" />

            </div>

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="string"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

        </bui-component>
    };

    private async Task HandleChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        CurrentValueAsString = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
    }

    private async Task HandleInput(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        string inputValue = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        _isDirty = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(inputValue);

        if (UpdateOnInput)
        {
            CurrentValueAsString = inputValue;
        }

        if (OnInput.HasDelegate)
        {
            await OnInput.InvokeAsync(inputValue);
        }
    }

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
        _isDirty = false;
    }

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out string? result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        result = value;
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;
        return true;
    }
}



=== Forms\Text\BUIInputText.razor.css ===




=== Forms\TextArea\JsInterop\TextAreaJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

public interface ITextAreaJsInterop
{
    ValueTask DisposeAutoResizeAsync(string textareaId);

    ValueTask InitializeAutoResizeAsync(ElementReference textarea, string textareaId);
}

public sealed class TextAreaJsInterop : ModuleJsInteropBase, ITextAreaJsInterop
{
    public TextAreaJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.TextArea)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAutoResizeAsync(string textareaId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("disposeAutoResize", textareaId);
    }

    public async ValueTask InitializeAutoResizeAsync(ElementReference textarea, string textareaId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("initializeAutoResize", textarea, textareaId);
    }
}



=== Forms\TextArea\BUIInputTextArea.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@inherits BUIInputComponentBase<string, BUIInputTextArea, BUIInputVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasLoading
@implements IHasDensity
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasPrefix
@implements IHasSuffix
@implements IInputFamilyComponent

@inject ITextAreaJsInterop TextAreaJs

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private ElementReference _textareaRef;
    private string _textareaId = $"bui-textarea-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private string _helperTextId = $"bui-helper-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private bool _jsInitialized;
    private bool _isFocused;
    private bool _isDirty;

    // IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasLoading
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;

    // IHasDensity
    [Parameter] public DensityEnum Density { get; set; } = DensityEnum.Standard;

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasPrefix
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? PrefixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasSuffix
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixColor { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? SuffixBackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // Component-specific
    [Parameter] public string? Label { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? HelperText { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int Rows { get; set; } = 3;
    [Parameter] public int? MaxLength { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool AutoResize { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public TextAreaResize Resize { get; set; } = TextAreaResize.Vertical;
    [Parameter] public bool UpdateOnInput { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<string> OnInput { get; set; }

    public override BUIInputVariant DefaultVariant => BUIInputVariant.Outlined;

    private bool HasValue => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(CurrentValue);
    private bool IsFloated => _isFocused || HasValue || _isDirty;

    protected override IReadOnlyDictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputTextArea, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } =
        new Dictionary<BUIInputVariant, Func<BUIInputTextArea, RenderFragment>>
        {
            [BUIInputVariant.Outlined] = t => t.RenderTextArea(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Filled] = t => t.RenderTextArea(),
            [BUIInputVariant.Standard] = t => t.RenderTextArea()
        };

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);

        if (firstRender && AutoResize)
        {
            await TextAreaJs.InitializeAutoResizeAsync(_textareaRef, _textareaId);
            _jsInitialized = true;
        }
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderTextArea() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-floated="@IsFloated.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       data-bui-resize="@Resize.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       data-bui-autoresize="@AutoResize.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

            <div class="bui-input__wrapper">

                <BUIInputOutline Label="@Label" For="@_textareaId" Required="@Required" />
                <BUIInputPrefix PrefixText="@PrefixText" PrefixIcon="@PrefixIcon" Size="@Size" />

                <textarea @ref="_textareaRef"
                          id="@_textareaId"
                          class="bui-input__field"
                          value="@CurrentValue"
                          rows="@Rows"
                          maxlength="@MaxLength"
                          placeholder="@(IsFloated? Placeholder : null)"
                          disabled="@IsDisabled"
                          readonly="@ReadOnly"
                          required="@Required"
                          @onchange="HandleChange"
                          @oninput="HandleInput"
                          @onfocus="HandleFocus"
                          @onblur="HandleBlur"
                          aria-label="@(string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(Label) ? Placeholder : null)"
                          aria-describedby="@_helperTextId"
                          aria-invalid="@IsError.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                          aria-required="@Required.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"></textarea>

                <BUIInputSuffix SuffixText="@SuffixText" SuffixIcon="@SuffixIcon" Size="@Size" />
                <BUIInputLoading Loading="@Loading" LoadingIndicatorVariant="@LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="@Size" />

            </div>

            <_BUIFieldHelper TValue="string"
                             Id="@_helperTextId"
                             HelperText="@HelperText"
                             ShowValidation="@IsError"
                             EditContext="@EditContext"
                             For="@ValueExpression" />

        </bui-component>
    };

    private void HandleFocus(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = true;
    }

    private void HandleBlur(FocusEventArgs e)
    {
        _isFocused = false;
        _isDirty = false;
    }

    private async Task HandleChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        CurrentValueAsString = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
    }

    private async Task HandleInput(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        string inputValue = e.Value?.ToString() ?? string.Empty;
        _isDirty = !string.IsNullOrEmpty(inputValue);

        if (UpdateOnInput)
        {
            CurrentValueAsString = inputValue;
        }

        if (OnInput.HasDelegate)
        {
            await OnInput.InvokeAsync(inputValue);
        }
    }

    protected override bool TryParseValueFromString(string? value, out string? result, out string validationErrorMessage)
    {
        result = value;
        validationErrorMessage = string.Empty;
        return true;
    }

    public override async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await TextAreaJs.DisposeAutoResizeAsync(_textareaId);
        }
        await base.DisposeAsync();
    }
}

=== Forms\TextArea\BUIInputTextAreaEnums.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms;

/// <summary>
/// Defines how the textarea can be resized by the user.
/// </summary>
public enum TextAreaResize
{
    /// <summary>
    /// User cannot resize the textarea.
    /// </summary>
    None,

    /// <summary>
    /// User can resize vertically only (default).
    /// </summary>
    Vertical,

    /// <summary>
    /// User can resize horizontally only.
    /// </summary>
    Horizontal,

    /// <summary>
    /// User can resize in both directions.
    /// </summary>
    Both
}



=== Forms\_Imports.razor ===

@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Forms



=== Generic\Badge\BUIBadge.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components
@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components

@inherits BUIVariantComponentBase<BUIBadge, BUIBadgeVariant>
@implements IHasSize
@implements IHasColor
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasShadow

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    /* ========= Public API ========= */

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Circular { get; set; }

    //  IHasSize
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;

    // IHasColor
    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    // IHasBackgroundColor
    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    // IHasBorder
    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    // IHasShadow
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    /* ========= Variant ========= */

    public override BUIBadgeVariant DefaultVariant => BUIBadgeVariant.Default;

    protected override Dictionary<BUIBadgeVariant, Func<BUIBadge, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } = new()
    {
        [BUIBadgeVariant.Default] = b => b.RenderBadge(),
    };

    /* ========= Base additions ========= */

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        if (ChildContent == null)
        {
            dataAttributes["data-bui-dot"] = "true";
        }

        if (Circular)
        {
            dataAttributes["data-bui-circular"] = "true";
        }
    }

    /* ========= Render ========= */

    private RenderFragment RenderBadge() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
            <span class="bui-badge">
                @if (ChildContent != null)
                {
                    @ChildContent
                }
            </span>
        </bui-component>
    };
}
