=== Generic\Tree\Abstractions\TreeStructure.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public sealed class TreeStructure<TNode, TItem>
    where TNode : TreeNodeBase<TItem, TNode>
{
    private readonly TreeNodeCache<TItem> _cache = new();
    private readonly HashSet<string> _expandedKeys = [];
    private readonly HashSet<string> _loadingKeys = [];
    private readonly Func<TreeNodeBuildContext<TItem>, TNode> _nodeFactory;
    private readonly Dictionary<string, TNode> _nodeMap = [];

    public TreeStructure(Func<TreeNodeBuildContext<TItem>, TNode> nodeFactory)
    {
        _nodeFactory = nodeFactory;
    }

    public IReadOnlySet<string> ExpandedKeys => _expandedKeys;
    public IReadOnlyDictionary<string, TNode> NodeMap => _nodeMap;
    public List<TNode> RootNodes { get; } = [];

    public void BuildFromItems(
        IEnumerable<TItem>? items,
        Func<TItem, string>? keySelector,
        Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? childrenSelector,
        Func<TItem, bool>? hasChildrenSelector,
        bool expandAll)
    {
        Clear();
        if (items == null) return;

        foreach (TItem item in items)
        {
            TNode node = BuildNodeFromItem(item, default, 0, keySelector, childrenSelector, hasChildrenSelector, expandAll);
            RootNodes.Add(node);
        }
    }

    public void Clear()
    {
        _nodeMap.Clear();
        RootNodes.Clear();
        _expandedKeys.Clear();
    }

    public void Collapse(string key) => _expandedKeys.Remove(key);

    public void CollapseAll() => _expandedKeys.Clear();

    public void Expand(string key)
    {
        _expandedKeys.Add(key);
    }

    public void ExpandAll()
    {
        foreach (TNode node in _nodeMap.Values.Where(n => n.HasChildren))
            _expandedKeys.Add(node.Key);
    }

    public void ExpandIfHasChildren(string key)
    {
        if (_nodeMap.TryGetValue(key, out TNode? node) && node.HasChildren)
            _expandedKeys.Add(key);
    }

    public TNode? GetNode(string key)
        => _nodeMap.TryGetValue(key, out TNode? node) ? node : null;

    public void InvalidateCache(string? key = null)
    {
        if (key != null)
            _cache.Invalidate(key);
        else
            _cache.InvalidateAll();
    }

    public bool IsExpanded(string key) => _expandedKeys.Contains(key);

    public bool IsLoading(string key) => _loadingKeys.Contains(key);

    public async Task<bool> LoadChildrenAsync(
        string key,
        Func<TItem, Task<IEnumerable<TItem>>>? loadFunc,
        Func<TItem, string>? keySelector,
        Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? childrenSelector,
        Func<TItem, bool>? hasChildrenSelector,
        Action onStateChanged)
    {
        if (loadFunc == null) return false;
        if (!_nodeMap.TryGetValue(key, out TNode? node) || node.Item == null) return false;
        if (node.ChildrenInternal.Count > 0) return true;

        _loadingKeys.Add(key);
        onStateChanged();

        try
        {
            IEnumerable<TItem> children;
            if (_cache.TryGet(key, out IEnumerable<TItem>? cached) && cached != null)
            {
                children = cached;
            }
            else
            {
                children = await loadFunc(node.Item);
                _cache.Set(key, children);
            }

            node.ChildrenInternal.Clear();
            foreach (TItem child in children)
            {
                TNode childNode = BuildNodeFromItem(
                    child, node, node.Depth + 1,
                    keySelector, childrenSelector, hasChildrenSelector, false);
                node.ChildrenInternal.Add(childNode);
            }
            node.HasChildrenFlag = node.ChildrenInternal.Count > 0;
            return true;
        }
        finally
        {
            _loadingKeys.Remove(key);
            onStateChanged();
        }
    }

    public void RegisterNode(TNode node)
    {
        _nodeMap[node.Key] = node;
    }

    public void SetExpandedKeys(IEnumerable<string>? keys)
    {
        _expandedKeys.Clear();
        if (keys != null)
        {
            foreach (string key in keys)
                _expandedKeys.Add(key);
        }
    }

    public void Toggle(string key)
    {
        if (IsExpanded(key))
            Collapse(key);
        else
            Expand(key);
    }

    private TNode BuildNodeFromItem(
        TItem item,
        TNode? parent,
        int depth,
        Func<TItem, string>? keySelector,
        Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? childrenSelector,
        Func<TItem, bool>? hasChildrenSelector,
        bool expandAll)
    {
        string key = keySelector?.Invoke(item) ?? $"item-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
        IEnumerable<TItem>? children = childrenSelector?.Invoke(item);
        bool hasChildren = hasChildrenSelector?.Invoke(item) ?? children?.Any() ?? false;

        TreeNodeBuildContext<TItem> context = new()
        {
            Key = key,
            Item = item,
            Depth = depth,
            Parent = parent,
            HasChildren = hasChildren
        };

        TNode node = _nodeFactory(context);
        node.HasChildrenFlag = hasChildren;
        _nodeMap[key] = node;

        if (expandAll && hasChildren)
            _expandedKeys.Add(key);

        if (children != null)
        {
            foreach (TItem child in children)
            {
                TNode childNode = BuildNodeFromItem(
                    child, node, depth + 1,
                    keySelector, childrenSelector, hasChildrenSelector, expandAll);
                node.ChildrenInternal.Add(childNode);
            }
        }

        return node;
    }
}



=== Generic\Tree\TreeMenu\BUITreeMenu.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Utilities
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Routing

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components

@typeparam TItem
@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IHasSize
@implements IDisposable

@inject NavigationManager NavigationManager

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

<bui-component @attributes="@ComputedAttributes">
    @if (_isDeclarativeMode)
    {
        <CascadingValue Value="@((ITreeNodeRegistry<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>)_registry)" Name="TreeNodeRegistry">
            @ChildContent
        </CascadingValue>
    }

    @if (_structureBuilt)
    {
        @if (_isOpen && ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout)
        {
            <div class="bui-tree-menu__overlay" @onclick="CloseAllMenus" @onclick:stopPropagation="true"></div>
        }

        <nav class="bui-tree-menu__nav" role="menubar" aria-orientation="@Orientation.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">
            @foreach (TreeMenuNode<TItem> node in _tree.RootNodes)
            {
                @RenderNode(node)
            }
        </nav>
    }
</bui-component>

@code {
    private readonly TreeNodeRegistry<TreeMenuNodeRegistration> _registry = new();
    private readonly DelayedActionHandler _hoverDelayHandler = new();
    private TreeStructure<TreeMenuNode<TItem>, TItem> _tree = null!;
    private bool _isDeclarativeMode;
    private bool _structureBuilt;
    private bool _isOpen;
    private string _currentUri = string.Empty;

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public IEnumerable<TItem>? Items { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, string>? KeySelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? ChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, bool>? HasChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, Task<IEnumerable<TItem>>>? OnLoadChildren { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment<TreeMenuNode<TItem>>? NodeTemplate { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public TreeNodeCache<TItem>? Cache { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public HashSet<string>? ExpandedKeys { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<HashSet<string>> ExpandedKeysChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ExpandAll { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public TreeMenuOrientation Orientation { get; set; } = TreeMenuOrientation.Vertical;
    [Parameter] public TreeMenuTrigger Trigger { get; set; } = TreeMenuTrigger.Click;
    [Parameter] public TreeMenuExpandMode ExpandMode { get; set; } = TreeMenuExpandMode.Inline;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public bool Collapsible { get; set; } = true;

    [Parameter] public int HoverOpenDelay { get; set; } = 150;
    [Parameter] public int HoverCloseDelay { get; set; } = 300;

    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeMenuNode<TItem>>> OnNodeClick { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<string> OnNavigate { get; set; }

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        dataAttributes["data-bui-orientation"] = Orientation.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-trigger"] = Trigger.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-expand-mode"] = ExpandMode.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        _tree = new TreeStructure<TreeMenuNode<TItem>, TItem>(CreateNodeFromContext);
        _currentUri = NavigationManager.Uri;
        NavigationManager.LocationChanged += OnLocationChanged;
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();

        _isDeclarativeMode = ChildContent != null && Items == null;

        if (ExpandedKeys != null)
        {
            _tree.SetExpandedKeys(ExpandedKeys);
        }

        if (!_isDeclarativeMode && Items != null)
        {
            _tree.BuildFromItems(Items, KeySelector, ChildrenSelector, HasChildrenSelector, ExpandAll);
            _structureBuilt = true;
        }
    }

    protected override void OnAfterRender(bool firstRender)
    {
        base.OnAfterRender(firstRender);

        if (firstRender && _isDeclarativeMode && !_structureBuilt)
        {
            BuildFromDeclarativeRegistrations();
            _structureBuilt = true;
            StateHasChanged();
        }
    }

    private TreeMenuNode<TItem> CreateNodeFromContext(TreeNodeBuildContext<TItem> context)
    {
        return new TreeMenuNode<TItem>
        {
            Key = context.Key,
            Item = context.Item,
            Text = context.Text,
            Icon = context.Icon,
            IsDisabled = context.IsDisabled,
            Depth = context.Depth,
            ParentNode = context.Parent as TreeMenuNode<TItem>,
            CustomContent = context.CustomContent,
            AdditionalData = context.AdditionalData,
            Navigation = new NavigationInfo(),
            OnClick = default
        };
    }

    private TreeMenuNode<TItem> CreateNodeFromRegistration(TreeMenuNodeRegistration reg, TreeMenuNode<TItem>? parent, int depth, bool hasChildren)
    {
        return new TreeMenuNode<TItem>
        {
            Key = reg.Key,
            Item = default,
            Text = reg.Text,
            Icon = reg.Icon,
            IsDisabled = reg.IsDisabled,
            Depth = depth,
            ParentNode = parent,
            CustomContent = reg.NodeContent,
            AdditionalData = reg.Data,
            Navigation = new NavigationInfo
            {
                Href = reg.Href,
                Target = reg.Target,
                Match = reg.Match
            },
            OnClick = reg.OnClick
        };
    }

    private void BuildFromDeclarativeRegistrations()
    {
        IReadOnlyList<TreeMenuNodeRegistration> registrations = _registry.GetRegistrations();
        _registry.Clear();

        Dictionary<string, List<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>> childrenByParent = new();

        foreach (TreeMenuNodeRegistration reg in registrations)
        {
            string parentKey = reg.ParentKey ?? string.Empty;

            if (!childrenByParent.ContainsKey(parentKey))
            {
                childrenByParent[parentKey] = new List<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>();
            }
            childrenByParent[parentKey].Add(reg);
        }

        if (childrenByParent.TryGetValue(string.Empty, out List<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>? roots))
        {
            foreach (TreeMenuNodeRegistration reg in roots)
            {
                TreeMenuNode<TItem> node = BuildNodeFromRegistration(reg, null, 0, childrenByParent);
                _tree.RootNodes.Add(node);
            }
        }
    }

    private TreeMenuNode<TItem> BuildNodeFromRegistration(
        TreeMenuNodeRegistration reg,
        TreeMenuNode<TItem>? parent,
        int depth,
        Dictionary<string, List<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>> childrenByParent)
    {
        bool hasChildren = childrenByParent.ContainsKey(reg.Key);
        TreeMenuNode<TItem> node = CreateNodeFromRegistration(reg, parent, depth, hasChildren);
        node.HasChildrenFlag = hasChildren;

        _tree.RegisterNode(node);

        if (reg.InitiallyExpanded || ExpandAll)
        {
            _tree.Expand(node.Key);
        }

        if (childrenByParent.TryGetValue(reg.Key, out List<TreeMenuNodeRegistration>? children))
        {
            foreach (TreeMenuNodeRegistration childReg in children)
            {
                TreeMenuNode<TItem> childNode = BuildNodeFromRegistration(childReg, node, depth + 1, childrenByParent);
                node.ChildrenInternal.Add(childNode);
            }
        }

        return node;
    }

    private void OnLocationChanged(object? sender, LocationChangedEventArgs e)
    {
        _currentUri = e.Location;

        if (ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout)
        {
            CloseAllMenus();
        }

        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderNode(TreeMenuNode<TItem> node) => __builder =>
    {
        bool isExpanded = _tree.IsExpanded(node.Key);
        bool isLoading = _tree.IsLoading(node.Key);
        bool isActive = IsActive(node.Navigation.Href);
        bool hasChildren = node.HasChildren;
        bool isFlyout = ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout;
        bool isHoverTrigger = Trigger == TreeMenuTrigger.Hover;

        <div class="bui-tree-menu__item @(node.IsDisabled ? "bui-tree-menu__item--disabled" : "") @(isActive ? "bui-tree-menu__item--active" : "") @(isExpanded ? "bui-tree-menu__item--expanded" : "")"
             role="none"
             data-depth="@node.Depth"
             @onmouseenter="@(isHoverTrigger && hasChildren ? () => HandleHoverEnter(node.Key) : null)"
             @onmouseleave="@(isHoverTrigger && hasChildren && isFlyout ? () => HandleHoverLeave(node.Key) : null)">

            @if (node.Navigation.HasNavigation && !hasChildren)
            {
                <a class="bui-tree-menu__link"
                   href="@node.Navigation.Href"
                   target="@node.Navigation.Target"
                   role="menuitem"
                   aria-disabled="@node.IsDisabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                   @onclick="() => HandleItemClickAsync(node)"
                   @onclick:preventDefault="@node.IsDisabled">
                    @RenderItemContent(node, hasChildren, isExpanded, isLoading)
                </a>
            }
            else
            {
                <button type="button"
                        class="bui-tree-menu__button"
                        role="menuitem"
                        aria-haspopup="@(hasChildren ? "true" : null)"
                        aria-expanded="@(hasChildren? isExpanded.ToString().ToLowerInvariant() : null)"
                        aria-disabled="@node.IsDisabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                        disabled="@node.IsDisabled"
                        @onclick="() => HandleItemClickAsync(node)">
                    @RenderItemContent(node, hasChildren, isExpanded, isLoading)
                </button>
            }

            @if (hasChildren && isExpanded)
            {
                <div class="bui-tree-menu__submenu @(isFlyout ? "bui-tree-menu__submenu--flyout" : "bui-tree-menu__submenu--inline")"
                     role="menu"
                     @onmouseenter="@(isHoverTrigger? HandleHoverEnterSubmenu : null)"
                     @onmouseleave="@(isHoverTrigger && isFlyout ? () => HandleHoverLeave(node.Key) : null)">
                    @foreach (TreeMenuNode<TItem> child in node.ChildrenInternal)
                    {
                        @RenderNode(child)
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    };

    private RenderFragment RenderItemContent(TreeMenuNode<TItem> node, bool hasChildren, bool isExpanded, bool isLoading) => __builder =>
    {
        @if (_isDeclarativeMode && node.CustomContent != null)
        {
            @node.CustomContent
        }
        else if (!_isDeclarativeMode && NodeTemplate != null)
        {
            @NodeTemplate(node)
        }
        else
        {
            @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(node.Icon))
            {
                <BUISvgIcon Icon="@node.Icon" Size="Size" class="bui-tree-menu__icon" />
            }
            <span class="bui-tree-menu__text">@(node.Text ?? node.Item?.ToString() ?? node.Key)</span>
        }

        @if (hasChildren)
        {
            <_BUIAddon Icon="@GetExpandIcon()"
                       IconRotation="@(isExpanded ? 90 : 0)"
                       Loading="@isLoading"
                       LoadingIndicatorVariant="BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.Spinner"
                       Size="Size" />
        }
    };

    private string GetExpandIcon()
    {
        if (Orientation == TreeMenuOrientation.Horizontal && ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout)
            return BUIIcons.UI.ChevronDown;
        return BUIIcons.UI.ChevronRight;
    }

    private async Task HandleItemClickAsync(TreeMenuNode<TItem> node)
    {
        if (node.IsDisabled) return;

        if (node.OnClick.HasDelegate)
        {
            await node.OnClick.InvokeAsync();
        }

        await OnNodeClick.InvokeAsync(new TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeMenuNode<TItem>>
        {
            Node = node,
            Key = node.Key,
            Depth = node.Depth,
            IsExpanded = _tree.IsExpanded(node.Key)
        });

        if (node.HasChildren)
        {
            await ToggleExpandAsync(node.Key);
        }
        else if (node.Navigation.HasNavigation)
        {
            if (OnNavigate.HasDelegate)
            {
                await OnNavigate.InvokeAsync(node.Navigation.Href);
            }

            if (ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout)
            {
                CloseAllMenus();
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task ToggleExpandAsync(string key)
    {
        if (_tree.IsExpanded(key))
        {
            await HandleCollapseAsync(key);
        }
        else
        {
            await HandleExpandAsync(key);
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleExpandAsync(string key)
    {
        TreeMenuNode<TItem>? node = _tree.GetNode(key);
        if (node == null) return;

        if (ExpandMode == TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout)
        {
            CollapseSiblingsOf(node);
        }
        else if (!Collapsible)
        {
            _tree.CollapseAll();
        }

        if (OnLoadChildren != null)
        {
            await _tree.LoadChildrenAsync(key, OnLoadChildren, KeySelector, ChildrenSelector, HasChildrenSelector, StateHasChanged);
        }

        _tree.Expand(key);
        _isOpen = true;
        await NotifyExpandedKeysChangedAsync();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async Task HandleCollapseAsync(string key)
    {
        _tree.Collapse(key);

        if (!_tree.ExpandedKeys.Any())
        {
            _isOpen = false;
        }

        await NotifyExpandedKeysChangedAsync();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void CollapseSiblingsOf(TreeMenuNode<TItem> node)
    {
        IEnumerable<TreeMenuNode<TItem>> siblings = node.ParentNode != null
            ? node.ParentNode.ChildrenInternal
            : _tree.RootNodes;

        foreach (TreeMenuNode<TItem> sibling in siblings)
        {
            if (sibling.Key != node.Key)
            {
                CollapseNodeAndDescendants(sibling);
            }
        }
    }

    private void CollapseNodeAndDescendants(TreeMenuNode<TItem> node)
    {
        _tree.Collapse(node.Key);
        foreach (TreeMenuNode<TItem> child in node.ChildrenInternal)
        {
            CollapseNodeAndDescendants(child);
        }
    }

    private void CloseAllMenus()
    {
        _hoverDelayHandler.Cancel();
        _tree.CollapseAll();
        _isOpen = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async Task HandleHoverEnter(string key)
    {
        if (Trigger != TreeMenuTrigger.Hover) return;

        TreeMenuNode<TItem>? node = _tree.GetNode(key);
        if (node == null || !node.HasChildren) return;

        _hoverDelayHandler.Cancel();
        await _hoverDelayHandler.ExecuteWithDelayAsync(async () =>
        {
            await HandleExpandAsync(key);
        }, TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(HoverOpenDelay));
    }

    private async Task HandleHoverLeave(string key)
    {
        if (Trigger != TreeMenuTrigger.Hover) return;
        if (ExpandMode != TreeMenuExpandMode.Flyout) return;

        await _hoverDelayHandler.ExecuteWithDelayAsync(async () =>
        {
            TreeMenuNode<TItem>? node = _tree.GetNode(key);
            if (node != null)
            {
                CollapseNodeAndDescendants(node);
            }

            if (!_tree.ExpandedKeys.Any())
            {
                _isOpen = false;
            }

            StateHasChanged();
            await Task.CompletedTask;
        }, TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(HoverCloseDelay));
    }

    private void HandleHoverEnterSubmenu()
    {
        if (Trigger != TreeMenuTrigger.Hover) return;
        _hoverDelayHandler.Cancel();
    }

    private bool IsActive(string? href)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(href)) return false;

        string currentPath = NavigationManager.ToBaseRelativePath(_currentUri);
        string targetPath = NavigationManager.ToBaseRelativePath(NavigationManager.ToAbsoluteUri(href).AbsoluteUri);

        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(currentPath)) currentPath = "/";
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(targetPath)) targetPath = "/";

        TreeMenuNode<TItem>? node = _tree.NodeMap.Values.FirstOrDefault(n => n.Navigation.Href == href);
        NavLinkMatch match = node?.Navigation.Match ?? NavLinkMatch.Prefix;

        if (match == NavLinkMatch.All)
            return string.Equals(currentPath, targetPath, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);

        return currentPath.StartsWith(targetPath, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase);
    }

    private async Task NotifyExpandedKeysChangedAsync()
    {
        if (ExpandedKeysChanged.HasDelegate)
        {
            await ExpandedKeysChanged.InvokeAsync(new HashSet<string>(_tree.ExpandedKeys));
        }
    }

    public void ExpandAllNodes()
    {
        _tree.ExpandAll();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void CollapseAllNodes()
    {
        _tree.CollapseAll();
        _isOpen = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void InvalidateCache(string? key = null) => _tree.InvalidateCache(key);

    public TreeMenuNode<TItem>? GetNode(string key) => _tree.GetNode(key);

    public void Dispose()
    {
        NavigationManager.LocationChanged -= OnLocationChanged;
        _hoverDelayHandler.Dispose();
    }
}

    padding-left: calc(var(--_tree-menu-item-padding-x) + var(--_tree-menu-indent));
}

bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"][data-bui-expand-mode="inline"] .bui-tree-menu__item[data-depth="2"] > .bui-tree-menu__link,
bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"][data-bui-expand-mode="inline"] .bui-tree-menu__item[data-depth="2"] > .bui-tree-menu__button {
    padding-left: calc(var(--_tree-menu-item-padding-x) + var(--_tree-menu-indent) * 2);
}

bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"][data-bui-expand-mode="inline"] .bui-tree-menu__item[data-depth="3"] > .bui-tree-menu__link,
bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"][data-bui-expand-mode="inline"] .bui-tree-menu__item[data-depth="3"] > .bui-tree-menu__button {
    padding-left: calc(var(--_tree-menu-item-padding-x) + var(--_tree-menu-indent) * 3);
}

bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"] .bui-tree-menu__link:focus-visible,
bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"] .bui-tree-menu__button:focus-visible {
    outline: var(--bui-highlight-outline);
    outline-offset: var(--bui-highlight-outline-offset);
}

bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"][data-bui-orientation="horizontal"] .bui-tree-menu__link,

    white-space: nowrap;
}

bui-component[data-bui-component="tree-menu"] .bui-tree-menu__submenu--flyout .bui-tree-menu__button {

}

=== Generic\Tree\TreeMenu\TreeMenuNode.cs ===

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public sealed class TreeMenuNode<TItem> : TreeNodeBase<TItem, TreeMenuNode<TItem>>

=== Generic\Tree\TreeSelector\BUITreeSelector.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components

@typeparam TItem
@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IHasSize

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

<bui-component @attributes="@ComputedAttributes">
    @if (_isDeclarativeMode)
    {
        <CascadingValue Value="@((ITreeNodeRegistry<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration>)_registry)" Name="TreeNodeRegistry">
            @ChildContent
        </CascadingValue>
    }

    @if (_structureBuilt)
    {
        <div class="bui-tree-selector__container" role="tree" aria-multiselectable="@(SelectionMode == TreeSelectionMode.Multiple)">
            @foreach (TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node in _tree.RootNodes)
            {
                @RenderNode(node)
            }
        </div>
    }
</bui-component>

@code {
    private readonly TreeNodeRegistry<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration> _registry = new();
    private TreeStructure<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>, TItem> _tree = null!;
    private readonly HashSet<string> _selectedKeysInternal = [];
    private bool _isDeclarativeMode;
    private bool _structureBuilt;
    private bool _preventKeyDefault;

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public IEnumerable<TItem>? Items { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, string>? KeySelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, IEnumerable<TItem>?>? ChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, bool>? HasChildrenSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, Task<IEnumerable<TItem>>>? OnLoadChildren { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>? NodeTemplate { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public Func<TItem, string>? DisplayTextSelector { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public TreeNodeCache<TItem>? Cache { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public HashSet<string>? ExpandedKeys { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<HashSet<string>> ExpandedKeysChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ExpandAll { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public HashSet<string>? SelectedKeys { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<HashSet<string>> SelectedKeysChanged { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public TreeSelectionMode SelectionMode { get; set; } = TreeSelectionMode.Single;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public bool ShowCheckboxes { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool AnimateExpand { get; set; } = true;

    [Parameter] public string ExpandIcon { get; set; } = BUIIcons.UI.ChevronRight;
    [Parameter] public string CollapseIcon { get; set; } = BUIIcons.UI.ChevronDown;

    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>> OnNodeClick { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>> OnNodeExpand { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>> OnNodeCollapse { get; set; }

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        dataAttributes["data-bui-selection-mode"] = SelectionMode.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-show-checkboxes"] = ShowCheckboxes.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        _tree = new TreeStructure<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>, TItem>(CreateNodeFromContext);
    }

    protected override void OnParametersSet()
    {
        base.OnParametersSet();

        _isDeclarativeMode = ChildContent != null && Items == null;

        if (ExpandedKeys != null)
        {
            _tree.SetExpandedKeys(ExpandedKeys);
        }

        if (SelectedKeys != null)
        {
            _selectedKeysInternal.Clear();
            foreach (string key in SelectedKeys)
            {
                _selectedKeysInternal.Add(key);
            }
        }

        if (!_isDeclarativeMode && Items != null)
        {
            _tree.BuildFromItems(Items, KeySelector, ChildrenSelector, HasChildrenSelector, ExpandAll);
            _structureBuilt = true;
        }
    }

    protected override void OnAfterRender(bool firstRender)
    {
        base.OnAfterRender(firstRender);

        if (firstRender && _isDeclarativeMode && !_structureBuilt)
        {
            BuildFromDeclarativeRegistrations();
            _structureBuilt = true;
            StateHasChanged();
        }
    }

    private TreeSelectionNode<TItem> CreateNodeFromContext(TreeNodeBuildContext<TItem> context)
    {
        return new TreeSelectionNode<TItem>
        {
            Key = context.Key,
            Item = context.Item,
            Text = context.Text,
            Icon = context.Icon,
            IsDisabled = context.IsDisabled,
            Depth = context.Depth,
            ParentNode = context.Parent as TreeSelectionNode<TItem>,
            CustomContent = context.CustomContent,
            AdditionalData = context.AdditionalData
        };
    }

    private TreeSelectionNode<TItem> CreateNodeFromRegistration(TreeSelectionNodeRegistration reg, TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? parent, int depth)
    {
        return new TreeSelectionNode<TItem>
        {
            Key = reg.Key,
            Item = default,
            Text = reg.Text,
            Icon = reg.Icon,
            IsDisabled = reg.IsDisabled,
            Depth = depth,
            ParentNode = parent,
            CustomContent = reg.NodeContent,
            AdditionalData = reg.Data
        };
    }

    private void BuildFromDeclarativeRegistrations()
    {
        _tree.Clear();

        IReadOnlyList<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration> registrations = _registry.GetRegistrations();
        _registry.Clear();

        Dictionary<string, List<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration>> childrenByParent = registrations
            .GroupBy(r => r.ParentKey ?? string.Empty)
            .ToDictionary(g => g.Key, g => g.ToList());

        if (childrenByParent.TryGetValue(string.Empty, out List<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration>? roots))
        {
            foreach (TreeSelectionNodeRegistration reg in roots)
            {
                TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node = BuildNodeFromRegistration(reg, null, 0, childrenByParent);
                _tree.RootNodes.Add(node);
            }
        }
    }

    private TreeSelectionNode<TItem> BuildNodeFromRegistration(
        TreeSelectionNodeRegistration reg,
        TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? parent,
        int depth,
        Dictionary<string, List<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration>> childrenByParent)
    {
        bool hasChildren = childrenByParent.ContainsKey(reg.Key);
        TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node = CreateNodeFromRegistration(reg, parent, depth);
        node.HasChildrenFlag = hasChildren;

        _tree.RegisterNode(node);

        if (reg.InitiallyExpanded || ExpandAll)
        {
            _tree.Expand(node.Key);
        }

        if (reg.IsSelected)
        {
            _selectedKeysInternal.Add(node.Key);
        }

        if (childrenByParent.TryGetValue(reg.Key, out List<TreeSelectionNodeRegistration>? children))
        {
            foreach (TreeSelectionNodeRegistration childReg in children)
            {
                TreeSelectionNode<TItem> childNode = BuildNodeFromRegistration(childReg, node, depth + 1, childrenByParent);
                node.ChildrenInternal.Add(childNode);
            }
        }

        return node;
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderNode(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node) => __builder =>
    {
        bool isExpanded = _tree.IsExpanded(node.Key);
        bool isLoading = _tree.IsLoading(node.Key);
        bool isSelected = IsSelected(node.Key);

        <div class="bui-tree-selector__node @(node.IsDisabled ? "bui-tree-selector__node--disabled" : "") @(isSelected ? "bui-tree-selector__node--selected" : "")"
             role="treeitem"
             aria-expanded="@(node.HasChildren? isExpanded.ToString().ToLowerInvariant() : null)"
             aria-selected="@isSelected.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
             aria-disabled="@node.IsDisabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
             data-depth="@node.Depth"
             data-key="@node.Key">

            <div class="bui-tree-selector__node-content"
                 style="padding-left: calc(@(node.Depth) * var(--bui-tree-selector-indent, 1.5rem))"
                 tabindex="@(node.IsDisabled ? -1 : 0)"
                 @onclick="() => HandleNodeClickAsync(node)"
                 @onclick:stopPropagation="true"
                 @onkeydown="e => HandleNodeKeyDown(e, node)"
                 @onkeydown:preventDefault="_preventKeyDefault">

                @if (node.HasChildren)
                {
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@ExpandIcon"
                             IconRotation="@(isExpanded ? 90 : 0)"
                             Loading="@isLoading"
                             Disabled="node.IsDisabled"
                             AriaLabel="@(isExpanded ? "Collapse" : "Expand")"
                             OnClick="() => ToggleExpandAsync(node)"
                             OnClickStopPropagation="true"
                             tabindex="-1"
                             class="bui-tree-selector__expander" />
                }
                else
                {
                    <span class="bui-tree-selector__expander-placeholder"></span>
                }

                @if (ShowCheckboxes)
                {
                    <_BUICheckMark Checked="@isSelected"
                                   Size="Size"
                                   Disabled="node.IsDisabled" />
                }

                <div class="bui-tree-selector__node-label">
                    @if (_isDeclarativeMode && node.CustomContent != null)
                    {
                        @node.CustomContent
                    }
                    else if (!_isDeclarativeMode && NodeTemplate != null)
                    {
                        @NodeTemplate(node)
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        @RenderDefaultContent(node)
                    }
                </div>
            </div>

            @if (node.HasChildren && isExpanded)
            {
                <div class="bui-tree-selector__children @(AnimateExpand ? "bui-tree-selector__children--animated" : "")"
                     role="group">
                    @foreach (TreeSelectionNode<TItem> child in node.ChildrenInternal)
                    {
                        @RenderNode(child)
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    };

    private RenderFragment RenderDefaultContent(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node) => __builder =>
    {
        @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(node.Icon))
        {
            <BUISvgIcon Icon="@node.Icon" Size="Size" class="bui-tree-selector__node-icon" />
        }
        <span class="bui-tree-selector__node-text">@GetNodeDisplayText(node)</span>
    };

    private string GetNodeDisplayText(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node)
    {
        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(node.Text))
            return node.Text;

        if (node.Item != null && DisplayTextSelector != null)
            return DisplayTextSelector(node.Item);

        return node.Key;
    }

    public bool IsSelected(string key) => _selectedKeysInternal.Contains(key);

    private async Task HandleNodeClickAsync(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node)
    {
        if (node.IsDisabled) return;

        await OnNodeClick.InvokeAsync(new TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>
        {
            Node = node,
            Key = node.Key,
            Depth = node.Depth,
            IsExpanded = _tree.IsExpanded(node.Key)
        });

        await ToggleSelectionAsync(node.Key);
    }

    private async Task HandleNodeKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e, TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node)
    {
        switch (e.Key)
        {
            case " ":
            case "Enter":
                _preventKeyDefault = true;
                if (!node.IsDisabled)
                {
                    await ToggleSelectionAsync(node.Key);
                }
                break;

            case "ArrowRight":
                _preventKeyDefault = true;
                if (node.HasChildren)
                {
                    if (!_tree.IsExpanded(node.Key))
                    {
                        await ToggleExpandAsync(node);
                    }
                }
                break;

            case "ArrowLeft":
                _preventKeyDefault = true;
                if (node.HasChildren && _tree.IsExpanded(node.Key))
                {
                    await ToggleExpandAsync(node);
                }
                break;

            case "ArrowDown":
                _preventKeyDefault = true;
                break;

            case "ArrowUp":
                _preventKeyDefault = true;
                break;

            default:
                _preventKeyDefault = false;
                break;
        }
    }

    private async Task ToggleExpandAsync(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node)
    {
        if (_tree.IsExpanded(node.Key))
        {
            _tree.Collapse(node.Key);
            await OnNodeCollapse.InvokeAsync(CreateEventArgs(node, false));
        }
        else
        {
            if (OnLoadChildren != null)
            {
                await _tree.LoadChildrenAsync(node.Key, OnLoadChildren, KeySelector, ChildrenSelector, HasChildrenSelector, StateHasChanged);
            }
            _tree.Expand(node.Key);
            await OnNodeExpand.InvokeAsync(CreateEventArgs(node, true));
        }

        await NotifyExpandedKeysChangedAsync();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async Task ToggleSelectionAsync(string key)
    {
        TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? node = _tree.GetNode(key);
        if (node?.IsDisabled == true) return;

        if (SelectionMode == TreeSelectionMode.Single)
        {
            bool wasSelected = IsSelected(key);
            _selectedKeysInternal.Clear();
            if (!wasSelected)
            {
                _selectedKeysInternal.Add(key);
            }
        }
        else
        {
            if (IsSelected(key))
            {
                _selectedKeysInternal.Remove(key);
            }
            else
            {
                _selectedKeysInternal.Add(key);
            }
        }

        await NotifySelectedKeysChangedAsync();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private TreeNodeEventArgs<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>> CreateEventArgs(TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node, bool isExpanded) => new()
    {
        Node = node,
        Key = node.Key,
        Depth = node.Depth,
        IsExpanded = isExpanded
    };

    private async Task NotifyExpandedKeysChangedAsync()
    {
        if (ExpandedKeysChanged.HasDelegate)
        {
            await ExpandedKeysChanged.InvokeAsync(new HashSet<string>(_tree.ExpandedKeys));
        }
    }

    private async Task NotifySelectedKeysChangedAsync()
    {
        if (SelectedKeysChanged.HasDelegate)
        {
            await SelectedKeysChanged.InvokeAsync(new HashSet<string>(_selectedKeysInternal));
        }
    }

    public void ExpandAllNodes()
    {
        _tree.ExpandAll();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void CollapseAllNodes()
    {
        _tree.CollapseAll();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void SelectAll()
    {
        if (SelectionMode != TreeSelectionMode.Multiple) return;

        foreach (TreeSelectionNode<TItem> node in _tree.NodeMap.Values.Where(n => !n.IsDisabled))
        {
            _selectedKeysInternal.Add(node.Key);
        }
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void ClearSelection()
    {
        _selectedKeysInternal.Clear();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    public void InvalidateCache(string? key = null) => _tree.InvalidateCache(key);

    public TreeSelectionNode<TItem>? GetNode(string key) => _tree.GetNode(key);

    public IReadOnlyCollection<TreeSelectionNode<TItem>> GetSelectedNodes()
        => _selectedKeysInternal.Select(k => _tree.GetNode(k)).Where(n => n != null).ToList()!;
}

=== Generic\Tree\TreeSelector\TreeSelectionNode.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Components.Selection;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public sealed class TreeSelectionNode<TItem> : TreeNodeBase<TItem, TreeSelectionNode<TItem>>, IHierarchicalSelectionOption
{
    IReadOnlyList<IHierarchicalSelectionOption> IHierarchicalSelectionOption.Children =>
        ChildrenInternal.Cast<IHierarchicalSelectionOption>().ToList();

    RenderFragment? ISelectionOption.Content => CustomContent;
    int IHierarchicalSelectionOption.Depth => Depth;
    string ISelectionOption.DisplayText => Text ?? Item?.ToString() ?? Key;
    bool ISelectionOption.IsDisabled => IsDisabled;
    string IHierarchicalSelectionOption.Key => Key;
    IHierarchicalSelectionOption? IHierarchicalSelectionOption.Parent => ParentNode;
    object? ISelectionOption.Value => Item;
}

=== Internal\_BUIAddon.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Internal

<div class="@ComputedClass" style="@ComputedStyle" @attributes="FilteredAttributes">
    @if (Loading)
    {
        <BUILoadingIndicator Variant="LoadingIndicatorVariant" Size="Size" />
    }
    else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Icon))
    {
        <BUISvgIcon Icon="@Icon" Size="Size" style="@IconStyle" />
    }
    @ChildContent
</div>

@code {
    [Parameter] public string? Icon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int IconRotation { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter(CaptureUnmatchedValues = true)]
    public Dictionary<string, object>? AdditionalAttributes { get; set; }

    private string? IconStyle => IconRotation != 0
        ? $"transform: rotate({IconRotation}deg); transition: transform 200ms ease;"
        : null;

    private string ComputedClass
    {
        get
        {
            List<string> classes = ["_bui-addon"];

            if (AdditionalAttributes?.TryGetValue("class", out object? extraClass) == true)
                classes.Add(extraClass.ToString() ?? "");

            return string.Join(" ", classes);
        }
    }

    private string? ComputedStyle
    {
        get
        {
            if (AdditionalAttributes?.TryGetValue("style", out object? extraStyle) == true)
                return extraStyle.ToString();

            return null;
        }
    }

    private Dictionary<string, object>? FilteredAttributes
    {
        get
        {
            if (AdditionalAttributes == null) return null;

            return AdditionalAttributes
                .Where(kv => kv.Key != "class" && kv.Key != "style")
                .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value);
        }
    }
}

=== Internal\_BUIBtn.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Internal

<button type="button"
        data-bui-size="@Size.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
        class="@ComputedClass"
        disabled="@IsDisabled"
        tabindex="@(IsDisabled ? "-1" : "0")"
        aria-label="@AriaLabel"
        @onclick="OnClick"
        @onclick:stopPropagation="OnClickStopPropagation"
        @onclick:preventDefault="OnClickPreventDefault"
        @attributes="FilteredAttributes">
    @if (Loading)
    {
        <BUILoadingIndicator Variant="LoadingIndicatorVariant" />
    }
    else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Icon))
    {
        <BUISvgIcon Icon="@Icon" Size="Size" style="@IconStyle" />
    }
    @ChildContent
</button>

@code {
    [Parameter] public string? Icon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Active { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Loading { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public BUILoadingIndicatorVariant LoadingIndicatorVariant { get; set; } = BUILoadingIndicatorVariant.CircularProgress;
    [Parameter] public int IconRotation { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? AriaLabel { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<MouseEventArgs> OnClick { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool OnClickStopPropagation { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool OnClickPreventDefault { get; set; }
    [Parameter(CaptureUnmatchedValues = true)]
    public Dictionary<string, object>? AdditionalAttributes { get; set; }

    private bool IsDisabled => Disabled || Loading;

    private string ComputedClass
    {
        get
        {
            List<string> classes = ["_bui-btn"];

            if (Active)
                classes.Add("_bui-btn--active");

            if (AdditionalAttributes?.TryGetValue("class", out object? extraClass) == true)
                classes.Add(extraClass.ToString() ?? "");

            return string.Join(" ", classes);
        }
    }

    private string? IconStyle => IconRotation != 0
        ? $"transform: rotate({IconRotation}deg); transition: transform 150ms ease;"
        : null;

    private Dictionary<string, object>? FilteredAttributes
    {
        get
        {
            if (AdditionalAttributes == null) return null;

            return AdditionalAttributes
                .Where(kv => kv.Key != "class" && kv.Key != "style")
                .ToDictionary(kv => kv.Key, kv => kv.Value);
        }
    }
}

=== Internal\_BUICheckMark.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Internal

<span class="@ComputedClass"
      role="@(Mode == CheckMarkMode.Radio ? "radio" : "checkbox")"
      aria-checked="@AriaChecked"
      aria-disabled="@Disabled.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">
    <BUISvgIcon Icon="@CurrentIcon" Size="Size" />
</span>

@code {
    [Parameter] public bool? Checked { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public CheckMarkMode Mode { get; set; } = CheckMarkMode.Checkbox;
    [Parameter] public SizeEnum Size { get; set; } = SizeEnum.Medium;
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? CheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? UncheckedIcon { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? IndeterminateIcon { get; set; }

    private bool IsChecked => Checked == true;
    private bool IsIndeterminate => Checked == null && Mode == CheckMarkMode.Checkbox;

    private string AriaChecked => IsIndeterminate ? "mixed" : Checked?.ToString().ToLowerInvariant() ?? "false";

    private string ComputedClass
    {
        get
        {
            List<string> classes = ["_bui-checkmark"];

            if (IsChecked)
                classes.Add("_bui-checkmark--checked");
            else if (IsIndeterminate)
                classes.Add("_bui-checkmark--indeterminate");

            if (Disabled)
                classes.Add("_bui-checkmark--disabled");

            return string.Join(" ", classes);
        }
    }

    private string CurrentIcon
    {
        get
        {
            if (IsIndeterminate)
                return IndeterminateIcon ?? BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_indeterminate_check_box;

            if (IsChecked)
            {
                return Mode == CheckMarkMode.Radio
                    ? (CheckedIcon ?? BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_radio_button_checked)
                    : (CheckedIcon ?? BUIIcons.MaterialIconsRound.i_check_box);
            }

            return Mode == CheckMarkMode.Radio
                ? (UncheckedIcon ?? BUIIcons.MaterialIconsOutlined.i_radio_button_unchecked)
                : (UncheckedIcon ?? BUIIcons.MaterialIconsRound.i_check_box_outline_blank);
        }
    }

    public enum CheckMarkMode
    {
        Checkbox,
        Radio
    }
}

=== Internal\_BUIInNumber.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Internal

<input type="number"
       class="_bui-simple-number"
       value="@Value"
       min="@Min"
       max="@Max"
       step="@Step"
       placeholder="@Placeholder"
       disabled="@Disabled"
       aria-label="@AriaLabel"
       @onchange="HandleChange"
       @oninput="HandleInput"
       @attributes="AdditionalAttributes" />

@code {
    [Parameter] public int? Value { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<int?> ValueChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Min { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Max { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Step { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Placeholder { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? AriaLabel { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool UpdateOnInput { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<int?> OnInput { get; set; }
    [Parameter(CaptureUnmatchedValues = true)]
    public Dictionary<string, object>? AdditionalAttributes { get; set; }

    private async Task HandleChange(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        int? newValue = ParseValue(e.Value?.ToString());
        Value = newValue;
        await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(newValue);
    }

    private async Task HandleInput(ChangeEventArgs e)
    {
        int? newValue = ParseValue(e.Value?.ToString());

        if (UpdateOnInput)
        {
            Value = newValue;
            await ValueChanged.InvokeAsync(newValue);
        }

        if (OnInput.HasDelegate)
            await OnInput.InvokeAsync(newValue);
    }

    private static int? ParseValue(string? value)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(value))
            return null;

        return int.TryParse(value, out int result) ? result : null;
    }
}

=== Internal\_BUIPagination.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Internal

<div class="_bui-pagination">
    @if (ShowInfo)
    {
        <div class="_bui-pagination__info">
            Showing @PaginationStart to @PaginationEnd of @TotalItems
        </div>
    }

    <div class="_bui-pagination__controls">
        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronLeft"
                 Disabled="@(CurrentPage == 1)"
                 AriaLabel="Previous page"
                 OnClick="HandlePrevious" />

        @foreach (int currentPage in GetVisiblePages())
        {
            @if (currentPage == -1)
            {
                <span class="_bui-pagination__ellipsis">…</span>
            }
            else
            {
                <_BUIBtn Active="@(CurrentPage == currentPage)"
                         AriaLabel="@($"Page {currentPage}")"
                         OnClick="() => HandlePageClick(currentPage)">
                    @currentPage
                </_BUIBtn>
            }
        }

        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.ChevronRight"
                 Disabled="@(CurrentPage == TotalPages)"
                 AriaLabel="Next page"
                 OnClick="HandleNext" />
    </div>
</div>

@code {
    [Parameter] public int CurrentPage { get; set; } = 1;
    [Parameter] public int TotalPages { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int TotalItems { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int PageSize { get; set; } = 10;
    [Parameter] public bool ShowInfo { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public int MaxVisiblePages { get; set; } = 5;
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<int> OnPageChange { get; set; }

    private int PaginationStart => TotalItems == 0 ? 0 : (CurrentPage - 1) * PageSize + 1;
    private int PaginationEnd => Math.Min(CurrentPage * PageSize, TotalItems);

    private IEnumerable<int> GetVisiblePages()
    {
        if (TotalPages <= MaxVisiblePages)
        {
            for (int i = 1; i <= TotalPages; i++)
                yield return i;
            yield break;
        }

        int halfVisible = MaxVisiblePages / 2;
        int startPage = Math.Max(1, CurrentPage - halfVisible);
        int endPage = Math.Min(TotalPages, startPage + MaxVisiblePages - 1);

        if (endPage - startPage < MaxVisiblePages - 1)
            startPage = Math.Max(1, endPage - MaxVisiblePages + 1);

        if (startPage > 1)
        {
            yield return 1;
            if (startPage > 2)
                yield return -1;
        }

        for (int i = startPage; i <= endPage; i++)
        {
            if (i != 1 && i != TotalPages)
                yield return i;
        }

        if (endPage < TotalPages)
        {
            if (endPage < TotalPages - 1)
                yield return -1;
            yield return TotalPages;
        }
    }

    private async Task HandlePrevious()
    {
        if (CurrentPage > 1)
            await OnPageChange.InvokeAsync(CurrentPage - 1);
    }

    private async Task HandleNext()
    {
        if (CurrentPage < TotalPages)
            await OnPageChange.InvokeAsync(CurrentPage + 1);
    }

    private async Task HandlePageClick(int page)
    {
        if (page != CurrentPage)
            await OnPageChange.InvokeAsync(page);
    }
}

=== Layout\Card\BUICard.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIVariantComponentBase<BUICard, BUICardVariant>
@implements IHasShadow
@implements IHasBorder
@implements IHasBackgroundColor
@implements IHasColor

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    /* === Content Parameters === */

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Header { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Media { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Actions { get; set; }

    /* === Behavior Parameters === */

    [Parameter] public bool Clickable { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<MouseEventArgs> OnClick { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? MediaHeight { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public CardMediaPosition MediaPosition { get; set; } = CardMediaPosition.Top;

    [Parameter] public CardActionsAlignment ActionsAlignment { get; set; } = CardActionsAlignment.End;

    // === IHasShadow === //
    [Parameter] public ShadowStyle? Shadow { get; set; }

    /* === IHasBorder === */

    [Parameter] public BorderStyle? Border { get; set; }

    /* === IHasBackgroundColor === */

    [Parameter] public string? BackgroundColor { get; set; }

    /* === IHasColor === */

    [Parameter] public string? Color { get; set; }

    /* === Variant === */

    public override BUICardVariant DefaultVariant => BUICardVariant.Default;

    protected override Dictionary<BUICardVariant, Func<BUICard, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } = new()
    {
        [BUICardVariant.Default] = c => c.RenderCard(),
    };

    /* === Render Methods === */

    private RenderFragment RenderCard() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       data-bui-clickable="@Clickable.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
                       data-bui-media-position="@MediaPosition.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()">

            <div class="bui-card"
                 @onclick="HandleClick">

                @if (MediaPosition == CardMediaPosition.Top)
                {
                    @RenderMedia()
                }

                @if (Header != null)
                {
                    <div class="bui-card__header">
                        @Header
                    </div>
                }

                @if (MediaPosition == CardMediaPosition.AfterHeader)
                {
                    @RenderMedia()
                }

                @if (ChildContent != null)
                {
                    <div class="bui-card__content">
                        @ChildContent
                    </div>
                }

                @if (MediaPosition == CardMediaPosition.BeforeActions)
                {
                    @RenderMedia()
                }

                @if (Actions != null)
                {
                    <div class="bui-card__actions @GetActionsClass()">
                        @Actions
                    </div>
                }

                @if (MediaPosition == CardMediaPosition.Bottom)
                {
                    @RenderMedia()
                }
            </div>
        </bui-component>
    };

    private RenderFragment RenderMedia() => __builder =>
    {
        @if (Media != null)
        {
            <div class="bui-card__media">
                @Media
            </div>
        }
    };

    /* === Helper Methods === */

    private string GetActionsClass()
    {
        List<string> classes = new();

        classes.Add($"bui-card__actions--{ActionsAlignment.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()}");

        return string.Join(" ", classes);
    }

    private async Task HandleClick(MouseEventArgs args)
    {
        if (Clickable && OnClick.HasDelegate)
        {
            await OnClick.InvokeAsync(args);
        }
    }

    public override void BuildComponentCssVariables(Dictionary<string, string> cssVariables)
    {
        base.BuildComponentCssVariables(cssVariables);

        if (MediaHeight != null)
        {
            cssVariables["--bui-card-inline-media-height"] = MediaHeight;
        }
    }
}



=== Layout\Card\BUICard.razor.css ===

/* Base Card Styles */
bui-component[data-bui-component="card"] {
    display: block;
    width: 100%;
    /* CSS Variables */
    --_card-background: var(--bui-inline-background, var(--palette-surface));
    --_card-color: var(--bui-inline-color, var(--palette-surfacecontrast));
    --_card-border-radius: var(--bui-inline-border-radius, var(--bui-border-radius));
    --_card-border: var(--bui-inline-border, var(--bui-border-width) var(--bui-border-style) var(--palette-border));
    --_card-border-top: var(--bui-inline-border-top, var(--bui-inline-border, var(--bui-border-width) var(--bui-border-style) var(--palette-border)));
    --_card-border-right: var(--bui-inline-border-right, var(--bui-inline-border, var(--bui-border-width) var(--bui-border-style) var(--palette-border)));

    --_card-border-left: var(--bui-inline-border-left, var(--bui-inline-border, var(--bui-border-width) var(--bui-border-style) var(--palette-border)));

}

    /* Card Container */

=== Layout\Dialog\JsInterop\ModalCallbacksRelay.cs ===

using Microsoft.JSInterop;
using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public sealed class ModalCallbacksRelay : IDisposable
{
    private readonly IModalJsCallback _callback;

    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnEscapePressed))]
    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnOverlayClick))]
    public ModalCallbacksRelay(IModalJsCallback callback)
    {
        _callback = callback;
        DotNetReference = DotNetObjectReference.Create(this);
    }

    public DotNetObjectReference<ModalCallbacksRelay> DotNetReference { get; }

    public void Dispose() => DotNetReference.Dispose();

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnEscapePressed() => _callback.OnEscapePressed();

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnOverlayClick() => _callback.OnOverlayClick();
}



=== Layout\Dialog\JsInterop\ModalJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public interface IModalJsInterop
{
    ValueTask LockScrollAsync();

    ValueTask ReleaseFocusAsync();

    ValueTask TrapFocusAsync(ElementReference element);

    ValueTask UnlockScrollAsync();
}

public sealed class ModalJsInterop : ModuleJsInteropBase, IModalJsInterop
{
    public ModalJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.Modal)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask LockScrollAsync()
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("lockScroll");
    }

    public async ValueTask ReleaseFocusAsync()
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("releaseFocus");
    }

    public async ValueTask TrapFocusAsync(ElementReference element)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("trapFocus", element);
    }

    public async ValueTask UnlockScrollAsync()
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("unlockScroll");
    }
}



=== Layout\Dialog\Services\ModalService.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services;

public interface IModalService
{
    event Action? OnChange;

    IReadOnlyList<ModalState> ActiveModals { get; }

    Task CloseAllAsync();

    Task CloseAsync();

    Task<TResult?> ShowDialogAsync<TComponent, TResult>(
                object? parameters = null,
        DialogOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent;

    Task ShowDialogAsync<TComponent>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DialogOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent;

    Task<TResult?> ShowDrawerAsync<TComponent, TResult>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DrawerOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent;

    Task ShowDrawerAsync<TComponent>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DrawerOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent;
}

public class ModalService : IModalService
{
    private readonly List<ModalState> _modals = [];

    public event Action? OnChange;

    public IReadOnlyList<ModalState> ActiveModals => _modals.AsReadOnly();

    public async Task CloseAllAsync()
    {
        while (_modals.Count > 0)
        {
            await CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    public async Task CloseAsync()
    {
        if (_modals.Count == 0) return;

        ModalState current = _modals[^1];
        await CloseModalAsync(current);
    }

    public async Task<TResult?> ShowDialogAsync<TComponent, TResult>(
                object? parameters = null,
        DialogOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent
    {
        ModalState state = CreateModalState<TComponent>(
            ModalType.Dialog,
            parameters,
            options ?? new DialogOptions());

        return await ShowAndWaitAsync<TResult>(state);
    }

    public Task ShowDialogAsync<TComponent>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DialogOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent
    {
        ModalState state = CreateModalState<TComponent>(
            ModalType.Dialog,
            parameters,
            options ?? new DialogOptions());

        return ShowAsync(state);
    }

    public async Task<TResult?> ShowDrawerAsync<TComponent, TResult>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DrawerOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent
    {
        ModalState state = CreateModalState<TComponent>(
            ModalType.Drawer,
            parameters,
            options ?? new DrawerOptions());

        return await ShowAndWaitAsync<TResult>(state);
    }

    public Task ShowDrawerAsync<TComponent>(
        object? parameters = null,
        DrawerOptions? options = null)
        where TComponent : IModalContent
    {
        ModalState state = CreateModalState<TComponent>(
            ModalType.Drawer,
            parameters,
            options ?? new DrawerOptions());

        return ShowAsync(state);
    }

    private async Task CloseModalAsync(ModalState state)
    {
        state.IsAnimatingOut = true;
        OnChange?.Invoke();

        await Task.Delay(200);

        _modals.Remove(state);
        ShowPreviousModal();
        OnChange?.Invoke();
    }

    private ModalState CreateModalState<TComponent>(
            ModalType type,
        object? parameters,
        ModalOptionsBase options)
        where TComponent : IModalContent
    {
        string id = $"modal-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
        ModalReference reference = new(id, OnModalClose);

        Dictionary<string, object?>? paramDict = null;
        if (parameters != null)
        {
            paramDict = parameters.GetType()
                .GetProperties()
                .ToDictionary(p => p.Name, p => p.GetValue(parameters));
        }

        return new ModalState
        {
            Id = id,
            Type = type,
            ComponentType = typeof(TComponent),
            Reference = reference,
            Options = options,
            Parameters = paramDict
        };
    }

    private void HideCurrentModal()
    {
        if (_modals.Count > 0)
        {
            _modals[^1].IsVisible = false;
        }
    }

    private void OnModalClose(ModalReference reference)
    {
        ModalState? state = _modals.FirstOrDefault(m => m.Reference == reference);
        if (state != null)
        {
            _ = CloseModalAsync(state);
        }
    }

    private async Task<TResult?> ShowAndWaitAsync<TResult>(ModalState state)
    {
        HideCurrentModal();
        _modals.Add(state);
        OnChange?.Invoke();

        try
        {
            object? result = await state.Reference.Result;
            return result is TResult typed ? typed : default;
        }
        catch (TaskCanceledException)
        {
            return default;
        }
    }

    private Task ShowAsync(ModalState state)
    {
        HideCurrentModal();
        _modals.Add(state);
        OnChange?.Invoke();
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    private void ShowPreviousModal()
    {
        if (_modals.Count > 0)
        {
            _modals[^1].IsVisible = true;
        }
    }
}



=== Layout\Dialog\BUIDialog.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IAsyncDisposable

@inject IModalJsInterop JsInterop

@if (Open)
{
    <div class="bui-dialog-host"
         @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown"
         tabindex="-1"
         @ref="_hostRef">
        <div class="bui-dialog-overlay @(_isClosing ? "bui-dialog-overlay--closing" : "")"
             @onclick="HandleOverlayClick">
        </div>

        <div class="bui-dialog @(_isClosing ? "bui-dialog--closing" : "")"
             @ref="_dialogRef"
             @onclick:stopPropagation="true"
             role="dialog"
             aria-modal="true"
             aria-labelledby="@_titleId"
             style="@GetDialogStyle()">

            @if (Header != null || !string.IsNullOrEmpty(Title) || Closable)
            {
                <div class="bui-dialog__header">
                    @if (Header != null)
                    {
                        @Header
                    }
                    else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Title))
                    {
                        <h2 id="@_titleId" class="bui-dialog__title">@Title</h2>
                    }

                    @if (Closable)
                    {
                        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                                    AriaLabel="Close"
                                    OnClick="CloseAsync" />
                    }
                </div>
            }

            @if (Content != null)
            {
                <div class="bui-dialog__content">
                    @Content
                </div>
            }

            @if (Footer != null)
            {
                <div class="bui-dialog__footer">
                    @Footer
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>
}

@code {
    private readonly string _titleId = $"dialog-title-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private ElementReference _hostRef;
    private ElementReference _dialogRef;
    private bool _jsInitialized;
    private bool _isClosing;

    [Parameter] public bool Open { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<bool> OpenChanged { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? Title { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Header { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Content { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Footer { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool Closable { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnOverlayClick { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnEscape { get; set; } = true;

    [Parameter] public string? MinWidth { get; set; } = "300px";
    [Parameter] public string? MaxWidth { get; set; } = "90vw";
    [Parameter] public string? MinHeight { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? MaxHeight { get; set; } = "90vh";
    [Parameter] public bool FullScreen { get; set; }

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (Open && !_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.LockScrollAsync();
            await JsInterop.TrapFocusAsync(_dialogRef);
            await _hostRef.FocusAsync();
            _jsInitialized = true;
        }
        else if (!Open && _jsInitialized)
        {
            await CleanupAsync();
        }
    }

    private string GetDialogStyle()
    {
        List<string> styles = [];

        if (FullScreen)
        {
            styles.Add("width: 100vw");
            styles.Add("height: 100vh");
            styles.Add("max-width: 100vw");
            styles.Add("max-height: 100vh");
            styles.Add("border-radius: 0");
        }
        else
        {
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MinWidth))
                styles.Add($"min-width: {MinWidth}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MaxWidth))
                styles.Add($"max-width: {MaxWidth}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MinHeight))
                styles.Add($"min-height: {MinHeight}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(MaxHeight))
                styles.Add($"max-height: {MaxHeight}");
        }

        return string.Join("; ", styles);
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.Key == "Escape" && CloseOnEscape)
        {
            await CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleOverlayClick()
    {
        if (CloseOnOverlayClick)
        {
            await CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private async Task CloseAsync()
    {
        _isClosing = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        await Task.Delay(150);

        _isClosing = false;
        Open = false;
        await OpenChanged.InvokeAsync(false);
    }

    private async Task CleanupAsync()
    {
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.ReleaseFocusAsync();
            await JsInterop.UnlockScrollAsync();
            _jsInitialized = false;
        }
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        await CleanupAsync();
    }
}

=== Layout\Dialog\BUIDrawer.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IAsyncDisposable

@inject IModalJsInterop JsInterop

@if (Open)
{
    <div class="bui-drawer-host"
         @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown"
         tabindex="-1"
         @ref="_hostRef">

        <div class="bui-drawer-overlay @(_isClosing ? "bui-drawer-overlay--closing" : "")"
             @onclick="HandleOverlayClick">
        </div>

        <div class="bui-drawer bui-drawer--@Position.ToString().ToLowerInvariant() @(_isClosing ? "bui-drawer--closing" : "")"
             @ref="_drawerRef"
             @onclick:stopPropagation="true"
             role="dialog"
             aria-modal="true"
             style="@GetDrawerStyle()">

            @if (Header != null || Closable)
            {
                <div class="bui-drawer__header">
                    @if (Header != null)
                    {
                        <div class="bui-drawer__header-content">
                            @Header
                        </div>
                    }

                    @if (Closable)
                    {
                        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                                    AriaLabel="Close"
                                    OnClick="CloseAsync" />
                    }
                </div>
            }

            <div class="bui-drawer__content">
                @ChildContent
            </div>

            @if (Footer != null)
            {
                <div class="bui-drawer__footer">
                    @Footer
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>
}

@code {
    private ElementReference _hostRef;
    private ElementReference _drawerRef;
    private bool _jsInitialized;
    private bool _isClosing;

    [Parameter] public bool Open { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<bool> OpenChanged { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Header { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? Footer { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public DrawerPosition Position { get; set; } = DrawerPosition.Right;
    [Parameter] public string Size { get; set; } = "300px";

    [Parameter] public bool Closable { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnOverlayClick { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool CloseOnEscape { get; set; } = true;

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (Open && !_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.LockScrollAsync();
            await JsInterop.TrapFocusAsync(_drawerRef);
            await _hostRef.FocusAsync();
            _jsInitialized = true;
        }
        else if (!Open && _jsInitialized)
        {
            await CleanupAsync();
        }
    }

    private string GetDrawerStyle()
    {
        return Position switch
        {
            DrawerPosition.Left or DrawerPosition.Right => $"width: {Size}",
            DrawerPosition.Top or DrawerPosition.Bottom => $"height: {Size}",
            _ => string.Empty
        };
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.Key == "Escape" && CloseOnEscape)
        {
            await CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleOverlayClick()
    {
        if (CloseOnOverlayClick)
        {
            await CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    private async Task CloseAsync()
    {
        _isClosing = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        await Task.Delay(200);

        _isClosing = false;
        Open = false;
        await OpenChanged.InvokeAsync(false);
    }

    private async Task CleanupAsync()
    {
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.ReleaseFocusAsync();
            await JsInterop.UnlockScrollAsync();
            _jsInitialized = false;
        }
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        await CleanupAsync();
    }
}
