=== Layout\Dialog\BUIModalContainer.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

<div class="bui-modal-container @GetVisibilityClass() @GetAnimationClass()"
     data-bui-modal-type="@Modal.Type.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()"
     @onclick:stopPropagation="true">

    @if (Modal.Type == ModalType.Dialog)
    {
        <div class="bui-modal-dialog" style="@GetDialogStyle()">
            @if (Modal.Options is DialogOptions { Title: not null } dialogOpts)
            {
                <div class="bui-modal-dialog__header">
                    <h2 class="bui-modal-dialog__title">@dialogOpts.Title</h2>
                    @if (Modal.Options.Closable)
                    {
                        <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                                    AriaLabel="Close"
                                    OnClick="HandleClose" />
                    }
                </div>
            }
            else if (Modal.Options.Closable)
            {
                <div class="bui-modal-dialog__header bui-modal-dialog__header--close-only">
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                                AriaLabel="Close"
                                OnClick="HandleClose" />
                </div>
            }

            <div class="bui-modal-dialog__content">
                @RenderComponent()
            </div>
        </div>
    }
    else
    {
        <div class="bui-modal-drawer @GetDrawerPositionClass()" style="@GetDrawerStyle()">
            @if (Modal.Options.Closable)
            {
                <div class="bui-modal-drawer__header">
                    <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                                AriaLabel="Close"
                                OnClick="HandleClose" />
                </div>
            }

            <div class="bui-modal-drawer__content">
                @RenderComponent()
            </div>
        </div>
    }
</div>

@code {
    [Parameter, EditorRequired]
    public ModalState Modal { get; set; } = default!;

    private string GetVisibilityClass() =>
        Modal.IsVisible ? "bui-modal-container--visible" : "bui-modal-container--hidden";

    private string GetAnimationClass() =>
        Modal.IsAnimatingOut ? "bui-modal-container--closing" : "bui-modal-container--opening";

    private string GetDialogStyle()
    {
        if (Modal.Options is not DialogOptions options)
            return string.Empty;

        List<string> styles = [];

        if (options.FullScreen)
        {
            styles.Add("width: 100vw");
            styles.Add("height: 100vh");
            styles.Add("max-width: 100vw");
            styles.Add("max-height: 100vh");
            styles.Add("border-radius: 0");
        }
        else
        {
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(options.MinWidth))
                styles.Add($"min-width: {options.MinWidth}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(options.MaxWidth))
                styles.Add($"max-width: {options.MaxWidth}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(options.MinHeight))
                styles.Add($"min-height: {options.MinHeight}");
            if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(options.MaxHeight))
                styles.Add($"max-height: {options.MaxHeight}");
        }

        return string.Join("; ", styles);
    }

    private string GetDrawerPositionClass()
    {
        if (Modal.Options is not DrawerOptions options)
            return string.Empty;

        return $"bui-modal-drawer--{options.Position.ToString().ToLowerInvariant()}";
    }

    private string GetDrawerStyle()
    {
        if (Modal.Options is not DrawerOptions options)
            return string.Empty;

        return options.Position switch
        {
            DrawerPosition.Left or DrawerPosition.Right => $"width: {options.Size}",
            DrawerPosition.Top or DrawerPosition.Bottom => $"height: {options.Size}",
            _ => string.Empty
        };
    }

    private async Task HandleClose()
    {
        await Modal.Reference.CloseAsync();
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderComponent() => builder =>
    {
        builder.OpenComponent(0, Modal.ComponentType);
        builder.AddAttribute(1, "ModalRef", Modal.Reference);

        if (Modal.Parameters != null)
        {
            int seq = 2;
            foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object?> param in Modal.Parameters)
            {
                builder.AddAttribute(seq++, param.Key, param.Value);
            }
        }

        builder.CloseComponent();
    };
}

=== Layout\Dialog\BUIModalHost.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@implements IAsyncDisposable

@inject IModalService ModalService
@inject IModalJsInterop JsInterop

@if (_modals.Count > 0)
{
    <div class="bui-modal-host"
         @onkeydown="HandleKeyDown"
         tabindex="-1"
         @ref="_hostRef">
        
        <div class="bui-modal-overlay @(_isClosing ? "bui-modal-overlay--closing" : "")"
             @onclick="HandleOverlayClick">
        </div>

        @foreach (ModalState modal in _modals)
        {
            <BUIModalContainer Modal="modal" />
        }
    </div>
}

@code {
    private ElementReference _hostRef;
    private List<ModalState> _modals = [];
    private bool _jsInitialized;
    private bool _isClosing;

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        ModalService.OnChange += HandleModalChange;
    }

    private async void HandleModalChange()
    {
        List<ModalState> previous = _modals;
        _modals = ModalService.ActiveModals.ToList();
        _isClosing = _modals.Any(m => m.IsAnimatingOut);

        if (_modals.Count > 0 && !_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.LockScrollAsync();
            _jsInitialized = true;
        }
        else if (_modals.Count == 0 && _jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.UnlockScrollAsync();
            _jsInitialized = false;
        }

        await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
    }

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (_modals.Count > 0)
        {
            ModalState? current = _modals.LastOrDefault(m => m.IsVisible && !m.IsAnimatingOut);
            if (current != null)
            {
                _hostRef.FocusAsync();
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs e)
    {
        if (e.Key == "Escape")
        {
            ModalState? current = _modals.LastOrDefault(m => m.IsVisible && !m.IsAnimatingOut);
            if (current?.Options.CloseOnEscape == true)
            {
                await current.Reference.CloseAsync();
            }
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleOverlayClick()
    {
        ModalState? current = _modals.LastOrDefault(m => m.IsVisible && !m.IsAnimatingOut);
        if (current?.Options.CloseOnOverlayClick == true)
        {
            await current.Reference.CloseAsync();
        }
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        ModalService.OnChange -= HandleModalChange;
        
        if (_jsInitialized)
        {
            await JsInterop.UnlockScrollAsync();
        }
    }
}

=== Layout\Dialog\ModalOptions.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public class DialogOptions : ModalOptionsBase
{
    public bool FullScreen { get; set; }
    public string? MaxHeight { get; set; } = "90vh";
    public string? MaxWidth { get; set; } = "90vw";
    public string? MinHeight { get; set; }
    public string? MinWidth { get; set; } = "300px";
    public string? Title { get; set; }
}

public class DrawerOptions : ModalOptionsBase
{
    public DrawerPosition Position { get; set; } = DrawerPosition.Right;
    public string Size { get; set; } = "300px";
}

public abstract class ModalOptionsBase
{
    public bool Closable { get; set; } = true;
    public bool CloseOnEscape { get; set; } = true;
    public bool CloseOnOverlayClick { get; set; } = true;
    public string? CssClass { get; set; }
}

public enum DrawerPosition
{
    Left,
    Right,
    Top,
    Bottom
}



=== Layout\Dialog\ModalReference.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public class ModalReference
{
    private readonly Action<ModalReference> _onClose;
    private readonly TaskCompletionSource<object?> _resultSource = new();

    internal ModalReference(string id, Action<ModalReference> onClose)
    {
        Id = id;
        _onClose = onClose;
    }

    public string Id { get; }

    internal Task<object?> Result => _resultSource.Task;

    public Task CloseAsync()
    {
        _resultSource.TrySetResult(null);
        _onClose(this);
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    public Task CloseAsync<TResult>(TResult result)
    {
        _resultSource.TrySetResult(result);
        _onClose(this);
        return Task.CompletedTask;
    }

    internal void Cancel()
    {
        _resultSource.TrySetCanceled();
    }
}

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public enum ModalType
{
    Dialog,
    Drawer
}

public class ModalState

    public string Id { get; init; }
    public bool IsAnimatingOut { get; set; }
    public bool IsVisible { get; set; } = true;
    public ModalOptionsBase Options { get; init; }
    public Dictionary<string, object?>? Parameters { get; init; }
    public ModalReference Reference { get; init; }
    public ModalType Type { get; init; }
}



=== Layout\Grid\BUIGrid.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIComponentBase

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    @ChildContent
</bui-component>

@code {
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Columns { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? MaxWidth { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? Gap { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? GapXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? GapSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? GapMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? GapLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? GapXl { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? RowGap { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? ColumnGap { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public GridDirection Direction { get; set; } = GridDirection.Row;
    [Parameter] public GridDirection? DirectionXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public GridDirection? DirectionSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public GridDirection? DirectionMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public GridDirection? DirectionLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public GridDirection? DirectionXl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public GridJustifyContent JustifyContent { get; set; } = GridJustifyContent.Start;
    [Parameter] public GridAlignItems AlignItems { get; set; } = GridAlignItems.Stretch;
    [Parameter] public GridWrap Wrap { get; set; } = GridWrap.Wrap;

    [Parameter] public string? P { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pt { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pr { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pb { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pl { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Px { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Py { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? M { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mt { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mr { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mb { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Ml { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mx { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? My { get; set; }

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        if (Direction != GridDirection.Row)
            dataAttributes["data-dir"] = ToKebab(Direction);
        if (DirectionXs.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-dir-xs"] = ToKebab(DirectionXs.Value);
        if (DirectionSm.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-dir-sm"] = ToKebab(DirectionSm.Value);
        if (DirectionMd.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-dir-md"] = ToKebab(DirectionMd.Value);
        if (DirectionLg.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-dir-lg"] = ToKebab(DirectionLg.Value);
        if (DirectionXl.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-dir-xl"] = ToKebab(DirectionXl.Value);

        if (JustifyContent != GridJustifyContent.Start)
            dataAttributes["data-justify"] = ToKebab(JustifyContent);
        if (AlignItems != GridAlignItems.Stretch)
            dataAttributes["data-align"] = ToKebab(AlignItems);
        if (Wrap != GridWrap.Wrap)
            dataAttributes["data-wrap"] = ToKebab(Wrap);

        if (MaxWidth != null)
            dataAttributes["data-contained"] = "true";
    }

    public override void BuildComponentCssVariables(Dictionary<string, string> cssVariables)
    {
        if (Columns.HasValue)
            cssVariables["--columns"] = Columns.Value.ToString();

        if (MaxWidth != null)
            cssVariables["--max-w"] = MaxWidth;

        if (Gap != null)
            cssVariables["--gap"] = Gap;
        if (GapXs != null)
            cssVariables["--gap-xs"] = GapXs;
        if (GapSm != null)
            cssVariables["--gap-sm"] = GapSm;
        if (GapMd != null)
            cssVariables["--gap-md"] = GapMd;
        if (GapLg != null)
            cssVariables["--gap-lg"] = GapLg;
        if (GapXl != null)
            cssVariables["--gap-xl"] = GapXl;
        if (RowGap != null)
            cssVariables["--row-gap"] = RowGap;
        if (ColumnGap != null)
            cssVariables["--col-gap"] = ColumnGap;

        BuildSpacing(cssVariables, P, Pt, Pr, Pb, Pl, Px, Py, "p");
        BuildSpacing(cssVariables, M, Mt, Mr, Mb, Ml, Mx, My, "m");
    }

    private static void BuildSpacing(Dictionary<string, string> css,
        string? all, string? t, string? r, string? b, string? l, string? x, string? y, string prefix)
    {
        if (all != null) { css[$"--{prefix}"] = all; return; }

        string? top = t ?? y;
        string? right = r ?? x;
        string? bottom = b ?? y;
        string? left = l ?? x;

        if (top != null) css[$"--{prefix}t"] = top;
        if (right != null) css[$"--{prefix}r"] = right;
        if (bottom != null) css[$"--{prefix}b"] = bottom;
        if (left != null) css[$"--{prefix}l"] = left;
    }

    private static string ToKebab(Enum value) =>
        string.Concat(value.ToString().Select((c, i) =>
            i > 0 && char.IsUpper(c) ? $"-{char.ToLower(c)}" : char.ToLower(c).ToString()));
}



=== Layout\Grid\BUIGrid.razor.css ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIComponentBase

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    @ChildContent
</bui-component>

@code {
    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public int? Span { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Xs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Sm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Md { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Lg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? Xl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool Auto { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public int? Offset { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OffsetXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OffsetSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OffsetMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OffsetLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OffsetXl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public int? Order { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OrderXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OrderSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OrderMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OrderLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public int? OrderXl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public GridAlignSelf? AlignSelf { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool HideXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool HideSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool HideMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool HideLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool HideXl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public bool ShowXs { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowSm { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowMd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowLg { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowXl { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? P { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pt { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pr { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pb { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Pl { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Px { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Py { get; set; }

    [Parameter] public string? M { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mt { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mr { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mb { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Ml { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? Mx { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string? My { get; set; }

    private bool HasSpan => Span.HasValue || Xs.HasValue || Sm.HasValue || Md.HasValue || Lg.HasValue || Xl.HasValue;

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        if (Auto)
            dataAttributes["data-auto"] = "true";
        else if (HasSpan)
            dataAttributes["data-sized"] = "true";

        if (AlignSelf.HasValue)
            dataAttributes["data-align-self"] = ToKebab(AlignSelf.Value);

        if (HideXs) dataAttributes["data-hide-xs"] = "true";
        if (HideSm) dataAttributes["data-hide-sm"] = "true";
        if (HideMd) dataAttributes["data-hide-md"] = "true";
        if (HideLg) dataAttributes["data-hide-lg"] = "true";
        if (HideXl) dataAttributes["data-hide-xl"] = "true";

        if (ShowXs) dataAttributes["data-show-xs"] = "true";
        if (ShowSm) dataAttributes["data-show-sm"] = "true";
        if (ShowMd) dataAttributes["data-show-md"] = "true";
        if (ShowLg) dataAttributes["data-show-lg"] = "true";
        if (ShowXl) dataAttributes["data-show-xl"] = "true";
    }

    public override void BuildComponentCssVariables(Dictionary<string, string> cssVariables)
    {
        if (Span.HasValue) cssVariables["--span"] = Span.Value.ToString();
        if (Xs.HasValue) cssVariables["--xs"] = Xs.Value.ToString();
        if (Sm.HasValue) cssVariables["--sm"] = Sm.Value.ToString();
        if (Md.HasValue) cssVariables["--md"] = Md.Value.ToString();
        if (Lg.HasValue) cssVariables["--lg"] = Lg.Value.ToString();
        if (Xl.HasValue) cssVariables["--xl"] = Xl.Value.ToString();

        if (Offset.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset"] = Offset.Value.ToString();
        if (OffsetXs.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset-xs"] = OffsetXs.Value.ToString();
        if (OffsetSm.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset-sm"] = OffsetSm.Value.ToString();
        if (OffsetMd.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset-md"] = OffsetMd.Value.ToString();
        if (OffsetLg.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset-lg"] = OffsetLg.Value.ToString();
        if (OffsetXl.HasValue) cssVariables["--offset-xl"] = OffsetXl.Value.ToString();

        if (Order.HasValue) cssVariables["--order"] = Order.Value.ToString();
        if (OrderXs.HasValue) cssVariables["--order-xs"] = OrderXs.Value.ToString();
        if (OrderSm.HasValue) cssVariables["--order-sm"] = OrderSm.Value.ToString();
        if (OrderMd.HasValue) cssVariables["--order-md"] = OrderMd.Value.ToString();
        if (OrderLg.HasValue) cssVariables["--order-lg"] = OrderLg.Value.ToString();
        if (OrderXl.HasValue) cssVariables["--order-xl"] = OrderXl.Value.ToString();

        BuildSpacing(cssVariables, P, Pt, Pr, Pb, Pl, Px, Py, "p");
        BuildSpacing(cssVariables, M, Mt, Mr, Mb, Ml, Mx, My, "m");
    }

    private static void BuildSpacing(Dictionary<string, string> css,
        string? all, string? t, string? r, string? b, string? l, string? x, string? y, string prefix)
    {
        if (all != null) { css[$"--{prefix}"] = all; return; }

        string? top = t ?? y;
        string? right = r ?? x;
        string? bottom = b ?? y;
        string? left = l ?? x;

        if (top != null) css[$"--{prefix}t"] = top;
        if (right != null) css[$"--{prefix}r"] = right;
        if (bottom != null) css[$"--{prefix}b"] = bottom;
        if (left != null) css[$"--{prefix}l"] = left;
    }

    private static string ToKebab(Enum value) =>
        string.Concat(value.ToString().Select((c, i) =>
            i > 0 && char.IsUpper(c) ? $"-{char.ToLower(c)}" : char.ToLower(c).ToString()));
}



=== Layout\Grid\BUIGridItem.razor.css ===

/*
 * Three modes:
 * 1. Default (no span, no auto): flex: 0 0 auto - fits content naturally
 * 2. Sized (has span): flex: 0 0 calc(...) - fixed column-based width
 * 3. Auto: flex: 1 1 0% - expands to fill available space
 *
 * Width formula for sized items:
 * width = (100% + gap) / columns * span - gap
 */

/* ========================================
   BASE - Content-fit (default)
   ======================================== */
bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"] {
    flex: 0 0 auto;
    order: var(--order, 0);
    min-width: 0;
    box-sizing: border-box;
    padding: var(--p, var(--pt, 0) var(--pr, 0) var(--pb, 0) var(--pl, 0));
    margin-top: var(--mt, var(--m, 0));
    margin-right: var(--mr, var(--m, 0));
    margin-bottom: var(--mb, var(--m, 0));
    margin-left: var(--ml, var(--m, 0));
}

    /* ========================================
   AUTO - Expand to fill space
   ======================================== */
    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-auto] {
        flex: 1 1 0%;
    }

    /* ========================================
   SIZED - Column-based width
   ======================================== */
    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-sized] {
        --_span: var(--span, 12);
        --_cols: var(--columns, 12);
        --_gap: var(--col-gap, var(--gap, 1rem));
        --_offset: var(--offset, 0);
        flex: 0 0 calc((100% + var(--_gap)) / var(--_cols) * var(--_span) - var(--_gap));
        margin-left: calc((100% + var(--_gap)) / var(--_cols) * var(--_offset) + var(--ml, var(--m, 0)));
    }

    /* Align Self */
    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-align-self="start"] {
        align-self: flex-start;
    }

    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-align-self="end"] {
        align-self: flex-end;
    }

    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-align-self="center"] {
        align-self: center;
    }

    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-align-self="stretch"] {
        align-self: stretch;
    }

    bui-component[data-bui-component="grid-item"][data-align-self="baseline"] {
        align-self: baseline;
    }

/* ========================================
   RESPONSIVE - XS (< 640px)
   ======================================== */

        --_offset: var(--offset-xs, var(--offset, 0));
        order: var(--order-xs, var(--order, 0));

    End,

=== Layout\ThemeGenerator\BUIThemeEditor.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Css

<div class="bui-theme-editor">
    @foreach (ColorCategory category in _categories)
    {
        <div class="bui-theme-editor__category">
            <h4 class="bui-theme-editor__category-title">@category.Name</h4>
            <BUIGrid Columns="12" Gap="0.75rem">
                @foreach (string propName in category.Properties)
                {
                    if (_palette.ContainsKey(propName))
                    {
                        string key = propName;
                        <BUIGridItem Xs="12" Md="4">
                            <BUIInputColor Label="@key"
                                           Value="_palette[key]"
                                           ValueChanged="c => HandleColorChanged(key, c)"
                                           ValueExpression="@(() => _palette[key])"
                                           Size="SizeEnum.Small"
                                           Density="DensityEnum.Compact" />
                        </BUIGridItem>
                    }
                }
            </BUIGrid>
        </div>
    }
</div>

@code {
    private Dictionary<string, CssColor> _palette = new();

    [Parameter]
    public Dictionary<string, CssColor> Palette
    {
        get => _palette;
        set => _palette = value ?? new();
    }

    [Parameter] public EventCallback<Dictionary<string, CssColor>> OnPaletteChanged { get; set; }

    private readonly List<ColorCategory> _categories = new()
    {
        new ColorCategory("Surface", new[] { "Background", "BackgroundContrast", "Surface", "SurfaceContrast" }),
        new ColorCategory("Main", new[] { "Primary", "PrimaryContrast", "Secondary", "SecondaryContrast" }),
        new ColorCategory("Status", new[] { "Error", "ErrorContrast", "Success", "SuccessContrast", "Warning", "WarningContrast", "Info", "InfoContrast" }),
        new ColorCategory("Utility", new[] { "Black", "White", "Border", "Shadow", "Highlight" })
    };

    private async Task HandleColorChanged(string propertyName, CssColor? newColor)
    {
        if (newColor == null) return;
        _palette[propertyName] = newColor;
        await OnPaletteChanged.InvokeAsync(_palette);
    }

    private record ColorCategory(string Name, string[] Properties);
}

    </Content>
    <Footer>
        <BUIButton Text="Close" OnClick="() => _exportDialogOpen = false" />
    </Footer>
</BUIDialog>

@code {
    private string _activeTheme = "dark";
    private Dictionary<string, CssColor> _darkPalette = new();
    private Dictionary<string, CssColor> _lightPalette = new();

    private bool _exportDialogOpen = false;
    private string _exportTitle = "";
    private string _exportContent = "";
    private SyntaxHighlightLanguage _exportLanguage = SyntaxHighlightLanguage.Json;

    private bool _importDialogOpen = false;
    private string _importContent = "";
    private string _importError = "";
    private const string _importPlaceholder = @"{
  ""dark"": { ""primary"": ""#8AB4F8"", ... },
  ""light"": { ""primary"": ""#1A73E8"", ... }
}";

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        InitializePalettes();
    }

    private void InitializePalettes()
    {
        DarkTheme dark = new();
        LightTheme light = new();

        _darkPalette = ExtractPaletteColors(dark);
        _lightPalette = ExtractPaletteColors(light);
    }

    private Dictionary<string, CssColor> ExtractPaletteColors(BUIThemePaletteBase palette)
    {
        Dictionary<string, CssColor> colors = new();
        PropertyInfo[] properties = typeof(BUIThemePaletteBase)
            .GetProperties(BindingFlags.Instance | BindingFlags.Public)
            .Where(p => p.PropertyType == typeof(CssColor))
            .ToArray();

        foreach (PropertyInfo prop in properties)
        {
            CssColor color = (CssColor)prop.GetValue(palette)!;
            colors[prop.Name] = color;
        }
        return colors;
    }

    private string GetPreviewStyles()
    {
        List<string> vars = new();
        Dictionary<string, CssColor> palette = _activeTheme == "dark" ? _darkPalette : _lightPalette;

        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, CssColor> kvp in palette)
        {
            string cssName = kvp.Key.ToLowerInvariant();
            vars.Add($"--palette-{cssName}: {kvp.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)}");
        }

        return string.Join("; ", vars);
    }

    private void OpenImportDialog()
    {
        _importContent = "";
        _importError = "";
        _importDialogOpen = true;
    }

    private void ImportJson()
    {
        _importError = "";

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(_importContent))
        {
            _importError = "Please paste JSON content.";
            return;
        }

        try
        {
            JsonDocument doc = JsonDocument.Parse(_importContent);
            JsonElement root = doc.RootElement;

            if (root.TryGetProperty("dark", out JsonElement darkElement))
            {
                MergePalette(_darkPalette, darkElement);
            }

            if (root.TryGetProperty("light", out JsonElement lightElement))
            {
                MergePalette(_lightPalette, lightElement);
            }

            _importDialogOpen = false;
        }
        catch (JsonException ex)
        {
            _importError = $"Invalid JSON: {ex.Message}";
        }
    }

    private void MergePalette(Dictionary<string, CssColor> target, JsonElement source)
    {
        foreach (JsonProperty prop in source.EnumerateObject())
        {
            string? key = FindMatchingKey(target, prop.Name);
            if (key != null && prop.Value.ValueKind == JsonValueKind.String)
            {
                string? colorValue = prop.Value.GetString();
                if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(colorValue))
                {
                    try
                    {
                        target[key] = new CssColor(colorValue);
                    }
                    catch
                    {
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private string? FindMatchingKey(Dictionary<string, CssColor> palette, string jsonKey)
    {
        foreach (string key in palette.Keys)
        {
            if (string.Equals(key, jsonKey, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))
            {
                return key;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    private void ShowExport(string title, string content)
    {
        _exportTitle = $"Export {title}";
        _exportContent = content;
        _exportLanguage = title switch
        {
            "JSON" => SyntaxHighlightLanguage.Json,
            "CSS" => SyntaxHighlightLanguage.Css,
            "C#" => SyntaxHighlightLanguage.CSharp,
            _ => SyntaxHighlightLanguage.Json
        };
        _exportDialogOpen = true;
    }

    private string GenerateJson()
    {
        var export = new
        {
            dark = _darkPalette.ToDictionary(k => k.Key.ToLowerInvariant(), v => v.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)),
            light = _lightPalette.ToDictionary(k => k.Key.ToLowerInvariant(), v => v.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex))
        };
        return JsonSerializer.Serialize(export, new JsonSerializerOptions { WriteIndented = true });
    }

    private string GenerateCss()
    {
        System.Text.StringBuilder sb = new();
        sb.AppendLine(":root {");
        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, CssColor> kvp in _darkPalette)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"  --palette-{kvp.Key.ToLowerInvariant()}: {kvp.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)};");
        }
        sb.AppendLine("}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("html[data-theme=\"light\"] {");
        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, CssColor> kvp in _lightPalette)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"  --palette-{kvp.Key.ToLowerInvariant()}: {kvp.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)};");
        }
        sb.AppendLine("}");
        return sb.ToString();
    }

    private string GenerateCSharp()
    {
        System.Text.StringBuilder sb = new();
        sb.AppendLine("using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Css;");
        sb.AppendLine("using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Theming.Abstractions;");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("public class CustomDarkTheme : BUIThemePaletteBase");
        sb.AppendLine("{");
        sb.AppendLine("    public CustomDarkTheme()");
        sb.AppendLine("    {");
        sb.AppendLine("        Id = \"dark\";");
        sb.AppendLine("        Name = \"Dark\";");
        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, CssColor> kvp in _darkPalette)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"        {kvp.Key} = new CssColor(\"{kvp.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)}\");");
        }
        sb.AppendLine("    }");
        sb.AppendLine("}");
        sb.AppendLine();
        sb.AppendLine("public class CustomLightTheme : BUIThemePaletteBase");
        sb.AppendLine("{");
        sb.AppendLine("    public CustomLightTheme()");
        sb.AppendLine("    {");
        sb.AppendLine("        Id = \"light\";");
        sb.AppendLine("        Name = \"Light\";");
        foreach (KeyValuePair<string, CssColor> kvp in _lightPalette)
        {
            sb.AppendLine($"        {kvp.Key} = new CssColor(\"{kvp.Value.ToString(ColorOutputFormats.Hex)}\");");
        }
        sb.AppendLine("    }");
        sb.AppendLine("}");
        return sb.ToString();
    }

    private void Reset()
    {
        InitializePalettes();
    }
}

=== Layout\ThemeSelector\BUIThemeSelector.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Forms

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIVariantComponentBase<BUIThemeSelector, BUIThemeSelectorVariant>

@inject IThemeJsInterop ThemeInterop

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    [Parameter] public string[] AvailableThemes { get; set; } = new[] { "light", "dark" };
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<string> OnThemeChanged { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool ShowIcon { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public Dictionary<string, string>? ThemeIcons { get; set; }

    private string _currentTheme = "light";
    private bool _isTransitioning = false;

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        await base.OnAfterRenderAsync(firstRender);

        if (firstRender)
        {
            _currentTheme = await ThemeInterop.GetThemeAsync();
            StateHasChanged();
        }
    }

    public override BUIThemeSelectorVariant DefaultVariant
        => BUIThemeSelectorVariant.Default;

    protected override Dictionary<BUIThemeSelectorVariant, Func<BUIThemeSelector, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates
        => new()
        {
            [BUIThemeSelectorVariant.Default] = b => b.RenderDefault(),
            [BUIThemeSelectorVariant.SunMoon] = b => b.RenderSunMoon()
        };

    private RenderFragment RenderDefault() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
       
            <button @onclick="SwitchTheme"
                    disabled="@_isTransitioning">
                <span class="bui-theme-switch__content @(_isTransitioning ? "ui-theme-switch__content--transitioning" : "")">
                    @if (ShowIcon)
                    {
                        <span class="bui-theme-switch__icon">@GetThemeIcon(_currentTheme)</span>
                    }
                    <span class="bui-theme-switch__label">@GetThemeLabel(_currentTheme)</span>
                </span>
            </button>
        </bui-component>
    };

    private RenderFragment RenderSunMoon() => __builder =>
    {
        <BUISwitch TValue="string"
                   @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                   OptionInactive="@("light")"
                   OptionActive="@("dark")"
                   IconInactive="@BUIIcons.MaterialIconsTwoTone.i_light_mode"
                   IconActive="@BUIIcons.MaterialIconsTwoTone.i_dark_mode"
                   Value="_currentTheme"
                   ValueChanged="OnSunMoonSwitchChanged" />
    };

    private async Task SwitchTheme()
    {
        _isTransitioning = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        // Small delay for animation start
        await Task.Delay(50);

        string newTheme = await ThemeInterop.ToggleThemeAsync(AvailableThemes);
        _currentTheme = newTheme;

        if (OnThemeChanged.HasDelegate)
        {
            await OnThemeChanged.InvokeAsync(newTheme);
        }

        // Keep transition state for animation duration
        await Task.Delay(300);
        _isTransitioning = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async Task OnSunMoonSwitchChanged(string requestedTheme)
    {
        // Evita doble toggle si por algún motivo llega el mismo valor
        if (requestedTheme == _currentTheme)
            return;

        string[] themes = { "light", "dark" };

        string newTheme = await ThemeInterop.ToggleThemeAsync(themes);
        _currentTheme = newTheme;

        if (OnThemeChanged.HasDelegate)
        {
            await OnThemeChanged.InvokeAsync(newTheme);
        }
    }

    private string GetThemeIcon(string theme)
    {
        if (ThemeIcons?.TryGetValue(theme, out string? icon) == true)
        {
            return icon;
        }

        return theme switch
        {
            "light" => "☀️",
            "dark" => "🌙",
            _ => "🎨"
        };
    }

    private string GetThemeLabel(string theme)
    {
        // Capitalize first letter
        return string.IsNullOrEmpty(theme) ? theme : char.ToUpper(theme[0]) + theme.Substring(1);
    }

    private string GetOppositeTheme()
    {
        return _currentTheme == "light" ? "dark" : "light";
    }
}

=== Layout\ThemeSelector\BUIThemeSelectorVariant.cs ===

=== Layout\ThemeSelector\ThemeJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout;

public interface IThemeJsInterop
{
    event Action<string>? OnThemeChanged;

    ValueTask<string> GetThemeAsync();

    ValueTask InitializeAsync(string? defaultTheme = null);

    ValueTask SetThemeAsync(string theme);

    ValueTask<string> ToggleThemeAsync(string[] themes);

    ValueTask<Dictionary<string, string>> GetPaletteAsync();
}

public sealed class ThemeJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
    : ModuleJsInteropBase(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.ThemeJs),
      IThemeJsInterop
{
    public event Action<string>? OnThemeChanged;

    public async ValueTask<string> GetThemeAsync()
    {
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        return await module.InvokeAsync<string>("getTheme");
    }

    public async ValueTask InitializeAsync(string? defaultTheme = null)
    {
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("initialize", defaultTheme);
    }

    public async ValueTask SetThemeAsync(string theme)
    {
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("setTheme", theme);
        OnThemeChanged?.Invoke(theme);
    }

    public async ValueTask<string> ToggleThemeAsync(params string[] themes)
    {
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        string newTheme = await module.InvokeAsync<string>("toggleTheme", new object[] { themes });
        OnThemeChanged?.Invoke(newTheme);
        return newTheme;
    }

    public async ValueTask<Dictionary<string, string>> GetPaletteAsync()
    {
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        return await module.InvokeAsync<Dictionary<string, string>>("getPalette");
    }
}



=== Layout\Toast\Services\ToastService.cs ===

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Rendering;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services;

public interface IToastService
{
    event Action? OnChange;

    IReadOnlyList<ToastState> ActiveToasts { get; }

    void Close(Guid toastId);

    void CloseAll();

    void Pause(Guid toastId);

    void Resume(Guid toastId);

    //void Show(RenderFragment content, ToastOptions? options = null);

    void Show(Action<RenderTreeBuilder> builder, ToastOptions? options = null);

    void Show<TComponent>(ToastOptions? options = null) where TComponent : IComponent;

    void Show<TComponent>(IDictionary<string, object?>? parameters, ToastOptions? options = null) where TComponent : IComponent;
}

public sealed class ToastService : IToastService
{
    private readonly object _lock = new();
    private readonly List<ToastState> _toasts = [];

    public event Action? OnChange;

    public IReadOnlyList<ToastState> ActiveToasts
    {
        get
        {
            lock (_lock)
            {
                return _toasts.ToList().AsReadOnly();
            }
        }
    }

    public int Count
    {
        get
        {
            lock (_lock)
            {
                return _toasts.Count;
            }
        }
    }

    public void Close(Guid toastId)
    {
        ToastState? toast;
        lock (_lock)
        {
            toast = _toasts.FirstOrDefault(t => t.Id == toastId);
            if (toast == null) return;

            toast.IsClosing = true;
            toast.DismissTokenSource?.Cancel();
        }

        NotifyChange();
    }

    public void CloseAll()
    {
        lock (_lock)
        {
            foreach (ToastState toast in _toasts)
            {
                toast.IsClosing = true;
                toast.DismissTokenSource?.Cancel();
            }
        }

        NotifyChange();
    }

    public void Pause(Guid toastId)
    {
        lock (_lock)
        {
            ToastState? toast = _toasts.FirstOrDefault(t => t.Id == toastId);
            if (toast == null || toast.IsPaused || !toast.Options.AutoDismiss) return;

            toast.DismissTokenSource?.Cancel();
            toast.ElapsedBeforePause += DateTime.UtcNow - toast.StartedAt;
            toast.IsPaused = true;
        }

        NotifyChange();
    }

    public void Resume(Guid toastId)
    {
        lock (_lock)
        {
            ToastState? toast = _toasts.FirstOrDefault(t => t.Id == toastId);
            if (toast == null || !toast.IsPaused || !toast.Options.AutoDismiss) return;

            toast.IsPaused = false;
            toast.StartedAt = DateTime.UtcNow;

            ScheduleDismiss(toast);
        }

        NotifyChange();
    }

    public void ShowFragment(RenderFragment content, ToastOptions? options = null)
    {
        ToastState state = new()
        {
            Content = content,
            Options = options ?? ToastOptions.Default
        };

        AddToast(state);
    }

    public void Show(Action<RenderTreeBuilder> builder, ToastOptions? options = null)
    {
        RenderFragment fragment = new(builder);
        ShowFragment(fragment, options);
    }

    public void Show<TComponent>(ToastOptions? options = null) where TComponent : IComponent
    {
        Show<TComponent>(null, options);
    }

    public void Show<TComponent>(IDictionary<string, object?>? parameters, ToastOptions? options = null) where TComponent : IComponent
    {
        RenderFragment fragment = builder =>
        {
            int seq = 0;
            builder.OpenComponent<TComponent>(seq++);

            if (parameters != null)
            {
                foreach (KeyValuePair<string, object?> param in parameters)
                {
                    builder.AddAttribute(seq++, param.Key, param.Value);
                }
            }

            builder.CloseComponent();
        };

        ShowFragment(fragment, options);
    }

    internal void Remove(Guid toastId)
    {
        ToastState? toast;
        lock (_lock)
        {
            toast = _toasts.FirstOrDefault(t => t.Id == toastId);
            if (toast == null) return;

            toast.DismissTokenSource?.Dispose();
            _toasts.Remove(toast);
        }

        toast.Options.OnClose?.Invoke();
        NotifyChange();
    }

    private void AddToast(ToastState toast)
    {
        lock (_lock)
        {
            _toasts.Add(toast);

            if (toast.Options.AutoDismiss)
            {
                ScheduleDismiss(toast);
            }
        }

        NotifyChange();
    }

    private async Task DismissAfterDelayAsync(Guid toastId, TimeSpan delay, CancellationToken cancellationToken)
    {
        try
        {
            await Task.Delay(delay, cancellationToken);
            Close(toastId);
        }
        catch (TaskCanceledException)
        {
        }
    }

    private void NotifyChange() => OnChange?.Invoke();

    private void ScheduleDismiss(ToastState toast)
    {
        toast.DismissTokenSource?.Cancel();
        toast.DismissTokenSource = new CancellationTokenSource();

        TimeSpan delay = toast.RemainingTime > TimeSpan.Zero
            ? toast.RemainingTime
            : toast.Options.Duration;

        _ = DismissAfterDelayAsync(toast.Id, delay, toast.DismissTokenSource.Token);
    }
}



=== Layout\Toast\Services\ToastState.cs ===

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services;

public sealed class ToastState
{
    public ToastState()
    {
        StartedAt = DateTime.UtcNow;
    }

    public RenderFragment Content { get; init; }
    public DateTime CreatedAt { get; } = DateTime.UtcNow;
    public CancellationTokenSource? DismissTokenSource { get; set; }
    public TimeSpan ElapsedBeforePause { get; set; } = TimeSpan.Zero;
    public Guid Id { get; } = Guid.NewGuid();
    public bool IsClosing { get; set; }
    public bool IsPaused { get; set; }
    public ToastOptions Options { get; init; }

    public double ProgressPercentage
    {
        get
        {
            if (!Options.AutoDismiss || Options.Duration == TimeSpan.Zero) return 0;

            TimeSpan elapsed = IsPaused
                ? ElapsedBeforePause
                : ElapsedBeforePause + (DateTime.UtcNow - StartedAt);

            double percentage = (elapsed.TotalMilliseconds / Options.Duration.TotalMilliseconds) * 100;
            return Math.Clamp(percentage, 0, 100);
        }
    }

    public TimeSpan RemainingTime
    {
        get
        {
            if (!Options.AutoDismiss) return TimeSpan.Zero;

            TimeSpan elapsed = IsPaused
                ? ElapsedBeforePause
                : ElapsedBeforePause + (DateTime.UtcNow - StartedAt);

            TimeSpan remaining = Options.Duration - elapsed;
            return remaining > TimeSpan.Zero ? remaining : TimeSpan.Zero;
        }
    }

    public DateTime StartedAt { get; set; }
}



=== Layout\Toast\BUIToast.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIVariantComponentBase<BUIToast, BUIToastVariant>
@implements IDisposable

@{
    base.BuildRenderTree(__builder);
}

@code {
    private System.Timers.Timer? _progressTimer;

    [Parameter, EditorRequired]
    public ToastState State { get; set; } = default!;

    [Parameter]
    public EventCallback<Guid> OnCloseAnimationComplete { get; set; }

    [CascadingParameter]
    private ToastService? ToastService { get; set; }

    public override BUIToastVariant DefaultVariant => BUIToastVariant.Default;

    protected override Dictionary<BUIToastVariant, Func<BUIToast, RenderFragment>> BuiltInTemplates { get; } = new()
    {
        [BUIToastVariant.Default] = t => t.RenderDefault()
    };

    public override void BuildComponentDataAttributes(Dictionary<string, object> dataAttributes)
    {
        dataAttributes["data-bui-position"] = GetPositionValue();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-animation"] = GetAnimationValue();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-closing"] = State.IsClosing.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        dataAttributes["data-bui-paused"] = State.IsPaused.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
    }

    public override void BuildComponentCssVariables(Dictionary<string, string> cssVariables)
    {
        cssVariables["--bui-toast-animation-duration"] = $"{State.Options.Animation.Duration.TotalMilliseconds}ms";
        cssVariables["--bui-toast-animation-easing"] = State.Options.Animation.Easing;
    }

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        base.OnInitialized();

        if (State.Options.AutoDismiss)
        {
            _progressTimer = new System.Timers.Timer(50);
            _progressTimer.Elapsed += (_, _) => InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
            _progressTimer.Start();
        }
    }

    protected override async Task OnParametersSetAsync()
    {
        await base.OnParametersSetAsync();

        if (State.IsClosing)
        {
            _progressTimer?.Stop();
            await Task.Delay((int)State.Options.Animation.Duration.TotalMilliseconds);
            await OnCloseAnimationComplete.InvokeAsync(State.Id);
        }
    }

    private RenderFragment RenderDefault() => __builder =>
    {
        <bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes"
                       @onmouseenter="HandleMouseEnter"
                       @onmouseleave="HandleMouseLeave"
                       @onclick="HandleClick">

            <div class="bui-toast__content">
                @State.Content
            </div>

            @if (State.Options.Closable)
            {
                <_BUIBtn Icon="@BUIIcons.UI.Close"
                         AriaLabel="Close"
                         OnClick="HandleClose"
                         OnClickStopPropagation="true" />
            }

            @if (State.Options.AutoDismiss)
            {
                <div class="bui-toast__progress">
                    <div class="bui-toast__progress-bar" style="@GetProgressStyle()"></div>
                </div>
            }
        </bui-component>
    };

    private string GetPositionValue() => State.Options.Position switch
    {
        ToastPosition.TopLeft => "top-left",
        ToastPosition.TopCenter => "top-center",
        ToastPosition.TopRight => "top-right",
        ToastPosition.BottomLeft => "bottom-left",
        ToastPosition.BottomCenter => "bottom-center",
        ToastPosition.BottomRight => "bottom-right",
        _ => "top-right"
    };

    private string GetAnimationValue() => State.Options.Animation.Type switch
    {
        ToastAnimationType.Fade => "fade",
        ToastAnimationType.Slide => "slide",
        ToastAnimationType.SlideAndFade => "slide-fade",
        _ => "none"
    };

    private string GetProgressStyle()
    {
        if (!State.Options.AutoDismiss) return "width: 0%";

        double progress = State.ProgressPercentage;
        return $"width: {100 - progress:F1}%";
    }

    private void HandleMouseEnter()
    {
        if (State.Options.AutoDismiss && !State.IsClosing)
        {
            ToastService?.Pause(State.Id);
            _progressTimer?.Stop();
        }
    }

    private void HandleMouseLeave()
    {
        if (State.Options.AutoDismiss && !State.IsClosing)
        {
            ToastService?.Resume(State.Id);
            _progressTimer?.Start();
        }
    }

    private void HandleClick()
    {
        State.Options.OnClick?.Invoke();
    }

    private void HandleClose()
    {
        ToastService?.Close(State.Id);
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        _progressTimer?.Stop();
        _progressTimer?.Dispose();
    }
}

=== Layout\Toast\BUIToastHost.razor ===

@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout.Services
@using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.Components

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IDisposable

@inject IToastService ToastService

<CascadingValue Value="_toastService" IsFixed="true">
    @foreach (ToastPosition position in Enum.GetValues<ToastPosition>())
    {
        IEnumerable<ToastState> toastsInPosition = GetToastsForPosition(position);
        @if (toastsInPosition.Any())
        {
            <bui-component data-bui-component="toast-host"
                           data-bui-position="@GetPositionValue(position)">
                @foreach (ToastState toast in toastsInPosition)
                {
                    <BUIToast @key="toast.Id"
                              State="toast"
                              OnCloseAnimationComplete="HandleAnimationComplete" />
                }
            </bui-component>
        }
    }
</CascadingValue>

@code {
    private ToastService? _toastService;
    private List<ToastState> _allToasts = [];

    [Parameter]
    public int MaxVisiblePerPosition { get; set; } = 5;

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        base.OnInitialized();
        _toastService = ToastService as ToastService;
        ToastService.OnChange += HandleToastChange;
    }

    private void HandleToastChange()
    {
        _allToasts = ToastService.ActiveToasts.ToList();
        InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
    }

    private IEnumerable<ToastState> GetToastsForPosition(ToastPosition position)
    {
        IEnumerable<ToastState> toasts = _allToasts.Where(t => t.Options.Position == position);

        bool isBottomPosition = position is ToastPosition.BottomLeft
            or ToastPosition.BottomCenter
            or ToastPosition.BottomRight;

        IEnumerable<ToastState> ordered = isBottomPosition
            ? toasts.OrderByDescending(t => t.CreatedAt)
            : toasts.OrderBy(t => t.CreatedAt);

        List<ToastState> visible = ordered
            .Where(t => !t.IsClosing)
            .Take(MaxVisiblePerPosition)
            .ToList();

        IEnumerable<ToastState> closing = ordered.Where(t => t.IsClosing);

        return visible.Concat(closing);
    }

    private async Task HandleAnimationComplete(Guid toastId)
    {
        _toastService?.Remove(toastId);
    }

    private string GetPositionValue(ToastPosition position) => position switch
    {
        ToastPosition.TopLeft => "top-left",
        ToastPosition.TopCenter => "top-center",
        ToastPosition.TopRight => "top-right",
        ToastPosition.BottomLeft => "bottom-left",
        ToastPosition.BottomCenter => "bottom-center",
        ToastPosition.BottomRight => "bottom-right",
        _ => "top-right"
    };

    public void Dispose()
    {
        ToastService.OnChange -= HandleToastChange;
    }
}

public sealed class ToastAnimation
{
    public static ToastAnimation Default => new();
    public static ToastAnimation FadeOnly => new() { Type = ToastAnimationType.Fade };
    public static ToastAnimation None => new() { Type = ToastAnimationType.None, Duration = TimeSpan.Zero };
    public static ToastAnimation SlideAndFade => new() { Type = ToastAnimationType.SlideAndFade };
    public static ToastAnimation SlideOnly => new() { Type = ToastAnimationType.Slide };
    public TimeSpan Duration { get; init; } = TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(300);
    public string Easing { get; init; } = "ease-out";
    public ToastAnimationType Type { get; init; } = ToastAnimationType.SlideAndFade;

    public ToastAnimation WithDuration(TimeSpan duration) => new()
    {
        Type = Type,
        Duration = duration,
        Easing = Easing
    };

    public ToastAnimation WithEasing(string easing) => new()
    {
        Type = Type,
        Duration = Duration,
        Easing = easing
    };
}

    None,
    Fade,
    Slide,
    SlideAndFade

=== Layout\BUIInitializer.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components.Layout
@using Microsoft.JSInterop

@inject IThemeJsInterop ThemeInterop

<HeadContent>
    <script>
        // Prevent theme flash on page load
        (function(){
            var t=localStorage.getItem('blazorui-theme')||'light';
            document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme',t);
        })();
    </script>
</HeadContent>

@if (_palette is not null)
{
    <CascadingValue Value="_palette" IsFixed="false">
        @ChildContent
    </CascadingValue>
}

@code{

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public string DefaultTheme { get; set; } = "dark";

    private BUIPalette? _palette;

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        ThemeInterop.OnThemeChanged += HandleThemeChanged;
    }

    protected override async Task OnAfterRenderAsync(bool firstRender)
    {
        if (!firstRender) return;

        await ThemeInterop.InitializeAsync(DefaultTheme);
        await LoadPaletteAsync();
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async void HandleThemeChanged(string theme)
    {
        await LoadPaletteAsync();
        await InvokeAsync(StateHasChanged);
    }

    private async Task LoadPaletteAsync()
    {
        Dictionary<string, string> colors = await ThemeInterop.GetPaletteAsync();
        _palette = new BUIPalette(colors);
    }

    public void Dispose()
    {
        ThemeInterop.OnThemeChanged -= HandleThemeChanged;
    }
}

public sealed class BUIPalette

    public CssColor Background { get; }
    public CssColor BackgroundContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Black { get; }
    public CssColor Error { get; }
    public CssColor ErrorContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Info { get; }
    public CssColor InfoContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Primary { get; }
    public CssColor PrimaryContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Secondary { get; }
    public CssColor SecondaryContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Shadow { get; }
    public CssColor Success { get; }
    public CssColor SuccessContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Surface { get; }
    public CssColor SurfaceContrast { get; }
    public CssColor Warning { get; }
    public CssColor WarningContrast { get; }
    public CssColor White { get; }

    public BUIPalette(IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> palette)
    {
        CssColor C(string key) => new(palette[key]);

        Background = C("--palette-background");
        BackgroundContrast = C("--palette-backgroundcontrast");
        Black = C("--palette-black");
        Error = C("--palette-error");
        ErrorContrast = C("--palette-errorcontrast");
        Info = C("--palette-info");
        InfoContrast = C("--palette-infocontrast");

        PrimaryContrast = C("--palette-primarycontrast");
        Secondary = C("--palette-secondary");
        SecondaryContrast = C("--palette-secondarycontrast");
        Shadow = C("--palette-shadow");
        Success = C("--palette-success");
        SuccessContrast = C("--palette-successcontrast");
        Surface = C("--palette-surface");
        SurfaceContrast = C("--palette-surfacecontrast");
        Warning = C("--palette-warning");
        WarningContrast = C("--palette-warningcontrast");
        White = C("--palette-white");
    }

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public interface IClipboardJsInterop
{
    ValueTask CopyTextAsync(string text);
}

public sealed class ClipboardJsInterop
    : ModuleJsInteropBase, IClipboardJsInterop
{
    public ClipboardJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.Clipboard)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask CopyTextAsync(string text)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;

        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("copyText", text);
    }
}



=== Utils\Draggable\JsInterop\DraggableCallbacksRelay.cs ===

using Microsoft.JSInterop;
using System.Diagnostics.CodeAnalysis;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public sealed class DraggableCallbacksRelay : IDisposable
{
    private readonly IDraggableJsCallback _callback;

    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnMouseMove))]
    [DynamicDependency(nameof(OnMouseUp))]
    public DraggableCallbacksRelay(IDraggableJsCallback callback)
    {
        _callback = callback;
        DotNetReference = DotNetObjectReference.Create(this);
    }

    public DotNetObjectReference<DraggableCallbacksRelay> DotNetReference { get; }

    public void Dispose() => DotNetReference.Dispose();

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnMouseMove(double clientX, double clientY) =>
        _callback.OnMouseMove(clientX, clientY);

    [JSInvokable]
    public Task OnMouseUp(double clientX, double clientY) =>
        _callback.OnMouseUp(clientX, clientY);
}



=== Utils\Draggable\JsInterop\DraggableJsInterop.cs ===

using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Core.Abstractions.JSInterop;
using CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Types;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.JSInterop;

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public interface IDraggableJsInterop
{
    ValueTask StartDragAsync(
        ElementReference element,
        DotNetObjectReference<DraggableCallbacksRelay> dotnetReference,
        string componentId);

    ValueTask StopDragAsync(string componentId);
}

public sealed class DraggableJsInterop : ModuleJsInteropBase, IDraggableJsInterop
{
    public DraggableJsInterop(IJSRuntime jsRuntime)
        : base(jsRuntime, JSModulesReference.Draggable)
    {
    }

    public async ValueTask StartDragAsync(
        ElementReference element,
        DotNetObjectReference<DraggableCallbacksRelay> dotnetReference,
        string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("startDrag", element, dotnetReference, componentId);
    }

    public async ValueTask StopDragAsync(string componentId)
    {
        await IsModuleTaskLoaded.Task;
        IJSObjectReference module = await ModuleTask.Value;
        await module.InvokeVoidAsync("stopDrag", componentId);
    }
}



=== Utils\Draggable\JsInterop\IDraggableJsCallback.cs ===

namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components;

public interface IDraggableJsCallback
{
    Task OnMouseMove(double clientX, double clientY);

    Task OnMouseUp(double clientX, double clientY);
}



=== Utils\Draggable\BUIDraggable.razor ===

@namespace CdCSharp.BlazorUI.Components

@inherits BUIComponentBase
@implements IDraggableJsCallback
@implements IAsyncDisposable

<bui-component @attributes="ComputedAttributes">
    <div @ref="_elementRef"
         class="bui-draggable"
         @onmousedown="HandleMouseDown"
         @onmousedown:preventDefault="PreventDefault">
        @ChildContent
    </div>
</bui-component>

@code {
    private readonly string _componentId = $"bui-draggable-{Guid.NewGuid():N}";
    private ElementReference _elementRef;
    private DraggableCallbacksRelay? _callbacksRelay;
    private bool _isDragging;

    [Inject] private IDraggableJsInterop JsInterop { get; set; } = default!;

    [Parameter] public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<DragEventArgs> OnDragStart { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<DragEventArgs> OnDrag { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public EventCallback<DragEventArgs> OnDragEnd { get; set; }
    [Parameter] public bool PreventDefault { get; set; } = true;
    [Parameter] public bool Disabled { get; set; }

    private async Task HandleMouseDown(MouseEventArgs e)
    {
        if (Disabled) return;

        _isDragging = true;
        _callbacksRelay ??= new DraggableCallbacksRelay(this);

        await JsInterop.StartDragAsync(_elementRef, _callbacksRelay.DotNetReference, _componentId);
        await OnDragStart.InvokeAsync(new DragEventArgs { ClientX = e.ClientX, ClientY = e.ClientY });
    }

    async Task IDraggableJsCallback.OnMouseMove(double clientX, double clientY)
    {
        if (!_isDragging) return;
        await OnDrag.InvokeAsync(new DragEventArgs { ClientX = clientX, ClientY = clientY });
    }

    async Task IDraggableJsCallback.OnMouseUp(double clientX, double clientY)
    {
        if (!_isDragging) return;

        _isDragging = false;
        await JsInterop.StopDragAsync(_componentId);
        await OnDragEnd.InvokeAsync(new DragEventArgs { ClientX = clientX, ClientY = clientY });
    }

    public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()
    {
        if (_isDragging)
        {
            await JsInterop.StopDragAsync(_componentId);
        }
        _callbacksRelay?.Dispose();
    }
}

    }
